### [1] [Scaling Breakdown as a Signature of Spinon-Gauge Interaction in the Quantum Spin Liquid YbZn$_2$GaO$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13087)
*Shannon Gould,John Singleton,Rabindranath Bag,Sara Haravifard,Sheng Ran*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过对量子自旋液体（QSL）候选材料YbZn₂GaO₅的高场磁化测量进行综合分析，揭示了磁化标度行为的温度依赖性特征。研究发现5-70K温度范围内存在类似零场量子临界点的标度不变性，而低于3K时标度不变性发生破坏，这种破坏与进入QSL区域时本征低能激发的出现相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁化标度行为在众多量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）候选材料中被广泛报道，通常被解释为无标度自旋液体物理的证据。然而，这种标度行为与QSL相本身的关系尚不明确，需要更深入的分析来澄清磁化标度行为的物理起源。

Method: 研究采用对QSL材料YbZn₂GaO₅进行高场磁化测量的方法，在5-70K和低于3K的不同温度区间进行系统性分析。通过综合标度分析（comprehensive scaling analysis）考察磁化M(H)的标度行为，并与μSR测量中观察到的自旋关联增强现象进行对比。

Result: 在5-70K温度范围内，M(H)显示出类似零场量子临界点（zero-field quantum critical point）的标度不变性。低于3K时，标度不变性发生破坏，且无法通过简单改变临界指数来恢复。标度偏离的形式与通过涌现规范相互作用（emergent gauge interactions）耦合的集体自旋子激发（collective spinon excitations）一致。

Conclusion: 标度破坏反映了进入QSL区域时本征低能激发的出现。磁化标度行为与量子临界涨落（quantum critical fluctuations）相关，而非自旋液体相本身。磁化标度分析可作为QSL系统中涌现能标（emergent energy scales）的灵敏热力学探针。

Abstract: Scaling behavior in magnetization has been reported in a wide range of quantum spin liquid (QSL) candidates and is often interpreted as evidence for scale-free spin liquid physics. Here we present a comprehensive scaling analysis of high-field magnetization measurements on the QSL material YbZn$_2$GaO$_5$. Between 5 K and 70 K, $M(H)$ displays scale invariance resembling that of a zero-field quantum critical point. Below 3 K, we observe a breakdown of this scale invariance that cannot be recovered by simply changing the critical exponents. This temperature coincides with the onset of enhanced spin correlations observed in $μ$SR measurements. Moreover, the form of the deviation from scaling is consistent with collective spinon excitations coupled via emergent gauge interactions. These results indicate that the breakdown of scaling reflects the emergence of intrinsic low-energy excitations upon entering the QSL regime. Our work clarifies that magnetic scaling is associated with quantum critical fluctuations rather than with the spin liquid phase itself, and establishes magnetization scaling as a sensitive thermodynamic probe of emergent energy scales in QSL systems.

</details>


### [2] [Entanglement in a molecular Lieb-lattice quantum computing circuit: A tensor network study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13093)
*Wei Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究设计了一种基于有限李晶格（finite Lieb lattice）的量子计算电路，使用自旋-1/2量子比特（qubits）和三重态耦合器（triplet couplers），分析了量子纠缠梯度，为分子自旋量子计算提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为分子自旋量子计算（molecular spin-based quantum computing）设计可扩展的电路架构，探索三重态介导的分子自组装量子计算电路（triplet-mediated molecular self-assembly quantum computing circuit）的实现途径。

Method: 研究设计了由自旋-1/2量子比特和三重态耦合器构成的有限李晶格量子计算电路，通过张量网络方法（tensor-network methods）计算了冯·诺依曼纠缠熵（von Neumann entanglement entropy）、约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrices）和自旋-自旋关联（spin-spin correlations）。

Result: 研究揭示了丰富的纠缠模式（entanglement patterns）、量子相变（quantum phase transitions）和可调的自旋相干性（tunable spin coherence），这些发现对基于分子的纠缠门（entangling gate）设计具有重要意义。

Conclusion: 该工作为实验实现可扩展的分子基量子计算电路（scalable molecule-based quantum computing circuits）提供了理论基石，展示了在含多个自由基的分子体系中通过光驱动三重态控制量子比特通信的可行性。

Abstract: Here a finite-Lieb-lattice quantum computing circuit consisting of spin-1/2 quantum bits (qubits) and triplet couplers is designed. Important gradient - quantum entanglement - is analysed. This type of design could be realised in a vast range of molecules containing multiple radicals, in which the communications among qubits are controlled by the optically driven triplets. The von Neumann entanglement entropy, reduced density matrices, and spin-spin correlations were computed using tensor-network methods by varying the magnetic anisotropy and external magnetic field. This work uncovers the rich entanglement patterns, quantum phase transitions, and tunable spin coherence in this mixed spin system, designed for molecular spin-based quantum computing. These findings have important implications for triplet-mediated molecular self-assembly quantum computing circuit, especially for the entangling gate based on molecules. This work would provide a theoretical cornerstone for the experimental realisation of scalable molecule-based quantum computing circuits.

</details>


### [3] [Superconductivity near two-dimensional Van Hove singularities: a determinant quantum Monte Carlo study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13161)
*Gustav Romare,Daniel Shaffer,Alex Levchenko,Edwin Huang,Ilya Esterlis*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，计算了二维吸引型哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）在范霍夫奇点（Van Hove singularity）附近的超导转变温度Tc，发现中等相互作用强度下，最大Tc出现在远离范霍夫点的密度处。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究二维吸引型哈伯德模型中范霍夫奇点对超导转变温度Tc的影响，特别是在普通对数奇点和高阶幂律奇点附近，以及不同相互作用强度下的行为差异。

Method: 采用行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）模拟方法，计算二维吸引型哈伯德模型在范霍夫奇点附近的超导转变温度Tc，对比普通对数奇点和高阶幂律奇点的情况。

Result: 对于弱相互作用（|U| ≲ W/3），Tc在范霍夫点附近有所增强，但弱于弱耦合BCS理论预期；将范霍夫奇点从对数增强为幂律仅带来轻微额外增强。对于强相互作用（|U| ≳ W/3），最大Tc偏离范霍夫点，出现在与非相互作用态密度特征无关的密度处。

Conclusion: 最大超导转变温度在中等相互作用强度U下实现，且出现在远离范霍夫点的密度处，这与强耦合解释一致，表明范霍夫奇点对Tc的增强效应在强相互作用区减弱。

Abstract: The superconducting transition temperature $T_c$ of the two-dimensional attractive Hubbard model is computed in the vicinity of both ordinary (logarithmic) and higher-order (power-law) Van Hove singularities using determinant quantum Monte Carlo simulations. For interaction strengths $|U| \lesssim W/3$, where $W$ is the electronic bandwidth, $T_c$ is enhanced in the neighborhood of the Van Hove point, albeit more weakly than expected from weak-coupling BCS theory. Enhancing the Van Hove singularity from logarithmic to power-law yields only a minor additional enhancement of $T_c$. For $|U| \gtrsim W/3$, the maximum $T_c$ shifts away from the Van Hove point and instead occurs at a density unrelated to any features in the non-interacting density of states, consistent with a strong-coupling interpretation. We find that the maximal $T_c$ in the model is achieved at intermediate $U$ and at a density away from the Van Hove point.

</details>


### [4] [Extreme Terahertz Nonlinear Phononics by Coherence-Imprinted Control of Hybrid Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13429)
*Liang Luo,Avinash Khatri,Martin Mootz,Tao Jiang,Liu Yang,Zijing Chen,Chuankun Huang,Zhi Xiang Chong,Joongmok Park,Ilias E. Perakis,Zhiwei Wang,Yugui Yao,Dao Xiang,Yong-Xin Yao,Jigang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在Ta₂NiSe₅中发现的一种极端太赫兹非线性声子机制，其中高度敏感的非平衡电子关联浴显著放大了相干驱动下的晶格非线性。利用太赫兹二维光谱作为相干层析工具，研究人员解析了约30个不同的多阶量子路径，建立了太赫兹非线性声子学的新基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子材料的相干控制面临两大挑战：传统晶格中声子非线性在太赫兹频率下本征较弱，而电子弗洛凯态常受限于光关闭后的快速退相干以及缺乏超越准稳态能带结构的相干分辨多关联探针。这些限制阻碍了在太赫兹频率下实现有效的材料控制。

Method: 研究采用太赫兹二维光谱作为相干层析工具，在Ta₂NiSe₅材料中探测非线性声子响应。该方法能够解析多阶量子路径，包括高次谐波声子产生、多量子相干以及多波非谐交叉模式混合等复杂过程。

Result: 实验观测到约30个不同的多阶量子路径，包括高次谐波声子产生、多量子相干和多波非谐交叉模式混合。这些高阶信号在约100K以上消失，定义了电子关联尺度，该尺度控制着超越线性和平衡响应的高阶量子关联和非线性路径的可持续性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种关联增强、声子锚定的周期性哈密顿量工程路径，并通过多关联相干层析验证了这种周期性驱动态。极端非线性声子机制为太赫兹频率下的量子材料控制提供了新范式，超越了传统晶格响应的限制。

Abstract: Coherent control of quantum materials has progressed along two major fronts: nonlinear phononics, which reshapes lattices to induce emergent states, and Floquet engineering, which tailors electronic band reconstruction via time-periodic driving. Both mechanisms face fundamental limitations at terahertz (THz) frequencies: phononic nonlinearities are intrinsically weak in standard lattices, while electronic Floquet states are often constrained by rapid decoherence upon light-off and by a scarcity of coherence-resolved, multi-correlation probes beyond (quasi-)stationary band structures. Here we report an extreme THz nonlinear-phononics mechanism in $\text{Ta}_\text{2}\text{NiSe}_\text{5}$, where a highly susceptible non-equilibrium electronic correlation bath dramatically amplifies lattice nonlinearities under coherent driving. Utilizing THz two-dimensional spectroscopy as a coherence-tomography tool, we resolve an exceptionally rich landscape of approximately 30 distinct multi-order quantum pathways, including high-harmonic phonon generation, multi-quantum coherences, and multi-wave anharmonic cross-mode mixing. The density and complexity of this extreme manifold establishes a new benchmark for THz nonlinear phononics, as the multi-order quantum pathways surpass the limits of conventional lattice responses. These high-order signals collapse above ~100~K, defining an electronic correlation scale of a coherence-imprinted hybrid electronic-phonon order that governs the sustainability of high-order quantum correlations and nonlinear pathways beyond linear and equilibrium responses. Our results establish a route for correlation-boosted, phonon-anchored periodic Hamiltonian engineering and for certifying such periodically-driven states via multi-correlation coherence tomography.

</details>


### [5] [Anomalous Low-temperature Magnetotransport in Kagome Metal CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$ under Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13553)
*Zikai Zhou,Wenyan Wang,Deng Hu,Zheyu Wang,Ying Kit Tsui,Tsz Fung Poon,Zhiwei Wang,Swee K. Goh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: CsCr₃Sb₅作为独特的kagome超导体，在约30K（T₃）处存在电阻异常，本研究通过静水压下的磁输运实验揭示了该异常丰富的电子输运特征，表明可能存在额外的奇异电子序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CsCr₃Sb₅作为展示强电子关联特征的独特kagome超导体，其丰富的温度-压力相图包含压力诱导超导性和两个类密度波相。在约30K（T₃）处观察到的电阻异常（表现为驼峰）性质尚未被充分探索，需要进一步研究。

Method: 本研究在静水压（hydrostatic pressure）条件下进行了系统的磁输运（magnetotransport）实验，以探究CsCr₃Sb₅中T₃温度附近异常的性质。

Result: 实验结果显示在T₃以下存在丰富的磁输运特征，包括霍尔系数（Hall coefficient）的非平凡温度依赖性、多带特性以及压力增强的类反常霍尔效应（anomalous-Hall-like effect）。这些特征与姐妹化合物CsV₃Sb₅中的电荷密度波态相似。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明CsCr₃Sb₅中可能存在额外的奇异电子序（exotic electronic order），这些发现呼吁进一步的详细研究来揭示其本质。

Abstract: As a unique kagome superconductor displaying clear signatures of strong electronic correlations, CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$ has drawn much attention. Its rich temperature-pressure phase diagram features intertwined orders including pressure-induced superconductivity and two density-wave-like phases, making it an outstanding platform to explore the complex coexistence and competition of multiple quantum orders. At around 30 K, which we designate as $T_3$, a possible anomaly manifesting as a hump in the resistivity has been observed, yet its nature remains largely unexplored due to limited supporting evidence from other probes. Here, we conducted systematic magnetotransport experiments under hydrostatic pressure to investigate the nature of this anomaly. Our results reveal an abundance of intriguing magnetotransport signatures below $T_3$, including a non-trivial temperature dependence of the Hall coefficient, multi-band characteristics, and pressure-enhanced anomalous-Hall-like effect. These signatures bear resemblance to those observed in the charge-density-wave state in the sister compound CsV$_3$Sb$_5$. These findings suggest the possibility of an additional, exotic electronic order in CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$, calling for further detailed investigations.

</details>


### [6] [Revisiting 9Be Nuclear Magnetic Resonance in UBe13: Itinerant-Localized Duality and Possible Fermi Surface Reconstruction at High Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13576)
*Rintaro Matsuki,Shoko Minami,Hisashi Kotegawa,Hisatomo Harima,Yoshinori Haga,Etsuji Yamamoto,Yoshichika Onuki,Hideki Tou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过9Be核磁共振（NMR）测量重费米子超导体UBe13单晶，修正了先前参数在高磁场下无法准确描述谱线角依赖性的问题，揭示了经典偶极场的重要影响，并发现6T附近奈特位移（Knight shift）异常，表明高磁场区域多重费米面的部分重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前2007年研究确定的NMR和电场梯度（EFG）参数虽能再现低磁场下的NMR谱，但无法准确描述高磁场下NMR谱的角依赖性。为解决这一矛盾，需要对UBe13进行更全面的NMR研究。

Method: 在0.5T至8T磁场范围内测量9Be-NMR谱的磁场依赖性，并在0.5T和6T下测量磁场角依赖性。通过考虑UBe13的非对称空间群进行详细模拟，确定能够再现高磁场下复杂NMR线型的新参数集。

Result: 新参数集成功再现了高磁场下观察到的复杂NMR线型。分析揭示了经典偶极场（classical dipolar fields）的显著影响，奈特位移（Knight shift）与经典偶极位移的比较为UBe13中巡游-局域二重性（itinerant-localized duality）提供了微观证据。此外，奈特位移在6T附近表现出异常，表明高磁场区域多重费米面（multiple Fermi surfaces）的部分重构。

Conclusion: 通过全面的9Be-NMR测量和考虑非对称空间群的模拟，研究解决了先前参数在高磁场下的局限性，揭示了经典偶极场的重要作用，并为UBe13的巡游-局域二重性提供了微观证据，同时发现高磁场下费米面重构的迹象。

Abstract: We report on new results of 9Be nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) measurements conducted on a single crystal of the heavy fermion superconductor UBe13. Our previous 2007 study [J. Phys. Soc. Jpn. 76 204705 (2007)] determined NMR and electric field gradient (EFG) parameters that successfully reproduced the NMR spectra at low magnetic fields. However, these parameters did not accurately describe the angular dependence of the NMR spectra at high magnetic fields. To address this discrepancy, we have now performed a more comprehensive investigation, measuring the magnetic field dependence of the 9Be-NMR spectra across a field range of 0.5 T to 8 T, as well as the magnetic field angle dependence at 0.5 T and 6 T. Through detailed simulations that take into account the non-symmorphic space group of UBe13, we have determined a new set of parameters capable of reproducing the complex NMR line profiles observed at high magnetic fields. Notably, our analysis reveals the significant influence of classical dipolar fields. A comparison between the Knight shift (KS) and the classical dipolar shift provides microscopic supporting evidence for the nature of an itinerant-localized duality in UBe13. Furthermore, the magnetic field dependence of the KS exhibits anomalies around 6 T, suggesting a reconstruction of a part of the multiple Fermi surfaces in the high magnetic field region.

</details>


### [7] [The ground ytterbium doublet in h-YbMnO3 and the related low-temperature peculiarities of the compound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13651)
*S. A. Klimin,N. D. Molchanova,N. N. Kuzmin,E. S. Sektarov,Lihua Yin,M. N. Popova*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过傅里叶变换光谱研究h-YbMnO3中Yb³⁺离子的光学f-f跃迁，确定了4b位点Yb³⁺基态Kramers双重态的分裂随温度变化函数D₀(T)，揭示了镱子系统受锰磁矩有序化影响，并解释了热容中的Schottky异常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究h-YbMnO3中Yb³⁺离子的温度依赖性光学f-f跃迁，以理解镱子系统与锰磁有序之间的相互作用机制，特别是基态Kramers双重态分裂的动力学行为。

Method: 采用傅里叶变换光谱（Fourier-transform spectroscopy）技术，对h-YbMnO3中Yb³⁺离子的光学f-f跃迁进行详细的温度依赖性研究，测定4b位点Yb³⁺离子基态Kramers双重态的分裂函数D₀(T)。

Result: D₀(T)函数在T_N = 87 K以下遵循锰磁矩的动力学行为，表明镱子系统受有序锰子系统产生的磁场磁化；计算得到的Yb(4b)磁矩温度行为与中子衍射数据一致；Yb(4b)对热容的贡献解释了C_P(T)依赖中的Schottky异常。

Conclusion: 提出h-YbMnO3相变的新机制，其中镱子系统的能量增益起关键作用；分裂基态双重态的上能级激发在晶体低温动力学中具有重要作用，为理解该体系的磁相互作用提供了新视角。

Abstract: We have performed detailed temperature-dependent study of optical f-f transitions of the Yb3+ ions in h-YbMnO3 by means of Fourier-transform spectroscopy. The splitting of the ground Kramers doublet as a function of temperature, D0(T), for the Yb3+ ion at 4b site was determined. The D0(T) function follows the dynamics of the manganese magnetic moment below TN = 87 K, indicating, that the ytterbium subsystem is magnetized by the magnetic field generated by an ordered manganese subsystem, which is consistent with the results of previous studies. Excitation of the upper component of the split ground doublet plays a significant role in low-temperature dynamics of the h-YbMnO3 crystal. Using the D0(T) function we calculated the temperature behavior of the of the Yb(4b) magnetic moment: it is in clear agreement with the neutron data [Phys. Rev. B 98, 134413, 2018]. The calculated contribution of Yb(4b) to heat capacity definitely explains the origin of the Schottky anomaly in the CP(T) dependence. A scenario for phase transitions in h-YbMnO3 is proposed in which the energy gain in the ytterbium system plays a key role.

</details>


### [8] [Probing the real-space density of spin-entangled electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13751)
*Federico Pisani,Leonie Spitz,Libor Vojáček,Flaviano José dos Santos,Alberto Carta,Bastien Dalla Piazza,Stanislav E. Nikitin,Karl W. Krämer,Björn Fåk,Taro Nakajima,Daichi Ueta,Hiraku Saito,Jian-Rui Soh,Nicola Marzari,Henrik M. Rønnow*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过测量铜(II)乙酸盐水合物中单重态-三重态激发的三维磁结构因子，首次从非弹性中子散射（INS）数据中提取了磁性形状因子和磁性电子密度分布，为确定磁性材料中的电子波函数空间包络建立了可靠框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在证明可以从磁性激发的非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering, INS）强度动量依赖性中提取磁性形状因子（magnetic form factor）和磁性电子密度分布。以反铁磁海森堡二聚体（antiferromagnetic Heisenberg dimer）为教科书范例，探索INS作为空间电子波函数包络探针的潜力。

Method: 研究采用实验与理论相结合的方法：首先测量铜(II)乙酸盐水合物中单重态-三重态激发的三维磁结构因子（three-dimensional magnetic structure factor）；其次使用磁性电子密度的最小参数化方法从实验数据推导自旋纠缠电子的实空间密度；最后通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算验证实验结果。

Result: 实验成功提取了金属与配体原子间的磁性电子密度转移信息。DFT计算定量再现了测量的结构因子，直接验证了DFT破缺对称性自旋密度与完整三维INS数据的一致性。实验、参数化和理论之间的定量一致性为确定磁性形状因子和磁性电子密度建立了稳健框架。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了从INS数据中提取磁性形状因子和磁性电子密度分布的可靠方法，证明了INS作为空间电子波函数包络探针的有效性。这一框架可广泛应用于各类磁性材料的研究，为理解磁性电子密度分布提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: On the textbook example of an isolated antiferromagnetic Heisenberg dimer, we demonstrate that the magnetic form factor and the magnetic electron density distribution can be extracted from the momentum-dependence of the inelastic neutron scattering (INS) intensity of a magnetic excitation. We measure the three-dimensional (3D) magnetic structure factor of the singlet-to-triplet excitation in Cu(II) acetate monohydrate with INS. Using a minimal parametrization of the magnetic electron density, we deduce the real-space density of the spin-entangled electrons and the transfer of magnetic electron density between metal and ligand atoms from the experimental data. Density functional theory (DFT) calculations reproduce the measured structure factor quantitatively, providing a direct validation of DFT broken-symmetry spin densities against full 3D INS data. The quantitative agreement between experiment, parametrization, and theory establishes a robust framework for determining magnetic form factors and the magnetic electron density in a broad range of magnetic materials and demonstrates INS as a probe of the envelope of spatial electronic wavefunctions.

</details>


### [9] [Low temperature Spin freezing and Diffuse Magnetic Correlations in Tb$_{2}$Zr$_{2-x}$Ti$_{x}$O$_{7}$ (x = 0, 0.5)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13864)
*Sujata Singh,Leon Carstens,M. Duc Le,R. Klingeler,C. S. Yadav*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了磁阻挫烧绿石（pyrochlore）系统中结构无序对磁性状态的影响，通过分析Tb₂Zr₂O₇及其Ti掺杂化合物的热力学行为和短程磁关联，揭示了无序诱导的关联磁性状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索磁阻挫烧绿石系统中的结构无序如何影响磁性状态，特别是通过Ti掺杂调控结构从缺陷萤石相向烧绿石相演化过程中的磁行为变化。

Method: 研究方法包括热力学测量、交流磁化率（ac susceptibility）测试和非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）分析，用于表征Tb₂Zr₂O₇和Tb₂Zr₁.₅Ti₀.₅O₇化合物的磁性行为。

Result: 研究结果显示两种化合物在0.4 K以下均无长程磁有序，但在1.25 K（母体）和1.05 K（掺杂）以下出现磁场依赖的自旋冻结（spin freezing）。交流磁化率测量表明20 K以下存在缓慢的自旋弛豫过程，非弹性中子散射揭示了低温下的宽扩散散射，表明存在短程磁关联。

Conclusion: 结论表明Tb₂Zr₂O₇和Tb₂Zr₁.₅Ti₀.₅O₇化合物中存在由结构无序影响的关联磁性状态，这种状态源于局部结构畸变和持续的自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）。

Abstract: Structural disorder in the magnetically frustrated pyrochlore system leads to intriguing magnetic states. We present the thermodynamic behavior and short range magnetic correlations in Tb$_{2}$Zr$_{2}$O$_{7}$ and Tb$_{2}$Zr$_{1.5}$Ti$_{0.5}$O$_{7}$ compounds. The parent compound Tb$_{2}$Zr$_{2}$O$_{7}$ has defect fluorite structure, which evolves toward the pyrochlore phase on Ti doping at Zr site. There is no long range magnetic order down to 0.4 K, and a magnetic field dependent spin freezing evolves below 1.25 K and 1.05 K for the parent and doped compounds, respectively. The ac susceptibility measurements indicate slow spin relaxation process below 20 K in these compounds. Inelastic neutron scattering reveals broad diffuse scattering, indicative of short range correlations at low temperature, owing to local structural distortions and persistent spin fluctuations. These results suggest a correlated, disorder influenced magnetic state in Tb$_{2}$Zr$_{2}$O$_{7}$, Tb$_{2}$Zr$_{1.5}$Ti$_{0.5}$O$_{7}$ compounds.

### [10] [Continuous correlated states and dual-flatness in a moiré heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13958)
*Mohammed M. Al Ezzi,Na Xin,Yanmeng Shi,Shuigang Xu,Julien Barrier,Alexey Berdyugin,Shubhadeep Bhattacharjee,Angelika Knothe,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Vladimir Falko,Giovanni Vignale,Andre K. Geim,Shaffique Adam,Kostya S. Novoselov,Minsoo Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究展示了小角度扭转单层-双层石墨烯中同时存在moire诱导的全局平带和局部能带平坦化效应，这为比较两种相关效应提供了直接平台。全局机制稳定了整数填充的相称态，而局部机制在非整数填充下产生近平坦能带，导致对称性破缺但无全局能隙，表现为反常霍尔响应和谷极化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凝聚态物理中的多体效应在电子态密度增强时会产生新颖量子态。平带通过抑制动能让相互作用主导，但平带和相称填充并非相关现象的唯一条件。局部增强的态密度即使在非整数填充下也能导致强关联，但这类情况常产生赝能隙而难以探测。

Method: 研究采用小角度扭转单层-双层石墨烯（small-angle twisted monolayer-bilayer graphene）作为平台，该系统结合了moire诱导的全局平带和额外的局部能带平坦化效应。通过比较这两种平坦化机制产生的相关效应来验证双重平坦性原理。

Result: 全局平坦化路径稳定了相称态（commensurate states），而局部机制在非整数填充下产生近平坦能带，解除简并并产生对称性破缺，但未打开全局能隙。系统保持金属性，但通过反常霍尔响应（anomalous Hall responses）揭示效应，表明时间反演对称性破缺和谷极化（valley polarization）。

Conclusion: 研究结果证明了双重平坦性（dual-flatness）作为指导原则，将moire物理扩展到相称填充之外，并确定拓扑输运（topological transport）作为无能隙关联金属的探测手段。该系统为比较全局和局部平坦化机制的相关效应提供了独特平台。

Abstract: Many-body effects in condensed matter yield novel quantum states when the electronic density of states is enhanced. A vivid example is flat bands, which suppress kinetic energy and let interactions dominate, when they are filled with an integer number of electrons in moire systems. Yet flat bands and commensurate fillings are not the only conditions for correlated phenomena. Situations may occur where the band structure develops locally enhanced density of states, leading to strong correlations even at non-integer fillings, although such cases often yield pseudogaps that make detection elusive. Here we demonstrate that small-angle twisted monolayer-bilayer graphene combines moire-induced global flat band and additional local band flattening. Their coexistence allows direct comparison of correlated effects. The global route stabilizes commensurate states, while the local mechanism produces nearly flat bands, lifting degeneracy and generating symmetry breaking at non-integer fillings, yet without opening a global gap. Because there is no global gapped signature, the system remains metallic, but the effect reveals itself in anomalous Hall responses, signaling time-reversal symmetry breaking and valley polarization. Our results demonstrate dual-flatness as a guiding principle, extending moire physics beyond commensurate fillings and identifying topological transport as a probe of gapless correlated metals.

</details>


### [11] [Spin-mediated hysteretic switching of unidirectional charge density waves by rotating magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14002)
*Zichao Chen,Shiyu Zhu,Kailin Xu,Ruwen Wang,Ningning Wang,Jianfeng Guo,Yunhao Wang,Xianghe Han,Zhongyi Cao,Jianping Sun,Hui Chen,Haitao Yang,Jinguang Cheng,Ziqiang Wang,Hong-Jun Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在磁性kagome金属GdTi3Bi4中，通过面内磁场旋转实现单向电荷密度波（CDW）取向的确定性和迟滞性切换，揭示了CDW与磁场耦合的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（charge density waves, CDWs）作为量子材料中广泛存在的集体电子序，为理解对称性破缺和竞争相提供了关键见解。然而，通过外场实现CDW的动态控制仍然是一个关键挑战。

Method: 研究在磁性kagome金属GdTi3Bi4中，通过旋转面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field）来驱动CDW构型之间的可逆转变。使用原子级分辨光谱学（atomically resolved spectroscopy）观察两种类型的3a₀×1a₀ CDW畴（Q₁和Q₂），它们沿两个不同的晶向呈60度角排列，并由原子级锐利的畴壁分隔。

Result: 磁场旋转驱动了CDW构型之间的可逆转变，表现出具有显著迟滞现象的稳健C₂对称相图。这种迟滞切换由底层反铁磁自旋（antiferromagnetic spins）的场依赖重取向介导，揭示了具有稳定和亚稳态的可调能量景观，并通过自旋-晶格耦合（spin-lattice coupling）调制电子电荷序。

Conclusion: 该发现不仅展示了通过面内磁场切换CDW构型，还揭示了CDW与磁场耦合的机制，为CDW操控提供了新见解，并为开发自旋介导的多态自旋-电荷耦合存储器（spin-mediated multistate spin-charge coupling memory）和可编程量子器件提供了多功能平台。

Abstract: Charge density waves (CDWs) are a widespread collective electronic order in quantum materials, furnishing key insights into symmetry breaking and competing phases. However, their dynamic control with external fields remains a pivotal challenge. Here, we report deterministic and hysteretic switching of unidirectional CDW orientation via in-plane magnetic field rotation in magnetic kagome metal GdTi3Bi4. Atomically resolved spectroscopy shows two types of 3a0*1a0 CDW domains, Q1 and Q2 oriented 60 degree apart along two distinct crystallographic directions and separated by atomically sharp domain walls. Rotating the magnetic field drives reversible transitions between these CDW configurations, exhibiting a robust C2-symmetric phase diagram with pronounced hysteresis. This hysteretic switching is mediated by a field-dependent reorientation of underlying antiferromagnetic spins, revealing a tunable energy landscape with stable and metastable states and modulates the electronic charge order via spin-lattice coupling. Our findings not only demonstrate the switching of CDW configurations by in-plane magnetic field but also reveal the mechanism of coupling between CDW and magnetic fields, offering new insights into CDW manipulation and versatile platform for developing a spin-mediated multistate spin-charge coupling memory and programmable quantum devices.

### [12] [Tunable bifurcation of magnetic anisotropy and bi-oriented antiferromagnetic order in kagome metal GdTi3Bi4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14012)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过直接可视化两个平台转变过程中的磁畴演化，揭示了沿a轴的显著面内各向异性。温度依赖表征显示约2K时各向异性发生分岔转变，并通过矢量磁场调制阐明了分岔各向异性的特征。

Conclusion: 研究不仅为GdTi3Bi4中磁各向异性的可调分岔提供了重要见解，而且为反铁磁自旋电子学（AFM spintronics）发展开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The novel kagome family RTi3Bi4 (R: rare-earth) offers a unique platform for exploring distinctive physical phenomena such as anisotropy, spin density wave, and anomalous Hall effect. In particular, the magnetic frustration and behavior of magnetic anisotropy in antiferromagnetic (AFM) kagome materials are of great interest for the fundamental studies and hold promise for next-generation device applications. Here, we report a tunable bifurcation of magnetic anisotropic and bi-oriented AFM order observed in the quasi-1D kagome antiferromagnet GdTi3Bi4. The magnetic domain evolutions during two plateau transition processes are directly visualized, unveiling a pronounced in-plane anisotropy along the a-axis. Temperature-dependent characterization reveals a bifurcation transition of anisotropy at approximately 2 K, where the a-axis anisotropy splits into two special orientations, revealing a hidden bi-oriented in-plane AFM order deviating from the high-symmetry direction by 7 degree. More intriguingly, the characteristics of the bifurcated anisotropy are clearly illustrated through vector magnetic field modulation, revealing three distinct in-plane domain phases in the transverse magnetic field phase diagram. Our results not only provide valuable insights into the tunable bifurcation of magnetic anisotropic in GdTi3Bi4, but also pave a novel pathway for AFM spintronics development.

### [13] [Topological anisotropic non-Fermi liquid from a Berry-dipole semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14146)
*Konstantinos Ladovrechis*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了三维Berry偶极半金属（Berry-dipole semimetal）在长程库仑相互作用下的行为，揭示了其向空间各向异性非费米液体（anisotropic non-Fermi liquid）的转变，并伴随增强的Berry偶极矩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究拓扑与电子-电子相互作用之间的相互作用是凝聚态物理领域的重要课题。本文旨在探究位于拓扑量子临界点（topological quantum critical point）的三维Berry偶极半金属在长程库仑相互作用下的演化命运。

Method: 采用大N_f分析（large-$N_f$ analysis）于三维空间，并结合重整化群（renormalization-group）方案中的ε展开（$ε$-expansion）方法进行研究。

Result: 发现了空间各向异性非费米液体（anisotropic non-Fermi liquid）的出现，其Berry偶极矩得到增强。推导了特定物理可观测量作为探测能量和温度尺度的函数的相应标度关系（scaling relations）。

Conclusion: 提供了区分拓扑各向异性非费米液体与Berry偶极半金属起始的简单观测判据，为理解拓扑量子临界点与电子相互作用的耦合效应提供了新见解。

Abstract: Investigating the interplay among topology and electron-electron interactions is an intriguing research quest which has recently gathered steam across the community of condensed-matter physics. In the present work, we study the fate of a three-dimensional Berry-dipole semimetal, lying at the topological quantum critical point separating a Hopf insulator from a trivial insulator, in the presence of long-range Coulomb interactions. Utilizing large-$N_f$ analysis at three spatial dimensions and an $ε$-expansion within the renormalization-group scheme, we uncover the emergence of a spatially \textit{anisotropic} non-Fermi liquid with enhanced Berry-dipole moment. We further derive the corresponding scaling relations of certain physical observables as functions of the probed energy and temperature scale, and we provide a simple observational criterion for distinguishing the onset of the topological anisotropic non-Fermi liquid from a Berry-dipole semimetal.

### [14] [Unified Microscopic Theory of Stress Relaxation, Structural Evolution, and Memory Effects in Dense Glass Forming Brownian Suspensions After Flow Cessation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13284)
*Anoop Mutneja,Kenneth S. Schweizer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个微观统计力学理论，统一预测非晶固体在机械驱动屈服后从非平衡态重新固化的结构恢复和应力松弛耦合演化过程，应用于硬球布朗胶体悬浮液体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶固体在机械驱动屈服后从非平衡态重新固化是一个基础软物质科学问题，对材料强度、加工和基于打印的增材制造具有重要意义。理解结构恢复和应力松弛的耦合演化过程具有广泛材料科学相关性。

Method: 基于对静态和启动连续剪切条件下布朗系统活化动力学的最新理解，建立了一个粒子级微观流变模型框架。该框架自洽地结合了应力生成、外部机械力导致的约束软化以及结构变形。

Result: 理论捕捉了流动停止后动力学约束和活化势垒随时间重建的过程，这些过程构成了结构恢复、应力松弛和通过动态松弛及对流弹性回流基本形式实现的重新固化的基础。理论正确捕捉了实验观察到的丰富应力松弛行为，包括从指数型、拉伸指数型到分数幂律型随堆积分数增加的形式演变。

Conclusion: 该理论为基于粒子的材料提供了通用框架，并定量应用于致密硬球布朗胶体悬浮液，这同时也是热波动重要的玻璃形成材料的基础范式。实现了对实验室时间尺度上表观残余应力出现、幂律无尽老化、弹性模量S型恢复、预剪切速率依赖记忆效应以及可与应力松弛解耦的两步结构松弛过程的微观理解。

Abstract: The re-solidification of amorphous solids after mechanically driven yielding from a nonequilibrium state is a fundamental soft matter science problem of broad relevance in materials science, with implications for material strength, processing, and printing-based additive manufacturing. We present a microscopic statistical mechanical theory that predicts in a unified manner the coupled time evolutions of structural and stress recovery following shear cessation from a mechanically prepared nonequilibrium state. The approach is built on recent advances in understanding activated dynamics in Brownian systems under both quiescent and startup continuous shear conditions. A particle-level microrheological model framework self-consistently incorporates stress generation, constraint softening due to external mechanical forces and structural deformation. After flow cessation, the theory captures the re-building of kinetic constraints and activation barriers over time that underlie structural recovery, stress relaxation, and re-solidification through dynamic relaxation and an elementary form of convective elastic backflow. The ideas are general for particle-based materials, and quantitatively applied to dense hard-sphere Brownian colloidal suspensions which also serve as a foundational paradigm for glass forming materials where thermal fluctuations are important. The theory properly captures the rich range of stress relaxation behaviors observed experimentally that evolve from exponential, to stretched exponential, to fractional power law in form with increasing packing fraction. A microscopic understanding is achieved of the emergence of apparent residual stresses on laboratory timescales, power-law endless aging, sigmoidal recovery of the elastic modulus, pre-shear-rate-dependent memory effects, and a two-step structural relaxation process that can become decoupled from stress relaxation.

</details>


### [15] [Dynamical Theory of Elastic Synchronization of Cardiomyocytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13391)
*Akinari Tomiie,Nariya Uchida*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过弹性基底介导的相互作用，探讨了两个心肌细胞（cardiomyocytes）的同步现象。基于振荡力偶极子（oscillating force dipole）模型和相位约化理论（phase reduction theory），研究揭示了细胞相对取向（mutual orientation）对同步状态选择的几何依赖性，预测了同相（in-phase）或反相（anti-phase）搏动的稳定收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解心肌细胞通过周围介质的弹性响应（elastic response）实现同步搏动的机制。该工作试图弥合早期的能量双体理论（energetic two-body theory）与动力学单细胞理论（dynamical single-cell theory）之间的鸿沟，为心肌细胞的弹性同步（elastic synchronization）提供一个动力学框架（dynamical framework）。

Method: 将每个心肌细胞建模为由瑞利型方程（Rayleigh-type equation）控制的振荡力偶极子（oscillating force dipole），从周围介质的弹性响应中推导出有效的机械耦合（mechanical coupling）。运用相位约化理论（phase reduction theory），并结合直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations），获得了两个心肌细胞的动力学相位描述（dynamical phase description）。

Result: 研究发现，根据细胞的相对取向（mutual orientation），细胞会稳定地收敛到同相（in-phase）或反相（anti-phase）搏动状态，产生一个具有非平凡状态边界（nontrivial state boundary）的取向依赖性状态图（orientation-dependent state map）。同步时间（synchronization time）也强烈依赖于细胞间的距离和相对取向。

Conclusion: 该研究预测了同步状态的几何依赖性选择（geometry-dependent selection），为心肌细胞的弹性同步提供了一个动力学框架（dynamical framework），连接了早期的理论方法，并揭示了细胞排列在协调组织水平搏动中的重要作用。

Abstract: We study synchronization of two cardiomyocytes mediated by elastic interactions through the substrate. Modeling each cell as an oscillating force dipole governed by a Rayleigh-type equation, we derive an effective mechanical coupling from the elastic response of the surrounding medium. Using phase reduction theory, supported by direct numerical simulations, we obtain a dynamical phase description for two cardiomyocytes that predicts geometry-dependent selection of synchronized states. Depending on the mutual orientation, the cells robustly converge to either in-phase or anti-phase beating, yielding an orientation-dependent state map with a nontrivial state boundary. The synchronization time also depends strongly on the distance and mutual orientation of the cells. These results bridge earlier energetic two-body theory and dynamical single-cell theory, and provide a dynamical framework for elastic synchronization of cardiomyocytes.

</details>


### [16] [Universal Scaling of Freezing Morphodynamics in Polymer Solution Droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13420)
*Nicolas G. Ulrich,Pravin P. Aravindhan,Olivia Berger,Bryan S. Beckingham,Jean-François Louf*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析聚合物溶液液滴的凝固过程，发现了一个单一的无量纲参数——毛细-刘易斯数（Capillary-Lewis number），该参数能够统一描述从稀溶液到缠结体系九个数量级范围内的凝固形态和动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂流体的凝固在自然和技术过程中普遍存在，但聚合物溶液因其传输和流变性质在凝固过程中的动态演化而难以预测。研究旨在理解聚合物溶液液滴从稀溶液到缠结体系的凝固行为。

Method: 研究考察了聚合物溶液液滴在稀溶液到缠结体系范围内的凝固过程，通过分析凝固形态和动力学，识别控制凝固行为的关键无量纲参数。

Result: 研究发现液滴形态和凝固动力学由单一无量纲参数——毛细-刘易斯数控制，该参数捕捉了粘性应力、毛细作用和溶质传输之间的竞争关系。圆形度、径向变形和凝固时间在九个数量级范围内坍缩到一条主曲线上，揭示了在接近1时的转变点。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一个最小化的传输-力学框架，将聚合物溶液凝固过程中的溶质再分布与界面变形联系起来。该框架在粘性流体体系中适用于不同聚合物化学结构，但在弹性主导响应（G' > G''）时出现偏差，表明纯传输-毛细控制的失效。

Abstract: Freezing of complex fluids is central to a wide range of natural and technological processes, where the interplay between heat transport, solute redistribution, and interfacial deformation gives rise to complex morphologies. Unlike simple liquids, polymer solutions exhibit strongly coupled transport and rheological properties that evolve dynamically during solidification, making their freezing behavior difficult to predict. Here, we examine the freezing of polymer solution droplets spanning dilute to entangled regimes. We find that droplet morphology and freezing dynamics in viscous solutions are governed by a single dimensionless parameter, the Capillary--Lewis number, which captures the competition between viscous stresses, capillarity, and solute transport. Circularity, radial deformation, and freezing time collapse onto a master curve spanning nine orders of magnitude, revealing a transition near unity corresponding to the point at which solute diffusion can no longer relax concentration gradients ahead of the freezing interface. This collapse holds across distinct polymer chemistries within the viscous fluid regime, while deviations emerge when the material exhibits elastic-dominated response ($G' > G''$), indicating the breakdown of purely transport--capillary control. These results establish a minimal transport--mechanics framework linking solute redistribution to interfacial deformation during freezing polymer solutions.

</details>


### [17] [Coarse-Grained Model of the Sodium Dodecyl Sulfate Anionic Surfactant Based on the MDPD--Martini Force Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13499)
*Luís H. Carnevale,Gabriela Niechwiadowicz,Panagiotis E. Theodorakis*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究基于MDPD-Martini力场开发了十二烷基硫酸钠（SDS）表面活性剂/水系统的粗粒化模型，该模型能够准确再现实验表面张力等温线，为含显式电荷的软物质系统模拟提供了可靠的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 十二烷基硫酸钠（SDS）表面活性剂广泛应用于日化产品和食品制造，需要开发合适的计算模型来研究其性质。粗粒化（coarse-grained, CG）模型特别适合捕捉表面活性剂的自组装（self-assembly）行为及其在水系统中的基本性质。

Method: 基于MDPD-Martini力场（force field, FF）开发了SDS/水系统的多体耗散粒子动力学（many-body dissipative particle dynamics, MDPD）粗粒化模型。该模型显式建模了带电荷基团（硫酸盐头基和钠阳离子），其余相互作用参数则从先前用于脂质系统的MDPD-Martini模型转移而来。

Result: 模型研究了相干散射强度和液-气界面表面活性剂分布等性质，并与分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟和实验结果进行了比较。MDPD-Martini模型能够准确再现实验表面张力等温线（surface tension isotherm），而MD模拟则无法做到这一点。

Conclusion: MDPD-Martini模型为含显式电荷的系统（如SDS）提供了可靠的MD-Martini模型替代方案。由于MDPD-Martini相互作用的可转移性（transferability），该研究的模型参数可扩展应用于更广泛的软物质系统模拟。

Abstract: The sodium dodecyl sulfate (SDS) surfactant is widely used in various applications, such as household products (e.g., shampoos, toothpaste, detergents, and cleaning products) and food manufacturing (e.g., emulsifiers). To investigate its properties via computer simulation, various models have been developed, including coarse-grained (CG) models that are suitable for capturing a surfactant's self-assembly and fundamental properties for aqueous systems with a surfactant, such as surface tension. Here, we present a CG model for SDS/water systems for many-body dissipative particle dynamics (MDPD), which is based on the MDPD--Martini force field (FF). In the model, charged groups, namely, the SDS sulfate headgroup and the sodium cation, are explicitly modeled following the standard mapping of the Martini force field for molecular dynamics (MD), while the remaining interactions have been obtained from previous MDPD--Martini models for lipid systems, thus demonstrating their transferability. Various relevant system properties, such as the coherent scattered intensity and surfactant distribution at the liquid--vapor surface, are investigated, and results are compared to those obtained by MD simulations and experiments at different surfactant concentrations. Our findings indicate that MDPD--Martini models can offer a credible alternative to MD--Martini models for systems with explicit charges as shown here for SDS. Moreover, MDPD--Martini models reproduce nicely the experimental surface tension isotherm, in contrast to MD simulations. In view of the transferability of the MDPD--Martini interactions, the model parameters of this study can be tested and used to simulate a wider range of soft-matter systems.

</details>

Abstract: In this perspective article, we discuss bacterial populations as a model system of active matter. Specifically, we focus on active gas, active liquid, active glass and active liquid crystal states observed in bacterial populations and describe how these differ from their thermal counterparts. A few future directions are also discussed that will deepen the physical interest in active matter as a new type of material, with its implications for several life phenomena observed in bacterial populations and other biological systems.

### [19] [Ternary liquid crystalline mixture showing broad antiferroelectric smectic C$_A$* and glassy hexatic smectic X$_A$* phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13653)
*Aleksandra Deptuch,Anna Drzewicz,Marcin Piwowarczyk,Michał Czerwiński,Mateusz Filipow,Mateusz Pączek,Ewa Juszyńska-Gałązka*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究设计了一种三元液晶混合物以获得玻璃态下的倾斜六方近晶相，通过结构、电光和介电性质表征，发现该混合物稳定了宽温域的SmC_A*相并实现了六方SmX_A*相的玻璃化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在设计一种三元液晶混合物，以获得玻璃态下的倾斜六方近晶相（tilted hexatic smectic phase），这对于研究液晶材料的玻璃化行为和相变特性具有重要意义。

Method: 通过X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）确定垂直近晶层的电子密度分布，并与密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算结果对比；测量混合物及其纯组分的结构、电光和介电性质；利用偏光显微镜观察SmC*、SmC_A*和SmX_A*相的选择性光反射；通过量热法检测玻璃化转变。

Result: 实验确定了混合物中近晶层间距和倾斜角，评估了分子二聚化可能性；在SmC_A*相中测定了螺旋螺距；在SmX_A*相中观察到玻璃化转变；介电谱检测到次级β-和γ-过程，但未直接显示初级α-过程；结构数据表明SmC*和SmC_A*相之间存在分子组织变化。

Conclusion: 三元混合物稳定了宽温域的SmC_A*相，并实现了六方SmX_A*相的玻璃化；结构数据揭示了SmC*和SmC_A*相之间的分子组织差异，为液晶材料的玻璃化行为研究提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: A ternary liquid crystalline mixture was designed to obtain a tilted hexatic smectic phase in the glassy state. Structural, electro-optic, and dielectric properties of the mixture are investigated, and selected measurements are also performed for its pure components. In particular, the electron density profile perpendicular to smectic layers is determined from the X-ray diffraction data and compared to the results of density functional theory calculations both for the mixture and pure components. Comparison of the experimental smectic layer spacing and tilt angle in the mixture allows us to assess whether molecular dimerization is likely to occur. On the mesoscopic scale, the helical pitch is determined in the SmC$_A$* phase of the mixture, and selective reflection of light is observed under a polarizing microscope in the SmC*, SmC$_A$*, and SmX$_A$* phases. The glass transition in the smectic X$_A$* phase is observed in calorimetric results. At the same time, the dielectric spectra do not directly reveal the primary $α$-process, although the secondary $β$- and $γ$-processes are detected. Overall, the results show that the ternary mixture stabilizes a broad SmC$_A$* phase and enables vitrification of the hexatic SmX$_A$* phase, while the structural data suggest a change in the molecular organization between the SmC* and SmC$_A$* phases.

### [20] [Hierarchical Bayesian calibration of mesoscopic models for ultrasound contrast agents from force spectroscopy data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13657)
*Brieuc Benvegnen,Nikolaos Ntarakas,Tilen Potisk,Ignacio Pagonabarraga,Matej Praprotnik*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于深度神经网络代理的贝叶斯校准工作流，用于高效校准包封微泡（EMBs）的高保真粒子模型力学参数，并应用于Definity和SonoVue两种商用超声造影剂的建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超声引导药物和基因递送（USDG）是一种有前景的非侵入性靶向治疗方法。包封微泡（EMBs）作为造影剂，其力学特性强烈影响其与超声的特定相互作用，因此对USDG的成功和效率至关重要。然而，使用耗散粒子动力学（DPD）进行直接贝叶斯推断来校准高保真粒子模型的计算成本极高。

Method: 研究采用了一种代理加速的贝叶斯校准工作流，结合了深度神经网络（DNN）代理、过渡马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（TMCMC）采样以及跨EMB直径的分层正则化。基于该框架，开发了两种商用EMB制剂（Definity和SonoVue）的数据驱动DPD模型，并基于已发表的压缩实验（Definity）和压痕实验（SonoVue）数据推断力场参数，每种实验涵盖三个不同直径。

Result: 推断的后验分布显示，关键模型参数（如拉伸刚度和弯曲模量）受到可用数据的一致约束。该方法可用于为广泛的超声造影剂（包括包封气体囊泡、由脂质、蛋白质或聚合物组成的多种囊壳的EMBs，以及功能化配体）开发定制的数据驱动模型。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法学能够为多种超声造影剂建立定制的、数据驱动的模型，解决了直接贝叶斯推断计算成本过高的问题，为超声引导治疗中EMBs力学特性的精确建模提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Ultrasound-guided drug and gene delivery (USDG) is a promising non-invasive approach for targeted therapeutic applications. Mechanical properties of encapsulated microbubbles (EMBs), which serve as contrast agents, strongly affect their specific interactions with ultrasound and are thus critical to the success and efficiency of USDG. Accurate calibration of high-fidelity particle-based models of EMB capsid mechanics is computationally challenging because direct Bayesian inference with dissipative particle dynamics (DPD) is prohibitively expensive. We employ a surrogate-accelerated Bayesian calibration workflow that combines deep neural network (DNN) surrogates, transitional Markov chain Monte Carlo sampling, and hierarchical regularization across EMB diameters. Using this framework, we develop two data-informed DPD models of commercial EMB agents, i.e., Definity and SonoVue, and perform inference of force field parameters based on published compression experiments for Definity and indentation experiments for SonoVue, each spanning three distinct diameters. The inferred posteriors show that key model parameters, such as the stretching stiffness and bending modulus, are consistently constrained by the available data. The presented methodology can be used to derive bespoke, data-informed models for a wide range of ultrasound contrast agents, including encapsulated gas vesicles, EMBs with diverse capsids consisting of lipids, proteins, or polymers, and functionalized with ligands.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文采用比较分析方法，评估两种主要建模范式：基于粒子的模型（明确表示离散组分及其相互作用）和连续介质模型（通过空间变化场描述系统）。分析跨越不同生物尺度，并聚焦于五个关键生物系统。

Abstract: Quantitative modeling has become an essential tool in modern biophysics, driven by advances in both experimental techniques and theoretical frameworks. Powerful high-resolution techniques now provide detailed datasets spanning molecular to tissue scales, allowing to visualize cellular structures with unprecedented detail. In parallel, developments in soft and active matter physics have established a robust theoretical basis for describing biological systems. In this context, two main modeling paradigms have emerged: particle-based models, which explicitly represent discrete components and their interactions, and continuum models, which describe systems through spatially varying fields. We compare these approaches across biological scales, highlighting their respective strengths, limitations, and domains of applicability. To keep our discussion biologically relevant, we focus on five systems of fundamental importance: the cytoskeleton, membranes, chromatin, biomolecular condensates and tissues. With this Review, we thus aim to provide a framework for both theorists and experimentalists to select appropriate modeling strategies, and highlight future directions in biophysical modeling.

### [22] [A Unified Glassy Rheology for Granular Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14109)
*Zhikun Zeng,Jiazhao Xu,Hanyu Li,Shiang Zhang,Houfei Yuan,Chijin Zhou,Xueliang Dai,Haiyang Lu,Xin Wang,Jun Zhao,Yonglun Jiang,Zhuan Ge,Gang Huang,Chengjie Xia,Jianqi Sun,Yan Xi,Yujie Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过高速X射线断层扫描技术研究密实颗粒流，建立了基于结构弛豫（structural relaxation）的普适本构定律，统一了准静态到惯性区域的颗粒流变学，并建立了非平衡统计框架，揭示了驱动颗粒物质与硬球液体之间的内在类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒流在自然和工业应用中普遍存在，但完整的连续介质理论仍是长期挑战。主导的经验方法μ(I)流变学缺乏微观基础，且在需要非局部修正的密实、慢剪切流中变得多值化。

Method: 利用最先进的高速X射线断层扫描技术研究库埃特几何中的密实颗粒流微观动力学，建立了基于结构弛豫的普适本构定律。进一步建立了颗粒流的非平衡统计框架。

Result: 建立了跨越准静态到惯性区域的普适本构定律，解决了原始μ(I)框架的基本困难。通过非平衡统计框架，证明了驱动颗粒物质与硬球液体因其相同的Carnahan-Starling状态方程而具有内在类比，自然解释了流变学方法和玻璃化行为的出现。

Conclusion: 该框架将颗粒流变学与更广泛的非平衡系统物理学统一起来，为密实颗粒流提供了完整的、基于微观的理论框架。

Abstract: Granular flows are ubiquitous in nature and industrial applications, yet a complete continuum theory remains a long-standing challenge. The leading empirical approach, μ(I) rheology, lacks microscopic foundations and becomes multivalued in dense, slowly sheared flows where nonlocal corrections are required. Exploiting state-of-the-art high-speed X-ray tomography to investigate microscopic dynamics of dense granular flows in a Couette geometry, we establish a new, universal constitutive law spanning quasi-static to inertial regimes based on structural relaxation, resolving the fundamental difficulty in the original μ(I) framework. By further establishing a non-equilibrium statistical framework for granular flows, we demonstrate an intrinsic analogy between driven granular matter and hard-sphere liquids owing to their identical Carnahan-Starling equation of state, naturally explaining our rheological approach and the emergence of glassy behaviors. Our framework unifies granular rheology with the broader physics of disordered systems and provides a complete, microscopically-based theoretical framework for dense granular flow.

### [23] [Distributional Inverse Homogenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14083)
*Arnaud Vadeboncoeur,Mark Girolami,Kaushik Bhattacharya,Andrew M. Stuart*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种称为"分布逆均质化（distributional inverse homogenization）"的非侵入性方法，通过大量宏观力学性质测量数据来学习微观结构统计信息，解决了从宏观性质反推微观结构的逆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统均质化理论（homogenization）能够将微观结构映射到宏观力学性质，但逆向过程（从宏观性质恢复微观信息）因平均化过程而困难重重。科学家和工程师通常需要依赖侵入性、高度局部化的调查来了解微观结构。

Method: 本文开发了一种非侵入性方法，利用大量测量的宏观力学性质集合来学习微观结构的全局统计信息。该方法在一维和二维空间中研究，同时考虑了周期性和随机性均质化（periodic and stochastic homogenization），并在二维Voronoi构造中进行了演示。

Result: 研究展示了如何利用微观结构的自然空间变异性来收集数据以实现分布逆均质化。同时学习了一个替代模型（surrogate model）来近似均质化映射，从而加速了计算过程。在一维情况下，通过理论支撑了观察到的经验成功。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了一类新的逆问题，将概率论和均质化理论的思想相结合，促进了从宏观测量中学习微观结构材料变异性的能力，为材料科学中的多尺度分析提供了新方法。

Abstract: For many materials, macroscopic mechanical behavior is determined by an intricate microstructure. Understanding the relation between these two scales helps scientists and engineers design better materials. The relation which maps microstructure to bulk mechanical properties can be understood via the well-established theory of homogenization. However inverting the homogenization process, to recover microstructural information from measured macroscopic properties, is fraught with difficulties because of the averaging processes that underlie homogenization. Therefore, scientists and engineers usually need recourse to more invasive, often highly localized, investigations to learn about a microstructure. In this work, we develop a noninvasive methodology by which one can leverage large collections of measured bulk mechanical properties to learn information about the statistics of microstructure at a global level. We call this, distributional inverse homogenization. We study this problem in one and two dimensions, considering both periodic and stochastic homogenization. We demonstrate the methodology in the context of 2D Voronoi constructions and underpin the observed empirical success with theory in 1D. We also show how the natural spatial variability of microstructure can be exploited to gather data that enables distributional inversion. And we concurrently learn a surrogate model, approximating the homogenization map, that accelerates the resulting computations in this setting. The work formulates a new class of inverse problems, bridging ideas from probability and homogenization to facilitate the learning of microstructural material variability from macroscopic measurements.

</details>

### [24] [Geometric Spin Degeneracy in Spin-Orbit-Free Compensated Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13266)
*Seung Hun Lee,Yuting Qian,Xi Dai,Bohm-Jung Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究建立了无自旋轨道耦合补偿磁体的理论框架，揭示自旋简并可由几何约束而非传统对称性保护，解释了补偿亚铁磁体中非常规能带简并的起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 补偿磁体（compensated magnets）在净磁化为零时仍能展现显著的自旋劈裂和非常规能带简并。补偿亚铁磁体（compensated ferrimagnets）中的简并可能在没有相应对称性保护的情况下出现，这引发了关于无自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit-free）磁性系统中自旋简并起源的基本问题。

Method: 研究者为无自旋轨道耦合补偿磁体开发了一个理论框架，其中自旋简并由几何约束而非自旋对称性保护。该分析适用于弱相互作用（weak-interaction）区域，识别了超越群论保护的自旋简并一般机制。

Result: 研究表明，零净磁化对形式上自旋简并能带形成的节点（nodes）出现施加了强约束条件，即使在没有传统自旋对称性的情况下也是如此。该框架解释了最近在补偿亚铁磁体中报道的非常规自旋简并，并为自旋轨道耦合可忽略的广泛磁性相中的能带简并提供统一描述。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了超越群论保护的自旋简并一般机制，为理解补偿磁体中非常规能带简并提供了统一的理论框架，特别适用于自旋轨道耦合可忽略的磁性系统。

Abstract: Compensated magnets with vanishing net magnetization can exhibit both pronounced spin splitting and unconventional band degeneracies. In altermagnets, such degeneracies are enforced by crystal and magnetic symmetries. In compensated ferrimagnets, however, they may arise even in the absence of the corresponding symmetry protection, raising a fundamental question about the origin of spin degeneracy in spin-orbit-free magnetic systems. Here, we develop a theoretical framework for spin-orbit-free compensated magnets in which spin degeneracies are protected by geometric constraints rather than by spin symmetry. We show that zero net magnetization imposes a strong condition for the emergence of nodes formed by formally spin-degenerate bands, even when no conventional spin symmetry is present. Our analysis, applicable in the weak-interaction regime, identifies a general mechanism for spin degeneracy beyond group-theoretical protection. The framework accounts for the unconventional spin degeneracies recently reported in compensated ferrimagnets and provides a unified description of band degeneracies across a broad class of magnetic phases with negligible spin-orbit coupling.

</details>


### [25] [Spin-Dependent Charge-State Conversion in NV Ensembles Mediated by Electron Tunneling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13337)
*Neil B. Manson,Morgan Hedges,Michael S. J. Barson,Carlos A. Meriles,Ronald Ulbricht,Marcus W. Doherty*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了金刚石中氮空位（NV）中心在特定激发波长下，NV0电荷态的发射与NV-自旋极化相关，从而可将全部荧光信号用于量子传感检测，提升灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基于NV中心的量子传感应用中，NV-和NV0两种电荷态共存带来挑战：NV-的自旋依赖特性是检测基础，而NV0荧光缺乏有用对比度，通常作为背景噪声被去除，减少了可用信号。

Method: 研究使用不同氮浓度的NV中心系综，比较了在575nm（NV0零声子线）和常用532nm波长下的激发效果，分析了NV0发射的起源机制。

Result: 发现575nm激发主要通过自旋选择性隧穿（spin-selective tunneling）从NV-激发态到邻近氮施主产生NV0，使得NV0荧光遵循NV-的自旋极化，从而贡献可测量的自旋对比度。

Conclusion: 该机制允许利用全部荧光信号进行检测，为基于NV中心的传感应用提供了提升灵敏度的新途径。

Abstract: The nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center in diamond enables optical initialization and readout of its electronic spin, forming the basis of a wide range of quantum sensing and metrology applications. A central challenge in such measurements is the coexistence of two charge states, NV- and NV0: While detection protocols rely on the spin-dependent properties of NV-, fluorescence from NV0 does not carry useful contrast and is typically removed as background, reducing the available signal. Here, we show that the origin of NV0 emission depends strongly on the excitation wavelength in nitrogen-containing diamond. Using ensembles of NV centers with varying nitrogen concentrations, we compare excitation at the NV0 zero-phonon line (ZPL) at 575 nm with the commonly used 532 nm. We find that excitation at 575 nm generates NV0 predominantly through spin-selective tunneling from the excited state of NV- to nearby nitrogen donors, such that the NV0 emission follows the spin polarization of NV-. As a result, the NV0 fluorescence contributes to the measurable spin contrast, allowing the full fluorescence signal to be used for detection. This result opens opportunities for improved sensitivity in NV-based sensing applications.

</details>


### [26] [Cryogenic Loss Limits in Microwave Epitaxial AlN Acoustic Resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13364)
*Hemant Gulupalli,Navnil Choudhury,Jiacheng Xie,Yufeng Wu,Huili Grace Xing,Hong X. Tang,Debdeep Jena,Kanad Basu,Wenwen Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个基于物理的模型来预测氮化铝薄膜体声波谐振器在低温下的品质因数极限，通过6.5K至300K的射频测量验证了模型准确性，为超导量子硬件的低温微波滤波器设计提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氮化铝薄膜体声波谐振器是6G通信和量子存储器件的紧凑平台，但其性能受温度依赖性声学耗散限制。当前缺乏能够预测低温下品质因数极限的理论模型，阻碍了超导量子硬件中低温微波滤波器的优化设计。

Method: 研究团队制备了16GHz外延氮化铝薄膜体声波谐振器作为测试平台，在6.5K至300K温度范围内进行小信号射频测量。开发了一个包含本征和非本征损耗机制的物理模型，特别提出了体声波谐振器的锚点辐射损耗解析模型，而非依赖有限元模拟。

Result: 测量结果显示加载品质因数随温度单调下降：从6.5K时的约1589（Qf=24.79 THz）降至294K时的363（Qf=5.66 THz）。这一趋势与基于谐振器几何结构和金属-绝缘体-金属堆叠的理论极限一致。通过23GHz高次谐波体声波谐振器的基准测试进一步验证了模型的普适性。

Conclusion: 验证后的模型提供了一个实用、可迁移的理论框架，能够通过量化限制品质因数的温度依赖性机制来解释低损耗谐振器的Q(T)极限。该框架为超导量子硬件的低温微波滤波器元件设计提供了理论基础，有助于优化量子存储器件的性能。

Abstract: Aluminum nitride (AlN)-based thin-film bulk acoustic wave resonators (FBARs) are promising compact platforms for 6G communications and quantum memory hardware, enabled by their integrable acoustic modes with high quality factors. However, temperature-dependent acoustic dissipation ultimately limits device performance. In this work, we fabricated a 16 GHz epitaxial AlN FBAR as a test platform, performed small-signal RF measurements from 6.5 K to 300 K, and developed a physics-based model to estimate the fundamental quality-factor limits of FBARs to cryogenic temperatures. The proposed model incorporates both intrinsic and extrinsic loss mechanisms, including an analytical anchor-radiation loss model for bulk acoustic wave resonators, rather than relying solely on finite-element simulations. Measured loaded quality factor (Q) decreases monotonically with temperature, from Qmax of approximately 1589 (Qf=24.79 THz) at 6.5 K to 363 at 294K (Qf=5.66 THz). This trend is consistent with the theoretical limit based on the resonator geometry and the chosen Metal-Insulator-Metal (MIM) stack. To demonstrate the generality of the physics-based framework, we further validate it by benchmarking against a 23 GHz high-overtone bulk acoustic resonator (HBAR) using previously reported data. The validated model provides a practical, transferable framework to interpret Q(T) limits in low-loss resonators by quantifying the temperature-dependent mechanisms that constrain Q, enabling the design of cryogenic microwave filter elements for superconducting quantum hardware.

</details>


### [27] [Sub-nm range momentum-dependent exciton transfer from a 2D semiconductor to graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13445)
*Aditi Raman Moghe,Delphine Lagarde,Sotirios Papadopoulos,Etienne Lorchat,Luis E. Parra López,Loïc Moczko,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Michelangelo Romeo,Maxime Mauguet,Xavier Marie,Arnaud Gloppe,Cédric Robert,Stéphane Berciaud*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过时间分辨光致发光光谱技术，在低温条件下测量了MoSe₂单层与石墨烯异质结中的激子转移时间约为2.5 ps，发现转移机制主要由电荷隧穿过程主导，而非偶极相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫化物（TMD）与石墨烯构成的范德华异质结（van der Waals heterostructures）是光电器件的重要构建模块，但关于其中电荷和能量转移机制的关键问题仍未解决。研究旨在阐明TMD/石墨烯界面耦合中的激子转移机制。

Method: 采用时间分辨光致发光光谱（time-resolved photoluminescence spectroscopy）技术，具有1 ps分辨率，在低温条件下直接测量MoSe₂单层与"阶梯状"多层石墨烯薄片耦合的异质结。同时对比研究了MoSe₂单层通过六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride）介电间隔层与石墨烯分离的样品。

Result: 在低温条件下观察到激子转移时间约为2.5 ps，且基本不受石墨烯层数影响。当介电间隔层厚度达到1 nm时，激子转移完全消失。结果表明电荷隧穿过程（charge tunnelling processes）主导激子动力学，而偶极相互作用（dipolar interactions）对亮激子（bright excitons）无显著影响，但可能加速有限动量"热"激子（hot excitons）的弛豫。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了范德华材料中电荷和能量转移的机制，表明电荷隧穿是主要过程，而Förster型能量转移对亮激子影响可忽略。这些发现对能量收集和汇聚应用具有直接指导意义。

Abstract: Van der Waals heterostructures made from atomically thin transition metal dichalcogenides (TMD) and graphene have emerged as a building block for optoelectronic devices. Such systems are also uniquely poised to investigate interfacial coupling as well as photoinduced charge and energy transfer in the 2D limit. Recent works have revealed efficient photoluminescence quenching and picosecond transfer in TMD/graphene heterostructures. However, key questions regarding the transfer mechanisms remain. Here, employing time-resolved photoluminescence spectroscopy with 1~ps resolution in MoSe$_2$ monolayer directly coupled to a few-layer ``staircase-like'' graphene flake, we consistently observe an exciton transfer time of $\approx 2.5~\mathrm{ps}$ at cryogenic temperature that is marginally affected by the number of graphene layers. Remarkably, exciton transfer vanishes in samples consisting in an MoSe$_2$ monolayer separated from graphene by a thin dielectric spacer of hexagonal boron nitride, as soon as the spacer thickness reaches 1~nm. These results suggest that charge tunnelling processes govern exciton dynamics. Other mechanisms mediated the dipolar interactions (Förster-type energy transfer) have no measurable impact on bright excitons (with near-zero center of mass momentum) but may accelerate the relaxation of finite momentum ``hot'' excitons, leading to larger photoluminescence quenching than anticipated based on the measurements of the photoluminescence decay rates. Our work provides important insights into charge and energy transfer in van der Waals materials with direct implications for energy harvesting and funneling.

</details>


### [28] [Emergence of Nontrivial Topological Magnon States in Skyrmionium Lattices with Zero Topological Charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13451)
*Xingen Zheng,Ping Tang,Xuejuan Liu,Zhixiong Li,Peng Yan,Hao Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究预测了零拓扑电荷斯格明子晶格中非平凡拓扑磁子态的出现，提出了加权磁通量概念，并将其映射到Haldane模型，挑战了此类态必须与非零拓扑电荷相关的传统观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索斯格明子晶格（skyrmionium lattice）中拓扑磁子态（topological magnon states）的出现机制，挑战传统认为此类态仅与斯格明子晶格的非零拓扑电荷相关的观点。

Method: 提出了加权磁通量（weighted magnetic flux）概念以解释该异常现象，并将斯格明子晶格映射到Haldane模型（Haldane model）提供替代解释框架；为实验验证提出了两种制备斯格明子晶格的方法，并计算了诱导的磁子热霍尔电导率（magnon thermal Hall conductivity）。

Result: 预测了零拓扑电荷斯格明子晶格中非平凡拓扑磁子态的出现，加权磁通量概念为此现象提供了清晰的物理图像，Haldane模型映射提供了替代解释框架。

Conclusion: 研究挑战了拓扑磁子态必须与斯格明子晶格非零拓扑电荷相关的传统观点，为拓扑磁子学（topological magnonics）提供了新视角；提出的实验方法和热霍尔电导率计算为实验验证提供了关键指标。

Abstract: We predict the emergence of nontrivial topological magnon states in the skyrmionium lattice with zero topological charge. We propose the concept of weighted magnetic flux, which provides a clear physical picture for this anomalous phenomenon. We also map the skyrmionium lattice onto the Haldane model, offering an alternative framework for interpreting this. Our findings challenge the conventional wisdom that such states are linked to nonzero topological charge in skyrmion lattices, offering a new perspective in topological magnonics. To facilitate experimental validation, we propose two methods for preparing the skyrmionium lattice and calculate the induced magnon thermal Hall conductivity, which is a key indicator in transport measurements.

</details>


### [29] [Coherent control of thermal transport with pillar-based phononic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13527)
*Tatu A. S. Korkiamäki,Tuomas A. Puurtinen,Mikko Kivekäs,Teemu Loippo,Adam Krysztofik,Bartlomiej Graczykowski,Ilari J. Maasilta*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了基于铝柱阵列的二维声子晶体（phononic crystals）在亚开尔文温度下可实现热导率的相干控制，相比未改性膜层热导率降低达一个数量级，但大晶格常数下相干理论失效，表明表面粗糙度引起的扩散散射破坏了相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于孔阵列的二维声子晶体已用于低温下热导率的相干控制，本研究旨在探索基于铝柱阵列的声子晶体是否也能实现类似相干控制，并研究其在不同晶格常数下的热输运特性。

Method: 研究采用实验测量与理论模拟相结合的方法，在未切割的SiN膜上制备了四种不同晶格常数（0.3至5 μm）的铝柱阵列声子晶体，并在亚开尔文温度下测量其热导率，同时进行相干理论模拟对比分析。

Result: 铝柱阵列声子晶体相比未改性膜层热导率降低达一个数量级，对于较小晶格常数（<1 μm）实验结果与相干理论模拟一致，但大晶格常数（>1 μm）下两者出现显著偏差。

Conclusion: 铝柱阵列声子晶体可实现热导率的相干控制，但大晶格常数下铝柱表面粗糙度引起的扩散散射（diffusive scattering）破坏了相干性，导致相干理论失效，表明表面粗糙度在热输运中起关键作用。

Abstract: Two-dimensional phononic crystals (PnCs) formed by a periodic array of holes in a suspended membrane have previously been used to coherently control thermal conductance at low temperatures by modifying the phonon dispersion, thereby altering the phonon group velocities and the density of states. Here, in contrast, we demonstrate that PnCs formed by a periodic array of Al pillars on an uncut \SiN membrane can also be used to achieve similar coherent control. We have measured and simulated the thermal conductance of four pillar-based PnCs with different lattice constants ranging from 0.3 to 5 $μ$m at sub-Kelvin temperatures, showing a strong up to an order of magnitude reduction in thermal conductance compared to an unaltered membrane. For the larger lattice constants $> 1 $ $μ$m, however, the experiments do not agree with the coherent theory simulations, which we interpret as a breakdown of coherence induced by increasingly effective diffusive scattering due to the roughness of the Al pillar surfaces.

### [30] [Emergent topological phase from a one-dimensional network of defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13532)
*Rahul Singh,Ritajit Kundu,Arijit Kundu,Adhip Agarwala*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出通过周期性调制缺陷阵列在金属平台上实现涌现拓扑相，构建了Su-Schrieffer-Heeger网络模型，展示了可通过缺陷强度调控的拓扑性质及其输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索不同于传统原子哈密顿量工程的新途径，通过缺陷工程在金属平台上实现涌现拓扑量子物态。对称性保护拓扑相通常具有非平凡能带拓扑和边界现象，但需要光谱带隙。

Method: 采用散射矩阵网络模型捕捉涌现对称性和准能带的非平凡绕数，构建了Su-Schrieffer-Heeger网络。通过嵌入缺陷超晶格的微观晶格模型产生布洛赫微带，直接映射到网络问题。

Result: 散射态通过周期性调制缺陷阵列可产生涌现拓扑相，其性质可通过调制缺陷强度调控。该物理现象对无序具有稳定性，并可进一步通过周期驱动实现鲁棒的Thouless电荷泵。

Conclusion: 缺陷工程在金属平台上可导致涌现拓扑量子物态，这为拓扑相的实现提供了不同于原子哈密顿量工程的新途径。研究指出了可在固态实验平台中实现的具体方案。

Abstract: Symmetry-protected topological phases of matter, characterized by non-trivial band topology, are spectrally gapped and show non-trivial boundary phenomena. Here, we show that scattering states when interjected by an array of periodically modulated defects can result in emergent topological phases whose properties can be tuned by modulating the defect strengths. We dub this the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger network. We show that a scattering-matrix network model can capture the emergent symmetries and nontrivial winding of the quasienergy bands, which lead to distinct transport signatures and can be further periodically driven to realize a robust Thouless charge pump. We show that a microscopic lattice model embedded with a defect superlattice yields Bloch minibands that directly map to the network problem. We further verify that the physics we report is stable to disorder and point out concrete experimental solid-state platforms where it is readily realizable. Our work, in contrast to engineering atomic Hamiltonians, shows that defect engineering on metallic platforms can lead to emergent topological phases of quantum matter.

</details>


### [31] [Exciton screening in C$_{60}$ and PTCDA complexes. TDDFT calculations with GGA and hybrid functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13661)
*N. L. Matsko,Mahmoud A. Salem*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究采用线性响应含时密度泛函理论（TDDFT）分析C$_{60}$和PTCDA分子复合物的低能区光吸收，重点考察不同交换关联泛函对激子能量计算精度随电子-空穴分离距离的变化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估不同交换关联泛函在计算分子复合物光吸收性质时的准确性，特别关注电荷转移（CT）激子的计算精度问题，为选择合适的泛函提供理论依据。

Method: 采用线性响应含时密度泛函理论（linear response TDDFT）研究C$_{60}$和PTCDA分子复合物的低能区光吸收，对比分析了PBE、B3LYP和HSE三种交换关联（xc）泛函的计算性能。

Result: 混合泛函（hybrid functionals）通过引入非局域交换提高了短程激子的计算精度，但对长程激子的计算精度显著下降；当激子半径接近"屏蔽长度"时，较简单的PBE泛函反而比混合泛函给出更准确的激子能量。

Conclusion: 混合泛函在计算短程激子时具有优势，但对于长程激子和接近屏蔽长度的体系，简单的PBE泛函可能更为准确，这为不同尺度激子体系的计算方法选择提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Photoabsorption in the low-energy region for C$_{60}$ and PTCDA molecular complexes is studied within linear response TDDFT. For the PBE, B3LYP and HSE exchange-correlation (xc) functionals the dependence of the accuracy of the exciton energy on the electron-hole separation is analyzed. Particular attention is paid to the charge-transfer (CT) excitons. The inclusion of non-local exchange using hybrid functionals increases the accuracy of calculations for short-range excitons, however, the accuracy of hybrid functionals decreases significantly for long-range excitons. Moreover, as the exciton radius approaches the "screening length"\ , the simpler PBE functional gives more accurate excitonic energies than the mentioned hybrid functionals.

Our model achieves an overall offline tuning success of 80.0% in locating the single-charge regime, with peak performance exceeding 88% for some designs. We analyze dominant failure modes and propose targeted mitigations. Finally, wide-range diagram segmentation also naturally enables scalable physic-based feature extraction that can feed back to fabrication and design workflows and outline a roadmap for real-time integration in a cryogenic wafer prober. ### [33] [Charge waves and dynamical signatures of topological phases in Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13682)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究分析了一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger拓扑链中电荷波出现的普遍条件，探讨了任意振荡周期的一般情况。特别关注了SSH晶胞内不等价原子情况下的亚晶格振荡，并研究了淬火后非平衡动力学中局域态密度和电荷占据的时间演化。

Result: 研究发现电荷波沿链传播不依赖于其拓扑结构，但在边界处两种拓扑相表现出本质差异。在SSH晶胞内不等价原子情况下，观察到与奇偶电荷振荡同时出现的规则长周期亚晶格振荡。淬火后，局域态密度和电荷占据的时间演化显示出区分拓扑平凡与非平凡相的清晰动态指纹。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of charge waves and their temporal dynamics in one-dimensional Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) topological chains. Contrary to the conventional view that charge oscillations are suppressed in gapped topological systems with preserved chiral symmetry, we show that such oscillations can indeed occur. The general condition for an arbitrary oscillation period is analysed, and we find that the charge waves propagating along the chain do not depend on its topology, except at the edges, where both topological phases exhibit essential differences. In chains with inequivalent atoms within the SSH unit cell, we observe regular long-period sublattice oscillations that appear simultaneously with even-odd charge oscillations. Furthermore, we study the nonequilibrium dynamics in SSH chains. After a quench, the time evolution of the local density of states and charge occupancies exhibits clear dynamical fingerprints that distinguish topologically trivial and nontrivial phases. Our results establish that transient charge dynamics can distinguish topologically trivial and nontrivial phases in real time by detecting the presence of topologically-protected edge states.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非线性光学基于宏观对称性论证，对角动量转移的微观起源缺乏深入理解。研究旨在揭示角动量守恒与电子量子几何之间的直接联系，扩展对非线性光学的理解。

Method: 通过理论证明光向晶体转移的角动量与光学共振处的局域贝里曲率（local Berry curvature）成正比，这一关系编码在非线性谐波圆二色性（nonlinear harmonic circular dichroism）中。在原子薄层半导体中进行实验测量验证该理论关系。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了对非线性光学的理解，建立了角动量守恒与电子量子几何的直接联系，并为局域贝里曲率的全光学控制和读取提供了一种新方法。

Abstract: Light-matter interactions are governed by conservation laws of energy and momentum. For harmonic generation in crystalline solids, energy conservation imposes that $m$ incoming photons with energy $\hbar ω_0$ are combined to form one photon at energy $m\hbar ω_0$. Linear momentum conservation governs phase matching, whereas angular momentum conservation connects the angular momentum carried by photons to the discrete rotational symmetry of the crystal lattice. As a consequence, circular harmonic generation exerts a torque on the lattice and, conversely, a macroscopic rotation of the crystal induces a nonlinear rotational Doppler shift. These cornerstone laws of nonlinear optics rely on macroscopic symmetry arguments, and therefore provide little insight into the microscopic origin of angular momentum transfer. Here we uncover a direct connection between angular momentum conservation in nonlinear optics and the electronic quantum geometry, by proving that the transferred angular momentum from light to the crystal is proportional to the local Berry curvature at one optical resonance. This relation is encoded in the nonlinear harmonic circular dichroism, which we measure experimentally in an atomically thin semiconductor. With this, we extend our understanding of nonlinear optics, and we establish a method for the all-optical control and read-out of the local Berry curvature.

However, existing minimal treatments often oversimplify the mesoscopic hybrid region. We perform a full microscopic treatment of this hybrid segment, capturing the quasiparticle continuum and spin-split Andreev bound states (ABSs), and show that it fundamentally alters the minimal picture. We derive analytical expressions for the renormalized couplings and sweet-spot conditions, establishing a direct link between microscopic chain parameters and Majorana optimization and identifying experimentally relevant regimes for improved device performance. Critically, we find that parity-crossings of the ABS, marking the onset of an odd-parity spin-polarized regime in the segment, identify the optimal operating windows where MZMs are simultaneously well localized with a large gap to excited states.

</details>


### [40] [Thermodynamic signatures of non-Hermiticity in Dirac materials via quantum capacitance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14150)
*Juan Pablo Esparza,Francisco J. Peña,Patricio Vargas,Vladimir Juričić*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过量子电容（quantum capacitance）探测狄拉克材料（Dirac materials）中非厄米（non-Hermitian）奇异点（exceptional point）物理的新平衡态方法，揭示了热力学态密度和量子电容在弱非厄米区域对奇异点的普适趋近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前非厄米能带描述的实验验证主要依赖波基或动力学探针，缺乏平衡态探测途径。本文旨在建立狄拉克材料中奇异点物理的新平衡态探测方法，通过热力学可观测量为非厄米物理提供实验验证途径。

Method: 采用最小非互易石墨烯模型（minimal non-reciprocal graphene model），研究弱非厄米区域（weakly non-Hermitian regime）中热力学态密度（thermodynamic density of states）和量子电容的普适行为。分析中考虑了跳跃不平衡（hopping imbalance）对狄拉克速度（Dirac velocity）的影响，并探讨了磁场中朗道能级（Landau-level）的行为。

Result: 在弱非厄米区域，低能态密度、热力学态密度和量子电容均按$(1-β^2)^{-1}$标度发散。在电荷中性点，量子电容保持温度线性关系但系数发散，而逆响应在趋近奇异点时线性软化。磁场中表现为朗道能级间距塌缩和热激活能级聚集。双正交布洛赫态（biorthogonal Bloch states）的佩特曼因子（Petermann factor）$K=(1-β^2)^{-1}$分离了本征矢量非正交性的不可约非厄米效应。

Conclusion: 量子电容可作为狄拉克材料中有效非厄米性的实验可及体平衡态探针，为探测奇异点物理提供了新的平衡态途径。该研究建立了热力学可观测量与不可约非厄米效应之间的直接联系。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian band descriptions capture how loss, gain, and environmental coupling reshape quantum matter, yet most experimental tests rely on wave-based or dynamical probes. Here we establish a new equilibrium route to exceptional physics in Dirac materials: in the weakly non-Hermitian regime, the thermodynamic density of states and the quantum capacitance exhibit a universal equilibrium approach to the exceptional point. In our minimal non-reciprocal graphene model, the hopping imbalance reduces the Dirac velocity as $v_F=v\sqrt{1-β^2}$, implying that the low-energy density of states, the thermodynamic density of states, and the quantum capacitance all scale as $(1-β^2)^{-1}$ as $|β|\to 1^-$. Consequently, at charge neutrality the quantum capacitance remains linear in temperature but with a diverging prefactor, while the inverse response softens linearly on approaching the exceptional point. In a magnetic field, this manifests as a collapse of the Landau-level spacing and a corresponding crowding of thermally active levels. Complementarily, the biorthogonal Bloch states exhibit a Petermann factor $K=(1-β^2)^{-1}$, which isolates the irreducibly non-Hermitian effect of eigenvector non-orthogonality. These results identify quantum capacitance as an experimentally accessible bulk equilibrium probe of effective non-Hermiticity in Dirac materials.

</details>

### [41] [Proposal for the first measurement of antiproton polarization in proton-nucleus interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13231)
*D. Alfs,D. Grzonka,G. Khatri,P. Kulessa,J. Ritman,T. Sefzick,J. Smyrski,V. Verhoeven,H. Xu,M. Zielinski*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在未极化质子-原子核碰撞中产生的反质子是否可能获得横向极化，并评估了通过弹性散射中的左右不对称性进行首次专门测量的实验可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管包容性强子产生中的自旋相关现象已被广泛研究，但其微观起源和在不同强子间的普适性仍未完全理解。特别是，目前尚不清楚在未极化强子碰撞中产生的反质子是否会因自旋相关的反质子-核子相互作用和非微扰强子化机制而获得横向极化。

Method: 通过弹性反质子-质子散射在库仑核干涉区域的左右不对称性来获取极化信息。基于欧洲核子研究中心（CERN）拟议实验装置的详细蒙特卡洛模拟，评估了检测特定极化程度所需的统计灵敏度。

Result: 研究估计了检测反质子横向极化所需的统计灵敏度，为首次专门测量提供了实验可行性评估。这种测量将为反核子-核子相互作用的旋结构提供新的经验约束。

Conclusion: 确定这种效应的存在与否将为反核子-核子相互作用的旋结构提供新的经验约束，而现有数据对此仅有微弱约束。该研究为首次专门测量反质子横向极化的实验可行性提供了评估框架。

Abstract: Spin dependent phenomena in inclusive hadron production have been extensively investigated, yet their microscopic origin and universality across different hadrons are still not fully understood. In particular, it is presently unknown whether antiprotons produced in unpolarized hadronic collisions can acquire a transverse polarization as a result of spin dependent $\bar{p}N$ interactions and nonperturbative hadronization mechanisms. Establishing the presence or absence of such an effect would provide new empirical constraints on the spin structure of the antinucleon-nucleon interaction, which is only weakly constrained by existing data. In this work, we investigate the experimental feasibility of a first dedicated measurement of the transverse polarization of antiprotons produced in proton-nucleus collisions. The polarization is accessed through the left-right asymmetry in elastic $\bar{p}p$ scattering in the Coulomb Nuclear Interference region. Based on detailed Monte Carlo simulations of the proposed experimental setup at the European Organization for Nuclear Research (CERN), we estimate the statistical sensitivity required to detect a certain degree of polarization.

Abstract: The BM@N experiment (Baryonic Matter at the Nuclotron) is the first fixed-target experiment at the JINR NICA accelerator complex. ### [43] [Highly boosted dielectron identification in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13320)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 开发了一种新方法来识别洛伦兹增强因子γ_L > 20的电子对，这些电子对在CMS探测器的电磁量能器中产生单个合并簇。该方法使用两个多变量模型：一个用于双径迹重建情况，另一个用于单径迹重建情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要识别高洛伦兹增强（Lorentz boost）的电子对，这些电子对在电磁量能器中产生单个合并簇，传统方法难以有效识别此类信号。

Method: 开发了两个多变量模型（multivariate models）：一个用于双径迹重建情况，另一个用于单径迹重建情况。使用质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量13 TeV）确定效率，并开发了专用的能量校正方法。

Result: 双径迹模型的整体效率为80%（使用增强J/ψ介子衰变估计），单径迹模型的效率约为60%（使用Z → μ^+μ^-γ事件估计）。同时开发了基于B^± → J/ψK^± → e^+e^-K^±数据的专用能量校正。

Conclusion: 成功开发了识别高洛伦兹增强电子对的新技术，能够有效处理电磁量能器中产生单个合并簇的情况，为相关物理分析提供了重要工具。

Abstract: A new technique is developed to identify dielectrons (e$^+$e$^-$) with Lorentz boost $γ_\mathrm{L}$ $\gt$ 20 that produce one single merged cluster in the electromagnetic calorimeter of the CMS detector. The identification uses two multivariate models: one for the case where both electron tracks are reconstructed, and another where only one of the tracks is reconstructed. The efficiency is determined using proton-proton collision data collected at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV. Boosted J/$ψ$ mesons decaying into e$^+$e$^-$ pairs are used to estimate the efficiency of the model with two tracks, yielding an overall efficiency of 80%. The Z $\to$ $μ^+μ^-γ$ events, where the photon converts into a collimated dielectron, are used for the model with a single track, yielding an efficiency of about 60%. A dedicated energy correction for dielectron candidates is also developed using B$^\pm$ $\to$ J/$ψ$K$^\pm$ $\to$ e$^+$e$^-$K$^\pm$ data.

</details>


### [44] [Enhancing Event Reconstruction in Hyper-Kamiokande with Machine Learning: A ResNet Implementation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13503)
*Andrew Atta,Nick Prouse,Shuoyu Chen,Kimihiro Okumura,Patrick de Perio,Eric Thrane,Phillip Urquijo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于神经网络的粒子事件重建方法，用于即将进行的Hyper-Kamiokande实验。该方法在保持与传统最大似然重建相当性能的同时，将每事件推理时间缩短至1-2毫秒，实现了3.2万至5.2万倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hyper-Kamiokande实验需要比以往实验更大的蒙特卡洛数据集以满足严格的系统不确定性要求。传统最大似然重建虽然提供高质量结果，但其每事件计算成本使得处理这些大型样本越来越不切实际。

Method: 使用模拟数据开发神经网络重建方法，将PMT电荷和时序信息映射为190×189双通道图像，作为WatChMaL框架中ResNet模型的输入。这些模型执行粒子分类（e、μ、γ、π⁰）和回归任务（顶点、方向、动量）。

Result: 回归模型在完整运动学范围内平均动量分辨率为1.35%（μ子）和2.39%（电子），角度分辨率为1.25°和1.94°，顶点分辨率为28.2厘米和25.4厘米。分类器改善了e-μ、e-γ和e-π⁰分离，ROC曲线下面积分别为0.9999992、0.633和0.9526。

Conclusion: 神经网络在单个GPU上实现每事件1-2毫秒的推理时间，相对于基于似然的重建实现了3.2×10⁴至5.2×10⁴倍的加速，证明了深度学习作为Hyper-Kamiokande事件重建可扩展替代方案的潜力。

Abstract: The forthcoming Hyper-Kamiokande experiment requires substantially larger Monte Carlo datasets than previous experiments to satisfy stringent systematic-uncertainty requirements. While traditional maximum-likelihood reconstruction provides high-quality results, its per-event computational cost makes processing these large samples increasingly impractical. We demonstrate a neural-network-based reconstruction approach for the Hyper-Kamiokande far detector using simulated data. Single-particle events with kinetic energies from the Cherenkov threshold up to 2 GeV are propagated through the detector, with PMT charge and timing information mapped to $190\times189$ two-channel images serving as inputs to ResNet models in the WatChMaL framework. These models (i) classify events into four particle hypotheses ($e$, $μ$, $γ$, $π^{0}$) and (ii) regress the vertex, direction, and momentum of electrons and muons. Averaged over the full kinematic range, the regression models achieve momentum resolutions of $1.35\%$ and $2.39\%$, angular resolutions of $1.25^\circ$ and $1.94^\circ$, and vertex resolutions of $28.2$ cm and $25.4$ cm, for muons and electrons respectively, broadly consistent with traditional methods. The classifier improves $e$-$μ$, $e$-$γ$, and $e$-$π^{0}$ separation, with ROC curve areas of $0.9999992$, $0.633$, and $0.9526$. Crucially, our networks achieve inference times of 1-2 ms per event on a single GPU, yielding speed-ups of $3.2\times10^{4}$-$5.2\times10^{4}$ relative to likelihood-based reconstruction, highlighting deep learning as a scalable alternative for Hyper-Kamiokande event reconstruction.

</details>

Abstract: The lowest lying charmonium system $η_c$ has been observed for more than four decades. Studies of its production and decay properties provide an unique platform to investigate the inner structure of charmonium systems, hence improve our understanding of strong interaction in the charm sector. BESIII detector at the $e^+e^-$ BEPCII collider has already collected the world largest $J/ψ$ and $ψ(3686)$ data sets, based on which massive $η_c$ samples are produced via radiative transitions.   <summary>Details</summary>
