### [47] [Phase transition in compressed sensing using log-sum penalty and adaptive smoothing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13511)
*Keisuke Morita,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi,Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在近似消息传递框架中采用自适应平滑策略的方法，用于解决稀疏信号恢复问题。该方法相比ℓ₁范数最小化能在更广区域实现精确恢复，但亚稳态限制了其达到信息论极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多实际问题中，从欠定线性系统恢复稀疏信号仍是一个基本挑战。虽然ℓ₁范数最小化被广泛使用，但其存在估计偏差，无法达到贝叶斯最优重建极限。非凸替代方法如对数求和惩罚虽能促进更强稀疏性，但算法稳定性难以保持。

Method: 为解决算法稳定性挑战，本文在近似消息传递（approximate message passing）框架中引入了自适应平滑策略。同时，使用副本方法（replica method）和状态演化（state evolution）评估了高斯测量矩阵的典型精确恢复阈值。

Result: 结果表明，自适应方法相比ℓ₁范数最小化能在更广区域实现精确恢复。然而，亚稳态（metastable states）阻碍了该方法达到信息论极限（information-theoretic limit）。

Conclusion: 自适应平滑策略在近似消息传递框架中能有效缓解算法不稳定性，扩展了精确恢复区域，但亚稳态的存在限制了其达到理论最优性能。

Abstract: In many real-world problems, recovering sparse signals from underdetermined linear systems remains a fundamental challenge. Although $\ell_1$ norm minimization is widely used, it suffers from estimation bias that prevents it from reaching the Bayes-optimal reconstruction limit. Nonconvex alternatives, such as the log-sum penalty, have been proposed to promote stronger sparsity. However, maintaining their algorithmic stability is challenging. To address this challenge, we introduce an adaptive smoothing strategy within an approximate message passing framework to mitigate algorithmic instability. Furthermore, we evaluate the typical exact-recovery threshold for Gaussian measurement matrices using the replica method and state evolution. The results indicate that the adaptive method achieves exact recovery over a broader region than $\ell_1$ norm minimization, although metastable states hinder reaching the information-theoretic limit.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多种模型依赖和模型无关方法表明，原初标量功率谱中的特定局域特征能显著改善对宇宙微波背景观测各向异性的拟合。本研究旨在检验这些特征是否能在单一场、正则标量场驱动的暴胀场景中生成。

Method: 采用缓慢滚动的基准模型，通过修改第一慢滚参数的功能形式在功率谱中生成所需特征。基于遗传算法构建机器学习流程，系统重构与数据一致的原初标量功率谱特征。

Result: 应用该方法于普朗克2018年CMB数据，重构特征使角功率谱拟合度改善Δχ²≲-10。遗传算法还识别出其他背景参数和原初特征组合，提供相似水平的拟合改善。

Abstract: [Abridged] A variety of model-dependent as well as model-independent approaches suggest that certain localized features in the primordial scalar power spectrum can lead to a significantly better fit to the observed anisotropies in the cosmic microwave background (CMB). In this work, we focus on three types of such features and examine whether these features can be generated in inflationary scenarios driven by a single, canonical scalar field. We consider a slowly rolling baseline model that is described by a specific time-dependence of the first slow roll parameter and we generate the desired features in the power spectrum through suitable modifications to the functional form of the slow roll parameter. To systematically reconstruct the desired features in the scalar power spectrum (or, equivalently, the modifications in the behavior of the first slow roll parameter) that are consistent with the data, we implement a machine learning pipeline based on the genetic algorithm (GA). Assuming the standard values for the background $Λ$CDM model (arrived at for a nearly scale-invariant primordial scalar power spectrum), we apply our method to the Planck 2018 CMB data, and show that the reconstructed features improve the fit to the observed angular power spectra by $Δχ^2 \lesssim -10$. Moreover, we find that GA points to other sets of background parameters and primordial features, which lead to a similar level of improvement in the fit to the data. Such alternative sets of background parameters and scalar power spectra offer possible pathways to alleviate existing cosmological tensions. Our approach provides effective single-field inflationary dynamics to generate features that are supported by the data.

Method: 研究采用多场模型（特别是两场模型）分析类轴子早期暗能量（EDE），通过对比单场与多场模型对高角动量（high-ℓ）CMB数据的拟合程度，评估模型对复合前历史（pre-recombination history）的修改效果。

Conclusion: 多场模型（特别是两场模型）能有效缓解CMB数据对早期暗能量（EDE）的约束，改善与H₀张力的兼容性，但超过两个场并无额外收益，且单场模型在高角动量区域最受排斥的问题得到缓解。

Abstract: We show that the strong constraints placed by Planck NPIPE Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data on axion-like early dark energy (EDE) are significantly alleviated in models with multiple fields. We find a $1.5σ$ residual tension with the Local Distance Network value of $H_0$ in a 2-field model, with no improvement beyond two fields, and a best-fit value of $H_0$ $\sim 1.4σ$ larger than in the 1-field case. The second field improves the fit to high-$\ell$ CMB data, where 1-field EDE is most strongly disfavored, and suggests modifications to the pre-recombination history over a wider redshift range.

### [50] [Dark energy, spatial curvature, and star formation efficiency from JWST photometric and spectroscopic high-redshift galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13866)
*Leonardo Comini,Sunny Vagnozzi,Abraham Loeb*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过贝叶斯分析JWST观测到的早期大质量星系，探讨其成因是超出ΛCDM的新物理还是恒星形成效率增强。结果表明问题更可能源于星系形成天体物理学而非宇宙学参数变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（James Webb Space Telescope, JWST）早期观测发现高红移大质量星系数量异常，这引发了一个关键问题：这一现象是否指向ΛCDM模型之外的新物理，还是反映了大质量恒星形成效率的增强。

Method: 研究采用全贝叶斯分析（full Bayesian analysis）方法，对CEERS成像和FRESCO光谱样本中最极端的星系进行分析。该方法联合约束宇宙学参数和重子到恒星的转换效率ε，不仅考虑平坦ΛCDM模型，还允许暗能量状态方程w和空间曲率参数Ω_K变化。

Result: 在平坦ΛCDM模型中，CEERS样本给出ε≳0.07的弱2σ下限，符合天体物理预期；而FRESCO样本要求ε≳0.5，ε≲0.2的值被>5σ排除。当允许w和Ω_K变化时，结果未发生质变，且未发现偏离w=-1或Ω_K=0的证据。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明"JWST张力（JWST tension）"的起源不太可能是宇宙学性质的，而更可能存在于星系形成的天体物理学中。分析未发现暗能量状态方程或空间曲率偏离标准值的证据。

Abstract: Early observations from the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) have revealed an overabundance of massive high-redshift galaxies, raising the question of whether this points to new physics beyond $Λ$CDM, or an enhanced formation efficiency of massive stars. We revisit this issue going beyond earlier analyses based on direct comparisons to theoretical bounds at a fixed cosmology, by performing a full Bayesian analysis of the most extreme galaxies in the CEERS imaging and FRESCO spectroscopic samples, jointly constraining cosmological parameters and the baryon-to-star conversion efficiency $ε$. We do so not only within the spatially flat $Λ$CDM model, but also in models where the dark energy equation of state $w$ and/or the spatial curvature parameter $Ω_K$ are allowed to vary, carefully discussing the impact of both $w$ and $Ω_K$ on the cumulative comoving stellar mass density. Within the flat $Λ$CDM model, once cosmological parameters are marginalized over, the CEERS sample provides a weak $2σ$ lower limit of $ε\gtrsim 0.07$, compatible with astrophysical expectations. In contrast, the FRESCO sample requires $ε\gtrsim 0.5$ at $2σ$, with values $ε\lesssim 0.2$ disfavored at $>5σ$. These results do not qualitatively change when we allow $w$ and/or $Ω_K$ to vary, with no evidence for deviations from $w=-1$ or $Ω_K=0$. Our results therefore suggest that the origin of the ``JWST tension'' is unlikely to be cosmological, but lies in the astrophysics of galaxy formation.

### [51] [Observability from measurable sets for strongly coupled parabolic systems via single-component observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13599)
*Xiaoyu Fu,Gengsheng Wang,Huaiqiang Yu,Xiaomin Zhu*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对一类强耦合双方程抛物系统，建立了从时空可测集出发的可观性不等式，其中观测仅作用于单个分量。通过发展基于Remez型不等式的积分型插值可观性估计，克服了强耦合系统特有的高频振荡抵消问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决强耦合抛物系统从可测集出发的可观性问题。模型受到具有复系数抛物方程的启发，作为强耦合系统的典型示例，其核心挑战在于观测分量可能因耦合而产生高频振荡抵消，导致逐点时间插值可观性估计失效。

Method: 作者发展了一种基于Remez型不等式的积分型插值可观性不等式（integral-type interpolation observability inequality）。结合Phung-Wang（2013）和Apraiz-Escauriaza-Wang-Zhang（2014）提出的从可测集推导可观性的策略，建立了完整的理论框架。

Result: 成功获得了从时空可测集出发的期望可观性不等式（desired observability inequality）。该方法有效克服了强耦合系统中观测分量可能产生的高频振荡抵消问题，解决了逐点时间插值估计失效的困难。

Conclusion: 通过发展积分型插值可观性不等式，本文成功解决了强耦合抛物系统从可测集出发的可观性问题。该方法为处理具有复杂耦合结构的系统提供了新的理论工具，克服了传统逐点估计在高频振荡情况下的局限性。

Abstract: We establish an observability inequality from space-time measurable sets for a class of strongly coupled parabolic systems consisting of two equations, where the observation acts on a single-component. The model is motivated by parabolic equations with complex coefficients and serves as a prototypical example of strongly coupled systems. The main difficulty lies in the fact that, unlike in the scalar and weakly coupled cases, pointwise-in-time interpolation observability estimates fail, as the observed component may exhibit high-frequency oscillatory cancellations induced by the coupling. To overcome this difficulty, we develop a new integral-type interpolation observability inequality based on a Remez-type inequality. With the aid of this integral-type interpolation observability inequality and the strategy developed in [Phung and Wang, JEMS, (2013), 681--703] and [Apraiz, Escauriaza,Wang and Zhang, JEMS, (2014), 2433--2475] for deriving observability from measurable sets, we obtain the desired observability inequality.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究采用非平衡动力学视角，通过快速淬灭（rapid quench）跨越临界点，研究全息超流模型（holographic superfluid model）的演化过程。

Result: 研究发现拓扑缺陷（topological defects）诱导的入侵现象在超临界区域持续存在，入侵速度随淬灭终点ρ_f变化存在明显转折点。该转折点定义了一条新的非平衡超临界交叉线（nonequilibrium supercritical crossover line）。

Conclusion: 与经典的维德姆线（Widom line）或弗伦克尔线（Frenkel line）不同，这条新的交叉线同时编码热力学信息和动力学信息，反映了非平衡条件下超临界区域的动力学本质。该研究为表征超临界亚相提供了一种新颖的非平衡动力学方法。

Abstract: Distinguishing different subphases in the supercritical region is a fundamental issue in statistical physics and condensed matter physics. Traditional approaches mainly rely on static thermodynamic response functions or equilibrium correlation functions, which are inherently confined to quasi-static processes. In this work, we adopt a nonequilibrium dynamical perspective to investigate the evolution of a holographic superfluid model following a rapid quench across the critical point. We find that the invasion phenomenon induced by topological defects persists in the supercritical region, and the invasion velocity exhibits a clear turning point as a function of the quench endpoint $ρ_f$. This turning point defines a new nonequilibrium supercritical crossover line. In contrast to the classical Widom line or Frenkel line, this new crossover line encodes both thermodynamic information and kinetic information, reflecting the dynamical nature of the supercritical region under nonequilibrium conditions. This study provides a novel nonequilibrium dynamical approach for characterizing supercritical subphases.

### [53] [Thermodynamic conditions ensure the stability of third-order extended heat conduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13110)
*Peter Ván,Réka Somogyfoki*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对Somogyfoki等人（2025）的研究结论——第二定律（Second Law）在最一般情况下不能保证稳定性，本文旨在证明该结论源于过于保守的证明策略，并重新确认热力学作为稳定性理论的基本作用。

Method: 通过分析色散多项式（dispersion polynomial）的系数结构，证明所有物理波数下系数保持正定，因为其结构阻止正实根的出现。同时与Giorgi等人的速率方程方法（rate-equation approach）进行比较。

Result: 标准热力学条件（熵凹性和非负熵产，由原论文的2×2块正定不等式表达）确实足以保证线性稳定性。这一结果确认了热力学作为稳定性理论在所有热力学一致的三阶扩展热传导理论中确保基本动态稳定性。

Conclusion: 热力学作为稳定性理论，能够确保所有热力学一致的三阶扩展热传导理论的基本动态稳定性，从而纠正了先前研究中关于第二定律不能保证稳定性的错误结论。

Abstract: In a recent work, Somogyfoki et al. (J. Non-Equilib. Thermodyn. 50, 59-76, 2025) analysed the linear stability of homogeneous equilibrium in third-order non-Fourier heat conduction within the framework of non-equilibrium thermodynamics with internal variables. They identified a stability condition, their equation (49), which could not be derived from the standard thermodynamic inequalities for the 2X2 conductivity blocks, and concluded that the Second Law does not guarantee stability in the most general case. Here we show that this conclusion was due to an overly conservative proof strategy: the standard thermodynamic conditions (concave entropy and non-negative entropy production, as expressed by the $2\times2$ block positive-definiteness inequalities (19)-(20) of the original paper) do suffice for linear stability. The key observation is that all coefficients of the dispersion polynomial remain positive for all physical wave numbers because their structure prevents positive real roots. This result confirms that thermodynamics, understood as a stability theory, ensures fundamental dynamic stability in all thermodynamically consistent third-order extended heat conduction theories. A comparison with the rate-equation approach of Giorgi, Morro and Zullo (Meccanica 59, 1757-1776, 2024) is also presented.

### [54] [Genuine quantum scars in Floquet chaotic many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13164)
*Harald Schmid,Andrea Pizzi,Johannes Knolle*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Floquet多体系统中不稳定周期轨道（unstable periodic orbits）引发的量子疤痕（quantum scarring）行为，揭示了驱动频率对疤痕稳定性的调控作用，并发现了静态系统所没有的驱动诱导疤痕态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子疤痕（quantum scarring）基于不稳定周期轨道（unstable periodic orbits），在静态多体系统中已有研究，但其在周期性驱动（periodic driving）下的命运尚不清楚。挑战在于这类系统通常预期会加热到无限温度（infinite temperature），因此需要探究真实疤痕（genuine scarring）如何与驱动竞争。

Method: 使用混沌自旋链（chaotic spin chains）作为研究平台，分析Floquet多体系统（Floquet many-body system）。通过经典李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）分析来理解疤痕行为的动力学稳定性，特别关注高频率极限（high-frequency limit）和中间频率区域（intermediate-frequency regimes）。

Result: 在高频率极限下，Floquet态仍保持疤痕特征；此外发现了静态系统所没有的驱动诱导Floquet疤痕（driving-induced Floquet scars）。构建了丰富的动力学稳定性相图（dynamical stability diagram），显示中间频率区域存在疤痕增强（enhanced scarring）和淬灭（quenched scarring）的不同机制。

Conclusion: Floquet系统为调控量子多体系统的疤痕行为提供了天然平台，不仅保留了静态对应关系，还产生了新的驱动诱导疤痕态，扩展了量子疤痕现象的研究范畴。

Abstract: Unstable periodic orbits act as organizing structures for classical chaotic systems and underpin quantum scarring. Long known in single-particle systems, genuine quantum scars based on unstable periodic orbits have been recently extended to isolated many-body systems for time-independent Hamiltonians. Their fate under periodic driving, however, remains largely uncharted, challenged by the expectation that these systems should in general heat to infinite temperature. Here, we investigate how genuine scarring competes with the drive in a Floquet many-body system. Using chaotic spin chains, we demonstrate that Floquet states remain scarred in the high-frequency limit. Beyond this static correspondence, we uncover additional, driving-induced Floquet scars with no static analog. We construct a rich dynamical stability diagram with intermediate-frequency regimes of enhanced and quenched scarring, which we understand with a classical analysis of the Lyapunov exponent. Our results position Floquet systems as a natural platform for tuning the scarring behavior of quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [55] [Global Oscillations in Depinning Models with Aging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13222)
*F. V. Pereyra Aponte,E. A. Jagla*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种扩展标准脱钉（depinning）范式的新模型，通过引入老化机制到局部钉扎力中，导致系统在强钉扎的"卡住"状态和弱钉扎的"滑动"状态之间振荡。研究发现平均场相互作用会产生"王者雪崩"和全局振荡的粘滑应力状态，而二维短程相互作用系统则表现出持续全局应力振荡但无系统尺度雪崩的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法包括：1）提出扩展的脱钉模型，在局部钉扎力中引入老化机制；2）分析平均场相互作用情况下的系统行为；3）构建平均场情况下的相图；4）研究二维系统中短程相互作用的影响。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）平均场相互作用下出现"王者雪崩（king avalanches）"和全局振荡的粘滑应力状态；2）相图识别出平滑动力学、纯粘滑和双稳态区域；3）二维短程相互作用系统中全局应力振荡持续存在，但无系统尺度雪崩，而是出现与应力振荡相关的交替雪崩活动区间。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入老化机制扩展了标准脱钉范式，揭示了平均场和短程相互作用系统中不同的动力学行为。关键发现是全局应力振荡在两种情况下均持续存在，但雪崩特征存在显著差异：平均场系统产生系统尺度雪崩，而二维短程系统则表现为与应力振荡相关的交替雪崩活动。

Abstract: We propose a model that extends the standard depinning paradigm by incorporating an aging mechanism into the local pinning force. This favors oscillations between a stuck state of large pinning, and a slipping state of smaller pinning. We show that for mean field interactions between sites this mechanism can lead to the appearance of ``king avalanches" and global instabilities, producing a global oscillatory stick-slip stress regime. We construct the phase diagram for this mean field case and identify regions of smooth dynamics, pure stick-slip, and bistability. Crucially, when considering two-dimensional systems with short-range interactions we find that states of global stress oscillation persist, but in contrast to the mean field case, no system-size avalanches appear. Instead, we observe alternating temporal intervals of larger and lower avalanche activity that correlate with the stress oscillations.

</details>


### [56] [First Passage Times for Variable-Order Time-Fractional Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13852)
*Wancheng Li,Daniel S. Han*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文推导了空间依赖变阶时间分数阶扩散的首达时（FPT）分布渐近行为，发现生存概率以$Ψ(t)\sim C\,t^{-α_*}/(\ln t)^ν$形式衰减，其中$α_*$是分数阶指数的最小值，$ν$由最小值的位置和形状决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究空间依赖变阶时间分数阶扩散（space-dependent variable-order time-fractional diffusion）的首达时分布，旨在理解分数阶指数$α(x)$随位置变化时异常输运（anomalous transport）的统计特性，为实验识别空间异质异常输运提供理论预测。

Method: 推导了首达时分布的渐近表达式，针对有限域上具有吸收和反射边界的光滑$α(x)$函数，通过理论分析确定生存概率的衰减形式，并利用拉普拉斯空间精确解（Laplace-space solutions）和蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）对线性和非线性$α(x)$剖面进行验证。

Result: 证明生存概率以$Ψ(t)\sim C\,t^{-α_*}/(\ln t)^ν$形式衰减，其中$α_*$是分数阶指数的最小值，$ν$由最小值的位置和形状决定；当分数阶指数为常数时$ν=0$，该理论预测可用于实验识别空间异质异常输运。

Conclusion: 建立了空间依赖变阶时间分数阶扩散的首达时分布理论框架，揭示了生存概率衰减行为由分数阶指数最小值主导，为分析空间异质异常输运现象提供了定量工具和实验验证方法。

Abstract: We derive the asymptotic first passage time (FPT) distribution for space-dependent variable-order time-fractional diffusion, where the fractional exponent $α(x)$ varies with position. For any sufficiently smooth $α(x)$ on a finite domain with absorbing and reflecting boundaries, we show that the survival probability decays as $Ψ(t)\sim C\,t^{-α_*}/(\ln t)^ν$, where $α_*$ is the minimum value of the fractional exponent and $ν$ is determined by the location and shape of the minimum. For a constant fractional exponent $ν=0$ and this provides a theoretical prediction that can identify spatially heterogeneous anomalous transport in experiments. We validate the theory against exact Laplace-space solutions and Monte Carlo simulations for linear and nonlinear profiles of $α(x)$.

</details>


### [57] [Role of volatility mixing in wealth condensation transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13885)
*Jaeseok Hur,Meesoon Ha,Hawoong Jeong*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了网络化财富动态模型中异质性波动率的作用及其对财富凝聚转变的影响。通过引入二元波动率并控制其配置，发现局部相互作用会中和组间指数，降低总体尾指数，从而驱动凝聚转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索网络化财富动态模型中异质性波动率（heterogeneous volatility）的作用，特别是其对财富凝聚转变（wealth condensation transition）的影响。这扩展了Bouchaud-Mézard框架，关注噪声异质性在非平衡系统网络中的重要性。

Method: 方法包括扩展Bouchaud-Mézard框架，在网络中引入二元波动率（binary volatility）。使用随机块模型（stochastic block model）控制波动率组间的混合程度，研究波动率配置如何影响财富分布的有效幂律尾指数（effective power-law tail exponent）。

Result: 研究发现有效指数不仅由全局参数Λ=2J/β²决定，还受网络中波动率配置的影响。具有不同波动率的节点间的局部相互作用会引发组间指数的中和（neutralization of group-wise exponents），从而降低总体尾指数，并能在γ_c=2处驱动凝聚转变。

Conclusion: 结论表明波动率混合（volatility mixing）是财富凝聚的另一个控制机制，强调了网络中非平衡系统噪声异质性的重要性。这为理解财富分布的形成机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study the role of heterogeneous volatility in a networked wealth dynamics model and its impact on the wealth condensation transition. Extending the Bouchaud--M{é}zard framework, we introduce binary volatility in networks and investigate how its configuration affects the effective power-law tail exponent of the wealth distribution. Using a stochastic block model, we control the mixing between volatility groups and show that the effective exponent is governed not only by the global parameter $Λ=2J/β^2$ but also by the volatility configuration in the network. We find that local interactions between nodes with different volatility induce a neutralization of group-wise exponents, which lowers the aggregate tail exponent and can drive a condensation transition across $γ_{\rm c}=2$. Our results identify volatility mixing as another control mechanism for wealth condensation and highlight the importance of noise heterogeneity in nonequilibrium systems on networks.

### [58] [Specific heat of thermally driven chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14056)
*Michiel Gautama,Faezeh Khodabandehlou,Christian Maes,Ion Santra*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了耦合在不同温度热浴边界上的谐振子链的热响应，通过引入热浴温度的缓慢变化量化了过剩热流，获得了非平衡热容矩阵，并证明了长链存在明确的热力学极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在量化非平衡条件下空间扩展驱动系统的热响应特性，特别是热容等热力学量在非平衡态下的行为，为理解驱动分子的高温行为提供理论框架。

Method: 采用边界耦合在不同温度热浴的谐振子链模型，通过引入热浴温度的缓慢变化来量化过剩热流，从而计算非平衡热容矩阵，并分析系统在固定但任意温度差下的响应。

Result: 研究证明了长链存在明确的热力学极限，发现与单个热浴能量交换相关的比热（specific heat）取决于系统-热浴耦合的摩擦系数差异，这种热动力学效应（thermokinetic effect）是非平衡响应的典型特征。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在局部相互作用的空间扩展驱动系统中明确确定了比热，当热浴耦合具有温度依赖性时，比热相应继承非平凡的温度依赖性，与平衡态形成鲜明对比，可能为杜隆-珀蒂定律（Dulong-Petit law）提供自然的非平衡扩展。

Abstract: We investigate the thermal responses of a harmonic oscillator chain coupled at its boundaries to heat baths held at different temperatures. This setup sustains a steady energy flux, continuously dissipating heat into both reservoirs. By introducing slow variations in the bath temperatures, we quantify the resulting excess heat currents and thereby obtain the nonequilibrium heat capacity matrix at fixed but arbitrary temperature differences. We demonstrate the existence of a well-defined thermodynamic limit for long chains. The specific heat associated with energy exchanges with a single bath depends on the difference in friction coefficients governing the system-bath couplings. That thermokinetic effect is typical for nonequilibrium response. When the couplings with the thermal baths acquire temperature dependence, the specific heat correspondingly inherits a nontrivial temperature dependence, in sharp contrast with equilibrium. Our results provide the first explicit determination of specific heat(s) in a locally interacting, spatially extended driven system. Beyond its exact solvability, the model may offer a natural nonequilibrium extension of the Dulong-Petit law, capturing the high-temperature behavior of driven molecules.

</details>


### [59] [Quantum matter is weakly entangled at low energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14143)
*Samuel J. Garratt,Dmitry A. Abanin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究构建了具有固定能量期望值的多体量子态纠缠熵的上界，特别关注约半系统的纠缠熵。上界形式为两个虚构系统热熵之和的一半加上可能的面积律项，有效温度由能量约束确定。该框架将热力学性质与低能多体希尔伯特空间结构联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立几何局域哈密顿量下具有固定能量期望值的多体量子态的纠缠熵上界。特别关注约半系统的纠缠熵，旨在将物理热力学性质与低能多体希尔伯特空间结构联系起来。

Method: 方法是通过构造纠缠熵上界，其中冯·诺依曼纠缠熵（von Neumann entanglement entropy）上界为两个虚构系统在相同温度下的热熵之和的一半，加上某些系统中的面积律贡献。有效温度的选择使得两个虚构系统的热能与原始问题中的能量约束相匹配。

Result: 结果显示，无阻挫（frustration-free）系统的基态施密特秩（Schmidt ranks）受子系统哈密顿量的基态简并度上界限制。当子系统零温热熵按表面积而非体积标度时，基态冯·诺依曼和瑞尼纠缠熵（Rényi entanglement entropies）遵循面积律。该结果与谱隙无关，且上界在多种系统中达到最优（至亚领头阶修正）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了将热力学数据（如比热容）转化为纯态纠缠约束的框架，适用于亚广延和广延能量范围。研究结果揭示了物理热力学性质与低能多体希尔伯特空间结构之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We construct upper bounds on entanglement entropies of many-body quantum states that have fixed energy expectation values with respect to geometrically local Hamiltonians. Our focus is on entanglement entropies of subsystems that make up approximately half of the full system. The upper bound on the von Neumann entanglement entropy is half the sum of the thermal entropies of two fictitious systems at the same temperature as one another, with an additional area-law contribution in some systems. The effective temperature is chosen such that the sum of the thermal energies of the two fictitious systems matches the constraint on the energy of the state in the original problem; at subextensive energies, this temperature decreases with increasing system size. Our upper bounds on Rényi entanglement entropies take an analogous form. As a first application we show that ground-state Schmidt ranks in frustration-free (FF) systems are upper bounded by the ground-state degeneracies of Hamiltonians acting on subsystems. Ground-state von Neumann and Rényi entanglement entropies therefore follow an area law when the zero-temperature thermal entropies of subsystems scale with surface areas, rather than with subsystem volumes. This result holds independently of the spectral gap. For physical models of quantum matter, which have well-defined specific heat capacities (and are not necessarily FF), our bounds provide a way to convert this thermodynamic data into constraints on pure-state entanglement at both subextensive and extensive energies. We also show that our upper bounds on half-system entanglement entropies are optimal, up to subleading corrections, in wide varieties of systems. Our results relate physical thermodynamic properties to the structure of many-body Hilbert space at low energies.

</details>

### [60] [Non-Gaussian fluctuations in relativistic hydrodynamics: Confluent equations for three-point correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14110)
*Xin An,Gokce Basar,Mikhail Stephanov*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文推导了相对论性随机流体动力学中非高斯涨落演化的确定性方程，通过定义平均局部朗道框架（average local Landau frame）和相应的涨落流体力学变量，将完全非线性随机流体动力学表达为统一的多分量矩阵形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论流体动力学中涨落速度（或动量密度）的相关函数计算是一个非平凡问题，需要建立能够描述所有流体力学变量相关函数的理论框架，特别是处理非高斯涨落（non-Gaussian fluctuations）的演化。

Method: 通过定义平均局部朗道框架和相应的涨落流体力学变量，将完全非线性随机流体动力学表达为统一的多分量矩阵形式。引入了一种新颖的相对论形式体系，该体系在平均局部朗道框架的局部空间基底的SO(3)旋转下具有明显协变性。

Result: 推导出了描述所有流体力学变量相关函数的确定性方程，包括涨落速度（fluctuating velocity）或动量密度的相关函数，这些方程能够处理相对论性随机流体动力学中的非高斯涨落演化。

Conclusion: 建立了一个统一的理论框架，能够系统地描述相对论性随机流体动力学中非高斯涨落的演化，特别是解决了涨落速度相关函数计算这一非平凡问题，为研究相对论流体系统的涨落行为提供了新工具。

Abstract: We derive deterministic equations for the evolution of non-Gaussian fluctuations in relativistic stochastic hydrodynamics. This is achieved by defining the average local Landau frame and corresponding fluctuating hydrodynamic variables. Fully nonlinear stochastic hydrodynamics is expressed in a unified multi-component matrix form. A novel relativistic formalism, also manifestly covariant under SO(3) rotations of the local spatial basis in the average local Landau frame, is introduced. The equations describe correlators of all hydrodynamic variables, including fluctuating velocity (or momentum density) -- a nontrivial problem in relativistic hydrodynamics.

### [61] [Dynamics of spin glasses in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13480)

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过薄膜多层结构探索自旋玻璃（spin glass）在二维和三维空间中的动力学差异，发现二维体系在长时间尺度下表现出更快的关联长度增长，并能在实验时间尺度内达到平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋玻璃动力学强烈依赖于空间维度D，其下临界维度约为2.5，导致二维体系中凝聚温度T_g=0，仅在有限温度下存在涨落。通过薄膜多层结构可以同时探索三维和二维维度的动力学行为。

Method: 采用CuMn 4.5 nm薄膜多层结构，通过测量关联长度（correlation length）的增长来研究自旋玻璃动力学。该方法允许在短到中等时间尺度观察三维动力学，在长时间尺度观察二维动力学。

Result: 二维维度中的关联长度增长比三维维度更快，在最长的测量时间内，实验上达到了与模拟结果定性一致的平衡状态。薄膜多层结构从短到中等时间的三维动力学过渡到长时间尺度的二维动力学。

Conclusion: 薄膜多层结构为研究不同维度下的自旋玻璃动力学提供了有效平台，二维体系在长时间尺度下表现出更快的动力学演化，并能在实验可及的时间范围内达到平衡状态。

Abstract: Spin glass dynamics is a strong function of spatial dimensionality $D$. The lower critical dimension is close to 2.5, so that, in two dimensions, the condensation temperature $T_\text{g}=0$, and only fluctuations are present at finite temperatures. However, by using thin film multilayers, one can explore the dynamics in both $D=3$ and $D=2$ dimensions. Spin glass thin film multilayers transition from $D=3$ dynamics at short to intermediate times to $D = 2$ dynamics at long times. Correlation lengths of CuMn 4.5 nm multilayers at long times are shown to be grow more rapidly in $D=2$ as compared to $D=3$, and for the longest measurement time, experimentally reach equilibrium in qualitative agreement with simulations.

### [62] [Bosonic Working Media in a Frustrated Rhombi Chain: Otto and Stirling Cycles from Flat Bands, Caging, and Flux Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13185)
*Francisco J. Peña,Rafael García-Zamora,Gabriele De Chiara,Jorge Flores,Santiago Henríquez,Felipe Barra,Patricio Vargas*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文证明，通过平带工程（flat-band engineering）可以控制和优化量子热机的热力学性能。在菱形链晶格的非相互作用玻色子系统中，磁通量作为可调参数重塑单粒子能谱，驱动系统进入完全受挫的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆囚禁（Aharonov-Bohm caging）区域，能带结构从色散转变为完全平带，显著改变模式的热占据。这种通量诱导的能谱重构对奥托循环（Otto cycle）和斯特林循环（Stirling cycle）产生不同的热力学影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索如何通过平带工程控制和优化量子热机的热力学性能。几何受挫（geometric frustration）和阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆囚禁作为热力学资源，通过合成规范场（synthetic gauge fields）进行能谱工程，为定制玻色子量子热机性能提供实验可行的途径。

Method: 采用菱形链晶格（rhombi-chain lattice）上的非相互作用玻色子，在非相互作用极限下描述为玻色-哈伯德模型（Bose-Hubbard model）。磁通量作为可调参数连续重塑单粒子能谱，驱动系统进入完全受挫的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆囚禁区域，使能带结构从色散转变为完全平带。

Result: 通量诱导的能谱重构产生明确可测量的热力学后果。奥托循环在接近囚禁区域工作时，输出功和效率均显著增强，其机制是释放到冷库的热量显著抑制而非吸收热量增加。斯特林循环则由等温通量驱动过程中的熵变控制，在更宽参数范围内实现更大功提取但效率较低。

Conclusion: 几何受挫和阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆囚禁被确立为热力学资源，通过合成规范场进行能谱工程为定制玻色子量子热机性能提供了可行且实验可及的途径。平带形成是增加功提取的有效策略，揭示了能谱结构对量子热机性能的关键调控作用。

Abstract: We demonstrate that flat-band engineering provides a direct route to control and optimize the thermodynamic performance of quantum heat engines. We consider noninteracting bosons on a rhombi-chain lattice described by a Bose-Hubbard model in the noninteracting limit, where a magnetic flux serves as a tunable parameter that continuously reshapes the single-particle spectrum. By driving the system toward the fully frustrated Aharonov-Bohm caging regime, the band structure transitions from dispersive to completely flat, strongly modifying the thermal occupation of the modes. We show that this flux-induced spectral restructuring has clear and measurable thermodynamic consequences. In particular, the Otto cycle exhibits a significant enhancement of both work output and efficiency when operating near the caging regime. We identify the underlying mechanism as a pronounced suppression of heat released to the cold reservoir, rather than an increase in absorbed heat, revealing that flat-band formation is an effective strategy to increase work extraction. In contrast, the Stirling cycle is governed by entropy variations along isothermal, flux-driven processes, leading to greater work extraction over a broader parameter range but at lower efficiency. These results establish geometric frustration and Aharonov-Bohm caging as thermodynamic resources and show that spectral engineering via synthetic gauge fields offers a viable, experimentally accessible pathway to tailor the performance of bosonic quantum thermal machines.

</details>


### [63] [Long-lived revivals and real-space fragmentation in chains of multispecies Rydberg atoms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13257)
*Jose Soto-Garcia,Natalia Chepiga*

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模矩阵乘积态模拟，揭示了双物种里德堡原子链中种内排斥与种间吸引竞争诱导的动态碎裂现象，表现为扩展冻结区域与局域振荡区域共存，为超越单物种系统的非平衡量子动力学提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然大多数里德堡原子研究集中于单物种系统，但多物种架构提供了额外的相互作用通道并实现了新形式的动力学约束。本研究旨在探索双物种里德堡原子链的非平衡动力学，超越单物种系统的限制。

Method: 采用大规模矩阵乘积态（matrix product state）模拟方法，研究一维铯（Cs）和铷（Rb）双物种里德堡原子链的动力学行为，该系统具有物种依赖的范德瓦尔斯（van der Waals）相互作用。

Result: 种内排斥与种间吸引的竞争诱导了动态碎裂（dynamical fragmentation），表现为扩展冻结区域与局域振荡区域共存。在纯排斥区域，物种选择性淬灭（species-selective quenches）驱动自发碎裂，形成动态断开区域并伴随不规则复苏（irregular revivals）。

Conclusion: 这些现象在不同相互作用区域均表现出鲁棒性，揭示了碎裂的普适机制，确立了多物种里德堡原子阵列作为探索超越单物种系统的非平衡量子动力学的通用平台。

Abstract: Arrays of Rydberg atoms provide a powerful platform for exploring constrained quantum dynamics and nonergodic many-body phenomena. While most work has focused on single-species systems, multispecies architectures offer additional interaction channels and enable new forms of dynamical constraints. We study the nonequilibrium dynamics of one-dimensional dual-species Rydberg chains of Cs and Rb atoms with species-dependent van der Waals interactions. Using large-scale matrix product state simulations, we show that the competition between intra-species repulsion and inter-species attraction induces dynamical fragmentation, marked by the coexistence of extended frozen regions and localized oscillatory sectors. The frozen regions act as emergent barriers that isolate and protect coherent dynamics. In the purely repulsive regime, we find that species-selective quenches drive spontaneous fragmentation, leading to dynamically disconnected regions with irregular revivals. These phenomena are robust across interaction regimes, revealing a universal mechanism for fragmentation and establishing multispecies Rydberg arrays as a versatile platform for exploring nonequilibrium quantum dynamics beyond single-species systems.

</details>


### [64] [Attractive Multidimensional Condensates--Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13370)
*Hikaru Tamura,Chen-Lung Hung*

Conclusion: 本章系统综述了吸引型玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的实验进展，展示了光学囚禁和相互作用控制技术如何推动对多维亮孤子、调制不稳定性等非平衡现象的理解，为研究复杂量子动力学提供了重要实验平台。

Abstract: Experiments on attractive Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs) have unlocked many intriguing out-of-equilibrium dynamics through the interplay between matter-wave dispersion and nonlinear attractive interaction. Competition between these effects leads to fascinating phenomena such as wave collapse, modulational instability, and formation of multidimensional bright solitons. This chapter reviews experimental studies on attractive condensates, with a primary focus on alkali atoms featuring two-body contact interactions. We review recent experimental advances in optical trapping and interaction control techniques, which have enabled new studies on attractive condensates in three and also in lower dimensions. Specifically, we discuss pioneering and recent experimental observations on the dynamics and stability of attractive BECs, including the formation of bright solitons, their collisions, and excitations in quasi-one-dimensional traps. Recent observations of the elusive two-dimensional Townes solitons and vortex solitons are also discussed in this Chapter. We then highlight an experimental technique revealing the nonclassical signatures of modulational instability in an attractive condensate.

### [65] [Hole and spin dynamics in an anti-ferromagnet close to half filling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14039)
*Magnus Callsen,Jens H. Nyhegn,Kristian Knakkergaard Nielsen,Georg M. Bruun*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种守恒图解法（conserving diagrammatic method）来分析强关联费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model），重点研究远离半填充反铁磁基态的小空穴掺杂效应。研究发现掺杂导致布里渊区（Brillouin zone）出现四个由磁极化子（magnetic polarons）形成的空穴口袋，并揭示了自旋与电荷自由度之间的复杂竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于电荷与自旋动力学在强关联材料中的相互作用，以及近期量子模拟实验的启发。需要发展系统理论来分析远离半填充反铁磁基态的小空穴掺杂情况，以理解自旋与电荷自由度之间的复杂竞争和赝隙相（pseudogap phase）的出现。

Method: 研究开发了一种守恒图解法来描述强排斥和小空穴掺杂下的费米-哈伯德模型。该方法适用于远离半填充反铁磁基态的情况，能够系统分析掺杂对系统的影响。

Result: 研究发现掺杂导致布里渊区出现四个由磁极化子形成的空穴口袋，这些口袋随空穴浓度增加而阻尼增强。同时，反铁磁体的磁振子谱（magnon spectrum）因空穴诱导的磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）而软化和阻尼，导致反铁磁关联被抑制。研究还计算了系统对晶格调制（lattice modulation）的响应，恢复了实验中观察到的同相与异相调制的定性差异。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，自旋与电荷自由度之间的复杂竞争以及赝隙相的出现可以在小掺杂情况下得到有效分析，此时可以发展系统理论。这些发现与近期实验结果一致，为理解赝隙物理（pseudogap physics）提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The interplay between charge and spin dynamics is at the heart of strongly correlated materials. Inspired by recent quantum simulation experiments, we develop a conserving diagrammatic method to describe the Fermi-Hubbard model for strong repulsion and small hole doping away from the half-filled anti-ferromagnetic ground state. We show that doping leads to four hole pockets in the Brillouin zone formed by magnetic polarons, which become increasingly damped with hole concentration. Likewise, the magnon spectrum of the anti-ferromagnet softens and dampens with doping due to hole-induced magnetic frustration. This gives rise to a suppression of the anti-ferromagnetic correlations in agreement with recent experiments. We then calculate the response of the system to a lattice modulation and recover the qualitative difference between in-phase and out-of-phase modulations seen in experiments, which was interpreted as signs of pseudogap physics. Our results indicate that the complex competition between spin and charge degrees of freedom and the emergence of the pseudogap phase may be usefully analyzed for small dopings, where systematic theories can be developed.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种计算不同化学计量水合物结构间自由能差的模拟方法，特别针对与特定压力气体储层相连的体系。该方法需要能够确定当两种水合物结构具有相同水分子数时的共存参数。

Method: 方法基于等压晶格切换蒙特卡洛（isobaric Lattice Switch Monte Carlo）模拟，测量水合物结构在完全充满气体分子或完全空置时的自由能差。该测量与热力学积分（thermodynamic integration）相结合，在客体分子数可随化学势波动的系综中进行。

Result: 通过分析恒定水分子数、化学势、压力和温度（constant-$N_w,μ_g,P,T$）系综的性质，展示了如何利用热力学循环计算共存点。应用于氩和甲烷结构时，获得的共存压力与现有实验数据总体吻合良好。

Conclusion: 所提出的模拟技术能够有效计算不同化学计量水合物结构的自由能差，并通过热力学循环确定共存参数，为水合物相平衡研究提供了可靠的计算方法。

Abstract: We introduce a simulation technique to compute the free energy difference between two hydrate structures of different stoichiometry connected to a reservoir of gas molecules at a prescribed pressure. The method permits the determination of coexistence parameters for the system when the two hydrate structures have the same number of water molecules $N_w$. The approach is based on performing isobaric Lattice Switch Monte Carlo simulations to measure free energy differences between the hydrate structures when they are either fully occupied by gas molecules, or fully empty. This measurement is combined with thermodynamic integration within an ensemble in which the number of guest molecules $N_g$ can fluctuate under the control of a chemical potential $μ_g$. We analyze the properties of the resulting constant-$N_w,μ_g,P,T$ ensemble and show how it can be used to calculate coexistence points via a thermodynamic cycle. Applying the method to argon and methane structures, we find coexistence pressures that are in good agreement overall with the available experimental data.

### [67] [Ion-Specific Anomalous Water Diffusion in Aqueous Electrolytes: A Machine-Learned Many-Body Force Field Study with MACE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13659)
*Massimo Ciacchi,Ilnur Saitov,Nico Di Fonte,Isabella Daidone,Carlo Pierleoni*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电解质溶液中水的动力学表现出显著的离子特异性异常：在离液序列高的CsI溶液中水扩散系数相对于纯水增强，而在亲液序列高的NaCl溶液中却被抑制。这一现象长期以来对基于经典力场的分子动力学模拟构成挑战。

Method: 采用基于MACE等变图神经网络框架训练的多体机器学习力场（many-body machine-learned force field, MLFF）进行经典分子动力学模拟。力场在revPBE-D3交换-关联泛函的密度泛函理论水平上训练能量、力和应力，该泛函为水体系提供了精度与计算效率的可靠平衡。

Result: 在环境条件下对0.89-3.56 mol/kg浓度范围的NaCl和CsI水溶液模拟，重现了实验观察到的异常扩散现象，并显示出比先前使用相同理论训练的DeePMD框架结果有定量改进。Na⁺的第一水合壳层相互作用更强，且第二水合壳层的阻滞贡献不可忽略；CsI溶液中水的加速主要由阴离子I⁻驱动，其弥散且弱结构化的水合壳层促进了与体相水的快速交换。

Conclusion: 通过时间依赖水扩散系数和离子-氧平均力势的壳层分解分析，为所研究水电解质中的加速-阻滞机制提供了连贯的微观图像，解释了离子特异性水扩散异常现象的微观机理。

Abstract: The dynamics of water in electrolyte solutions exhibits a striking, ion-specific anomaly: the diffusion coefficient of water is enhanced relative to the neat liquid in chaotropic CsI solutions, yet suppressed in kosmotropic NaCl solutions. This phenomenon, long challenging for classical force-field-based molecular dynamics, is studied here using classical molecular dynamics simulations with a many-body machine-learned force field (MLFF) trained within the MACE equivariant graph neural network framework. The force field is trained on energies, forces, and stresses computed at the density functional theory level with the revPBE-D3 exchange--correlation functional, which provides a reliable balance between accuracy and computational efficiency for aqueous systems. Simulations of NaCl and CsI aqueous solutions at ambient conditions over a concentration range of 0.89--3.56~mol/kg reproduce the experimentally observed anomalous diffusion and show a quantitative improvement over previous results obtained with the DeePMD framework, trained on the same theory, particularly for NaCl solutions. This improvement is traced to a stronger Na$^{+}$--water interaction in the first hydration shell and the non-negligible retarding contribution of the second hydration shell of Na$^{+}$. For CsI solutions, the water acceleration is shown to be primarily driven by the anion I$^{-}$, whose diffuse and weakly structured hydration shell facilitates rapid water exchange with the bulk. These results are rationalised through a shell-decomposition analysis of time-dependent water diffusivities and ion--oxygen potentials of mean force providing a coherent microscopic picture of the acceleration--retardation mechanism in the studied aqueous electrolytes.

*Airi Kawasaki,Fei Gao,Gustavo E. Scuseria*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：1）开发AGP-CI波函数，通过CI展开引入关联；2）将AGP-CI重写为线性组合AGP（LC-AGP），利用标准AGP计算工具；3）基于边界秩分解（border-rank decompositions）将波函数重组为紧凑的线性组合形式，引入小变形参数τ控制截断近似的精度。

Result: 在哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）和小分子H₂O、N₂上的基准测试表明，所提出的波函数实现了持续的高精度，特别是在电子数较多和强关联区域，其性能优于LC-AGP方法。

Conclusion: AGP-CI波函数通过有效引入双粒子组间关联，在保持计算可行性的同时显著提升了强关联体系的描述精度，为量子化学计算提供了有前景的新方法。

Abstract: In this paper, we develop a class of antisymmetrized geminal power configuration interaction (AGP-CI) wave functions that extend the AGP framework by incorporating inter-geminal correlations through a CI expansion. To make these wavefunctions computationally tractable, we evaluate them by rewriting the AGP-CI ansatz as a linear combination of AGPs (LC-AGP), for which overlaps and Hamiltonian matrix elements can be computed with standard AGP machinery. Motivated by border-rank decompositions, we further reorganize this ansatz into a compact linear combination of AGPs depending on a small deformation parameter $τ$, which controls how closely the truncated expansion approximates the full AGP-CI state. Benchmark applications to the Hubbard model and to the small molecules H$_2$O and N$_2$ demonstrate that the proposed wavefunctions achieve consistently high accuracy and outperform the LC-AGP, particularly for systems with more electrons and in strongly correlated regimes.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We show that electron drag by nonequilibrium phonons describes the actual waveform and spectrum of terahertz pulses generated during femtosecond laser irradiation of metals. In contrast to previous models, there is a picosecond delay in the drag force development due to the relatively slow lattice heating and finite phonon lifetime. We also predict that, at high pump fluences, a macroscopic deformation wave enhances nonlinearly the drag force and terahertz response. Our results establish the terahertz pulse waveform as a direct probe of ultrafast lattice dynamics in metals.

### [70] [Confinement-controlled pathways to complex skyrmionic textures in Co/W/Pt multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13497)
*Y. Al Sadi,R. Sbiaa,W. Al Saidi,M. Souier,G. Lezier,O. Marbouh,M. T. Z. Myint,Y. Dusch,S. Al Harthi,A. Talbi,N. Tiercelin,S. N. Piramanayagam*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明几何限制（geometric confinement）可作为控制参数，在室温下实现手性自旋纹理（chiral spin textures）从迷宫畴（labyrinth domains）到斯格明子（skyrmions）再到高阶拓扑态（higher-order topological states）的层级转变，为多态斯格明子器件提供了可扩展的材料策略。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性斯格明子（magnetic skyrmions）和高阶拓扑自旋纹理（higher-order topological spin textures）为多级信息编码提供了丰富机会，但它们在室温下几何限制中的确定性稳定和转变机制尚不明确。

Method: 研究采用Pt/Co/W多层微轨道（multilayer micro-tracks）体系，通过改变几何限制程度，结合微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）和统计分析（statistical analysis）来观察自旋纹理的转变过程。

Result: 随着限制增强，扩展的迷宫畴（labyrinth domains）分裂为孤立斯格明子（isolated skyrmions），随后斯格明子对被抑制，紧凑的高阶纹理（higher-order textures）优先稳定。限制促进了斯格明子环（skyrmioniums）的形成及其向均匀斯格明子袋（skyrmion bags）的演化，在最窄轨道中斯格明子袋成为主导状态。

Conclusion: 几何限制是复杂拓扑纹理的确定性选择器，揭示了在室温下工程化高阶斯格明子态（higher-order skyrmionic states）的新途径，为基于多态斯格明子的自旋电子学（spintronic）和存储器架构提供了可扩展的材料策略。

Abstract: Magnetic skyrmions and higher-order topological spin textures offer rich opportunities for multi-level information encoding, yet their deterministic stabilization and transformation under geometric confinement at room temperature remain poorly understood. Here, we demonstrate that geometric confinement acts as a robust and universal control parameter that governs a hierarchical transformation pathway of chiral spin textures in Pt/Co/W multilayer micro-tracks. As the confinement increases, extended labyrinth domains fragment into isolated skyrmions, followed by the systematic suppression of skyrmion pairs and the preferential stabilization of compact higher-order textures. We find that confinement strongly enhances the formation of skyrmioniums via recombination and promotes their subsequent evolution into uniform skyrmion bags by capturing additional skyrmions. Statistical analysis reveals a confinement-driven redistribution of topological populations, with skyrmion bags emerging as the dominant state in the narrowest tracks. Supported by micromagnetic simulations, our results establish geometric confinement as a deterministic selector of complex topological textures and reveal a previously unexplored route for engineering higher-order skyrmionic states at room temperature. These findings provide a scalable materials strategy for multistate skyrmion-based spintronic and memory architectures.

### [71] [Universal thermometry of solid-liquid interfacial thermal conductance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13741)
*Tao Chen,Puqing Jiang*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通用的宽带方脉冲测温方法，能够同时测量任意固液界面的热导（ITC）和纳米级液膜厚度，验证了该方法在多种材料组合中的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固液界面热导（ITC）对微流体、电子和能源系统中的热传输至关重要，但大多数光学测温技术仅限于特定的金属-液体界面，缺乏通用测量方法。

Method: 开发了一种通用的宽带方脉冲测温方法（universal broadband square-pulsed thermometry method），能够同时量化各种任意固液界面的ITC并精确测量纳米级液膜厚度。

Result: 该方法测得铝-水界面的ITC值为50-55 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)，与先前研究一致；玻璃-水（9.9 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)）和硅-水（5.7 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)）的ITC显著更低；铝-硅油（~10 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)）和PMMA-硅油（~0.4 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)）的测量进一步验证了该方法在高粘度非极性液体和聚合物-液体界面的适用性。

Conclusion: 该方法能够捕捉不同固液组合的热传输差异，通过与声学/扩散失配模型和分子动力学模拟的比较及理论分析，揭示了振动失配、润湿性和表面条件对界面热传输的影响，为界面传热科学和技术提供了广泛应用的快速定量表征工具。

Abstract: Solid-liquid interfacial thermal conductance (ITC) critically influences heat transport in microfluidic, electronic, and energy systems, yet most optical thermometry techniques are limited to specific metal-liquid interfaces. In this work, we introduce a universal broadband square-pulsed thermometry method that enables simultaneous quantification of ITC across a wide range of arbitrary solid-liquid interfaces, while also providing accurate measurements of nanoscale liquid-film thickness. To validate the method, we applied it to Al-water interfaces, yielding ITC values in the range of 50-55 MW m^(-2) K^(-1), consistent with prior studies. The technique also reveals markedly lower ITCs for glass-water (9.9 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)) and Si-water (5.7 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)), and further measurements on Al-silicone oil (~10 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)) and PMMA-silicone oil (~0.4 MW m^(-2) K^(-1)) extend the validation to highly viscous nonpolar liquids and polymer-liquid interfaces. These results highlight the capability of the method to capture thermal transport differences across diverse solid-liquid combinations. Further comparisons with acoustic/diffuse mismatch models and molecular dynamics simulations, together with theoretical analysis, highlight the influence of vibrational mismatch, wettability, and surface condition on interfacial thermal transport. This broadly applicable technique enables rapid, quantitative characterization of solid-liquid interfacial thermal transport, with broad implications for interfacial heat transfer science and technology.

</details>


### [72] [A Variable-Spot-Size and Multi-Frequency Square-Pulsed Source (SPS) Approach for Comprehensive Characterization of Anisotropic Thermal Transport Properties in Multilayered Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13744)
*Kexin Zhang,Tao Chen,Jinlong Ma,Puqing Jiang*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种可变光斑尺寸多频方波脉冲源（SPS）方法，用于同时测定多层薄膜结构中的各向异性热导率、热容和界面热导，并在硅绝缘体（SOI）样品上验证了其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多层薄膜结构在工业应用中普遍存在，但其热性能表征面临挑战。这些薄膜通常具有纳米至微米级厚度，表现出各向异性热导率（anisotropic thermal conductivity）和非体相热容（non-bulk heat capacity），难以精确测量。

Method: 本研究引入了可变光斑尺寸多频方波脉冲源（variable-spot-size and multi-frequency square-pulsed source, SPS）方法。该方法利用宽调制频率范围（1 Hz至10 MHz）和可调激光光斑尺寸，增强了对不同层热参数的敏感性。

Result: 在包含1.59微米Si层、1.03微米SiO2层和带有122纳米铝（Al）换能器的硅衬底的SOI样品上，SPS方法成功提取了七个关键热参数。温度依赖性测量（80至500 K）结果与文献值和第一性原理预测高度一致。

Conclusion: SPS方法被证明是复杂多层结构全面热表征的强大工具，对基础研究和实际应用均有重要意义。该方法能够同时测定各向异性热导率、热容和界面热导，具有高准确性和可靠性。

Abstract: Multilayered thin-film structures are frequently encountered in industrial applications, where accurate thermal property characterization is essential for performance optimization. These films, typically ranging from nanometers to micrometers in thickness, often exhibit anisotropic thermal conductivity and non-bulk heat capacity, which are challenging to measure. In this study, we introduce a variable-spot-size and multi-frequency square-pulsed source (SPS) method for the simultaneous determination of anisotropic thermal conductivities, heat capacities, and interfacial thermal conductance in multilayered systems. By leveraging a broad modulation frequency range (1 Hz to 10 MHz) and tunable laser spot sizes, the SPS method enhances sensitivity to different thermal parameters across layers. We validate this approach on a silicon-on-insulator (SOI) sample comprising a 1.59 um Si layer, 1.03 um SiO2 layer, and a silicon substrate with a 122 nm aluminum (Al) transducer. The SPS method successfully extracts seven key thermal parameters, including the in-plane and cross-plane thermal conductivities and heat capacity of the Si film, the thermal conductivity and heat capacity of the SiO2 layer, the thermal conductivity of the substrate, and the interfacial thermal conductance between Al and Si. Temperature-dependent measurements from 80 to 500 K showed excellent agreement with literature values and first-principles predictions, confirming the method's accuracy and reliability. These results demonstrate the SPS method as a powerful tool for comprehensive thermal characterization of complex multilayered structures, with implications for both fundamental research and practical applications.

### [73] [Z Boson Radiative Decay $Z\to μ^+ μ^- γ$ at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13156)
*Yifan Fei,Peiran Li,Zhen Liu,Maxim Pospelov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了LHC上Z玻色子的辐射衰变过程Z→μ⁺μ⁻γ，提供了标准模型精度分析和新物理探测能力评估。研究显示该衰变模式可在亚百分比统计精度下测量，并可作为探测轴子类粒子和反常规范玻色子的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索Z玻色子辐射衰变Z→μ⁺μ⁻γ作为标准模型（Standard Model, SM）精度测试和新物理探测工具的潜力。重点关注该衰变通道对轴子类粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs）和反常U(1)_X规范玻色子的敏感性。

Method: 方法包括对LHC Run-2和未来HL-LHC性能的详细分析，以及从现有Run-1数据中提取分支比。通过分析Z→a/X+γ→μ⁺μ⁻γ末态中的双μ子不变质量谱（dimuon invariant mass spectrum）的共振结构来探测新物理。

Result: 从Run-1数据中提取了分支比Br^fid(Z→μμγ)=(3.34±0.016)×10⁻⁴。研究表明该衰变通道能够以亚百分比统计精度测量，并对ALPs和反常规范玻色子具有高灵敏度，可将当前对撞机探测范围扩展至g_X∼O(10⁻³)。

Conclusion: Z玻色子辐射衰变为探测轻子性新物理提供了干净且统计能力强的探针，突显了稀有电弱规范玻色子衰变作为标准模型精度测试和LHC上新相互作用灵敏探测器的潜力。

Abstract: We study the radiative decay of the $Z$ boson, $Z \to μ^+μ^-γ$, at the LHC, providing both Standard Model (SM) precision analysis and new physics projections. With detailed analysis of Run-2 and future HL-LHC performances, we demonstrate that this decay mode can be measured with a statistical precision at the sub-percentage level. From existing Run-1 data, we extract $\text{Br}^\text{fid}(Z \to μμγ) = (3.34 \pm 0.016)\times 10^{-4}$. We further explore the sensitivity of this channel to axion-like particles (ALPs) and to an anomalous $U(1)_X$ gauge boson coupled to the muon. Both scenarios feature resonant structures in the dimuon invariant mass spectrum within the $Z \to a/X + γ\to μ^+μ^-γ$ final state. Our results show that the radiative $Z$ decay provides a clean and statistically powerful probe of such leptophilic new physics, extending the current collider reach for ALPs and anomalous gauge forces down to $g_X \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$. This study highlights the potential of rare electroweak gauge boson decays as precision tests of the SM and sensitive probes of new interactions at the LHC.

### [74] [Proton Structure from Neural Simulation-Based Inference at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13157)
*Ricardo Barrué,Lisa Benato,Ali Kaan Güven,Elie Hammou,Jaco ter Hoeve,Claudius Krause,Ang Li,Luca Mantani,Juan Rojo,Sergio Sánchez Cruz,Robert Schöfbeck,Maria Ubiali,Daohan Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子部分子分布函数（PDFs）的精确测定是LHC分析的关键要素，但现有方法基于对分箱低维数据的全局拟合，存在信息损失。本研究旨在探索利用无分箱高维数据提升PDF约束精度的新方法。

Method: 采用神经模拟推理（neural simulation-based inference, NSBI）方法，利用LHC在$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV能量下顶夸克对产生（top quark pair production）的模拟数据，同时考虑探测器级特征中的实验和理论系统不确定性。

Result: 作为概念验证，成功确定了胶子PDF（gluon PDF），NSBI流程相比现有低维分箱分析实现了精度上的显著提升，展示了无分箱推理减少对不确定性粗糙近似依赖的潜力。

Conclusion: 无分箱推理方法能够充分利用数据的完整统计能力，消除分箱过程导致的信息损失，为LHC探测器级机器学习辅助测量开辟了新范式，有助于减少PDF确定中对不确定性及其相关性近似处理的依赖。

Abstract: The precise determination of the parton distribution functions (PDFs) of the proton is an essential ingredient for LHC analyses, including for those at the upcoming High-Luminosity LHC. So far, PDFs are determined from global fits to binned low-dimensional data obtained from unfolded hard-scattering cross section measurements. In this work we demonstrate for the first time the feasibility of neural simulation-based inference (NSBI) for constraining the proton PDFs using a high-dimensional unbinned data set. Exploiting the full statistical power of unbinned data removes the loss of information inherited by the binning procedure. As a proof-of-concept, we determine the gluon PDF from simulated data of top quark pair production at the LHC with $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV. Taking into account both experimental and theoretical systematic uncertainties in the detector-level features, we demonstrate how the NSBI pipeline achieves significant improvements in precision compared to existing low-dimensional binned analyses. Our results illustrate the potential of unbinned inference to reduce the reliance on coarse approximations of uncertainties and their correlations entering PDF determinations, hence contributing to a new paradigm of unbinned detector-level ML-assisted measurements at the LHC.

### [75] [Sensitivity to top-quark FCNC interactions at future muon colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13562)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索未来μ子对撞机作为探测顶夸克味改变中性流（FCNC）相互作用的平台，这些过程在标准模型中高度压低，是寻找超出标准模型物理的敏感探针。

Method: 采用有效场论框架参数化反常tqZ和tqγ耦合，通过蒙特卡洛技术模拟信号和背景事件，使用Pythia进行部分子簇射和强子化，并基于Delphes进行快速探测器模拟，最后采用提升决策树进行多变量分析。

Result: 在10 ab⁻¹积分亮度下，获得对反常耦合κ_{tqZ}和λ_{tqγ}的灵敏度达到O(10⁻³)量级，对应稀有衰变t→qZ和t→qγ的分支比极限为O(10⁻⁶)，比当前CMS和ATLAS合作组的限制提高了一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 多TeV μ子对撞机为探测稀有顶夸克相互作用提供了强大且互补的平台，通过味改变中性流过程为探索超出标准模型物理提供了独特机会。

Abstract: We investigate flavor-changing neutral current (FCNC) interactions of the top quark at a future muon collider with a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s} = 10~\mathrm{TeV}$. The process $μ^{+}μ^{-} \to ν_μ\,μ^+\,b\,j$ and its corresponding charge conjugate are considered as a probe of anomalous $tqZ$ and $tqγ$ couplings, parametrized within an effective field theory framework in terms of $κ_{tqZ}$ and $λ_{tqγ}$. Signal and background events are simulated using Monte Carlo techniques, including parton showering and hadronization with \texttt{Pythia} and a fast detector simulation based on \texttt{Delphes} with a dedicated 10~TeV muon collider setup. A multivariate analysis based on boosted decision trees is employed to enhance the signal discrimination. Assuming an integrated luminosity of $10~\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$, we obtain projected sensitivities to the anomalous couplings at the $\mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$ level, corresponding to branching ratio limits of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$ for the rare $t \to qZ$ and $t \to qγ$ decays. These results significantly improve upon the current bounds from the CMS and ATLAS collaborations, extending the sensitivity by more than one order of magnitude. Our findings demonstrate that a multi-TeV muon collider provides a powerful and complementary platform for probing rare top-quark interactions, offering a unique opportunity to explore physics beyond the Standard Model through FCNC processes.

We quantify the contributions of thermal vorticity and magnetic field to the global spin polarization of $Λ$ hyperons. Comparing results with recent ALICE measurements in Pb+Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$ = 2.76 and 5.02 TeV shows qualitative agreement, offering new insights into the vortical structure of QCD matter. ### [79] [AI-assisted modeling and Bayesian inference of unpolarized quark transverse momentum distributions from Drell-Yan data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14133)
*Zhong-Bo Kang,Luke Sellers,Congyue Zhang,Curtis Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在贝叶斯推断框架下，结合人工智能技术，从Drell-Yan数据中提取了非极化夸克横向动量依赖部分子分布函数（TMD PDFs）。研究采用N³LO微扰QCD结合N⁴LL求和精度，通过AI驱动的迭代程序探索候选函数形式，并构建机器学习模拟器进行高效贝叶斯推断。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用贝叶斯推断框架，在N³LO微扰QCD结合N⁴LL求和精度下进行分析。首先使用AI驱动的迭代程序探索和排序TMD PDFs非微扰贡献及Collins-Soper演化核的候选函数形式。通过训练机器学习模拟器构建TMD截面的代理模型，替代计算昂贵的重复评估，并采用仿射不变马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）集成进行可扩展采样。

Result: 对来自固定靶、RHIC和LHC实验的Drell-Yan数据进行了全局分析，提取了具有量化不确定性的TMD PDFs。将结果与使用副本方法（replica method）获得的结果进行比较，并突出了不确定性估计的差异。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了一个结合人工智能技术的贝叶斯推断框架，用于从Drell-Yan数据中提取TMD PDFs。该方法通过AI驱动的函数形式探索和机器学习模拟器的使用，实现了高效的不确定性量化，为TMD PDFs的精确提取提供了新途径。

Abstract: We present an extraction of unpolarized quark transverse-momentum-dependent parton distribution functions (TMD PDFs) from Drell-Yan data within a Bayesian inference framework, incorporating artificial intelligence at multiple stages of the analysis. Our analysis is performed at ${\rm N^3LO}$ in perturbative QCD combined with ${\rm N^4LL}$ resummation accuracy. We first employ an AI-driven iterative procedure to explore and rank candidate functional forms for the nonperturbative contributions to TMD PDFs at the initial scale, as well as for the Collins-Soper evolution kernel, using $χ^2$ fits and physics constraints. To enable efficient Bayesian inference, we construct a surrogate model for TMD cross sections by training a machine-learning emulator over the parameter space, replacing computationally expensive repeated evaluations and allowing scalable sampling with an affine-invariant Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) ensemble. Using this framework, we perform a global analysis of Drell-Yan data from fixed-target, RHIC, and LHC experiments and extract TMD PDFs with quantified uncertainties. We compare the results with those obtained using the replica method and highlight differences in the resulting uncertainty estimates.

### [80] [A Core Representation Theorem for Scheme-Invariant Collinear Factorization in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13439)
*Dustin Keller*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将微扰QCD中的共线因子化（collinear factorization）和领头扭度算子乘积展开（leading-twist OPE）的形式冗余性（presentation non-uniqueness）进行范畴化（categorically）形式化，引入接口代数对象（interface algebra object）和模结构（module structures），并证明了核心表示定理（Core Representation Theorem）识别出普适的方案不变量载体（scheme-invariant carrier）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微扰QCD中的共线因子化和领头扭度算子乘积展开存在结构性的"表示非唯一性"（presentation non-uniqueness）：系数和关联函数（correlators）本身不具有物理性，仅通过有限因子化方案重定义（finite factorization-scheme redefinitions）来定义。需要形式化这种冗余性以理解其数学结构。

Method: 通过引入编码允许的有限共线抵消项/混合核（finite collinear counterterms/mixing kernels）的接口代数对象（interface algebra object），并将系数数据和强子数据组织为该代数上的右/左模（right/left modules）。在编码所选重组计算（recomposition calculus）的对称幺半范畴（symmetric monoidal category）中构建数学框架。

Result: 主要成果是核心表示定理（Core Representation Theorem），该定理识别出普适的方案不变量载体：平衡（方案不变）配对（balanced pairings）的函子（functor）由相对张量积（relative tensor product）$C\otimes_A f$表示，这是在保持方案不变语义的所有朴素复合（naive composite）$C\otimes f$的商（quotients）中终端的（terminal）。

Conclusion: 论文展示了标准物理输入（对称性约束、定域性/OPE和精度截断）如何规范地诱导接口代数和模结构，并证明了将长距离算子/关联函数的生成集（generating set）完备化为A稳定扇区（A-stable sector）的最小闭包原理（minimal closure principle）。

Abstract: Collinear factorization and the leading-twist operator product expansion (OPE) in perturbative QCD express suitably inclusive observables in scale-separated kinematics as composites of perturbative short-distance coefficients with universal long-distance non-perturbative correlators such as parton distribution functions (PDFs), up to controlled power corrections. A persistent structural feature is \emph{presentation non-uniqueness}: coefficients and correlators are not individually physical, but are defined only up to finite factorization-scheme redefinitions induced by collinear subtractions and renormalized-operator mixing. We formalize this redundancy categorically by introducing an \emph{interface algebra object} encoding admissible finite collinear counterterms/mixing kernels and by organizing coefficient data and hadronic data as right/left modules over this algebra in a symmetric monoidal category encoding the chosen recomposition calculus. Our main result, the \emph{Core Representation Theorem}, identifies the universal scheme-invariant carrier: the functor of balanced (scheme-invariant) pairings is represented by the relative tensor product $C\otimes_A f$, which is terminal among all quotients of the naive composite $C\otimes f$ that preserve scheme-invariant semantics. Finally, we show how standard physics inputs (symmetry constraints, locality/OPE, and a stated accuracy truncation) canonically induce the interface algebra and module structures, and we prove a minimal closure principle for completing a generating set of long-distance operators/correlators to an $A$-stable sector.

</details>

*Kai-Ge Zhang,Jian-Feng He,Chengjie Fu,Zong-Kuan Guo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过积分重狄拉克费米子，推导了轴子暴胀（axion inflation）的单圈有效描述，发现阈值跃迁（threshold transition）会瞬态增强规范场产生，在deci-hertz频段产生手征随机引力波背景（chiral stochastic gravitational-wave background）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过积分具有暴胀子依赖复质量的狄拉克费米子，推导单圈有效描述，分析平滑局域化阈值跃迁（smooth localized threshold transition）对暴胀子和规范场（gauge sectors）的修正。

Result: 阈值跃迁诱导了Coleman-Weinberg项、真空极化修正（vacuum-polarization correction）和反常诱导的Chern-Simons耦合（anomaly-induced Chern-Simons coupling），这些效应共同瞬态增强并局域化规范场产生，在deci-hertz频段产生手征随机引力波背景，位于BBO和DECIGO探测器的预期灵敏度范围内，同时低于原初黑洞（primordial-black-hole）代表性界限。

Conclusion: 轴子暴胀中的重费米子阈值跃迁能够产生可观测的引力波信号，为暴胀物理和早期宇宙探测提供了新的可能性，且该信号在当前实验探测范围内。

Abstract: We derive a one-loop effective description of axion inflation by integrating out a heavy Dirac fermion with an inflaton-dependent complex mass undergoing a smooth localized threshold transition. The threshold induces correlated corrections to the inflaton and gauge sectors, including a Coleman-Weinberg term, a vacuum-polarization correction, and an anomaly-induced Chern-Simons coupling. Together, these effects transiently enhance and localize gauge-field production, generating a chiral stochastic gravitational-wave background in the deci-hertz band within the projected sensitivities of BBO and DECIGO, while remaining below representative primordial-black-hole bounds.

### [82] [Torsion induced one-loop corrections to inflaton decay and the Stochastic gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13844)
*AlexKen Lee,Keyun Wu*

TL;DR: 本文研究了由挠率（torsion）诱导的四费米子相互作用对暴胀子（inflaton）三体衰变的一圈修正及其对相关随机引力波信号的影响，发现费米子自相互作用能显著抑制引力波信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨挠率诱导的四费米子相互作用对暴胀子衰变过程的量子修正，特别是这些修正如何影响基于树图分析预测的随机引力波信号，这对于现实唯象研究至关重要。

Method: 研究方法包括计算挠率诱导的四费米子相互作用对暴胀子三体衰变的一圈修正，并分析这些修正对重整化群（renormalization group）尺度u的依赖关系，在微扰理论框架内考察代表性暴胀子质量远低于普朗克尺度的情形。

Result: 研究结果显示重整化群尺度依赖存在显著不对称性：引力波谱增强有限（不超过约一个数量级），而抑制效应更强（可达两个数量级，对应百分之一水平的减少）。费米子自相互作用能显著降低基于树图分析的引力波信号预测。

Conclusion: 结论指出一圈修正（特别是费米子自相互作用）能显著抑制引力波信号，可能使信号超出未来观测的灵敏度范围，因此在现实唯象研究中必须考虑这些量子修正效应。

Abstract: We investigate one-loop corrections from torsion-induced four-fermion interactions to inflaton three-body decay and their impact on the associated stochastic gravitational-wave signal. We find a pronounced asymmetry in the dependence on the renormalization scale $u$. While the enhancement of the gravitational-wave spectrum remains modest, not exceeding roughly a factor of order unity for representative inflaton masses well below the Planck scale within the perturbative regime, the suppression can be much stronger, reaching up to two orders of magnitude, corresponding to reductions at the percent level. These results imply that loop corrections, particularly fermionic self-interactions, can significantly reduce the predicted gravitational-wave signal in models based on tree-level analyses. This suppression may shift the signal outside the sensitivity range of future observations and should therefore be taken into account in realistic phenomenological studies.

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) is transforming modern physics research, but practical, hands-on experience with ML techniques remains limited due to cost and complexity barriers. To address this gap, we introduce an affordable, autonomous, Internet-of-Things (IoT)-enabled experimental platform designed specifically for applied physics education. Utilizing an Arduino microcontroller, a customizable multi-wavelength light emitting diode (LED) array, and photosensors, our setup generates diverse, real-time optical datasets ideal for training and evaluating foundational ML algorithms, including traversal methods, Bayesian inference, and deep learning. The platform facilitates a closed-loop, self-driving experimental workflow, encompassing automated data collection, preprocessing, model training, and validation. Through systematic performance comparisons, we demonstrate the superior ability of deep learning to capture complex nonlinear relationships compared to traversal and Bayesian methods. At approximately $60, this open-source IoT platform provides an accessible, practical pathway for students to master advanced ML concepts, promoting deeper conceptual insights and essential technical skills required for the next generation of physicists and engineers.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（density functional theory）因忽略多体电子-电子相互作用而存在局限性，导致单粒子能级误差，如低估带隙和带宽以及界面带对齐错误。GW自能修正（GW self-energy correction）可改善这些缺陷，并能预测准粒子寿命（quasiparticle lifetime）。

Method: 使用近边X射线吸收和发射光谱（near-edge x-ray absorption and emission）探测Li₂CO₃的电子结构。实验测量与第一性原理计算进行比较，计算包括GW自能修正对单粒子能级的修正以及来自Bethe-Salpeter方程的激子效应（exciton effects）。

Result: 未在摘要中明确说明具体实验结果，但研究通过比较实验测量与包含GW修正和激子效应的理论计算来验证理论方法的准确性。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了结合GW自能修正和Bethe-Salpeter方程激子效应的多体微扰理论（many-body perturbation theory）方法在描述材料电子结构方面的应用，特别是对Li₂CO₃的X射线光谱分析。

Abstract: While highly successful, density functional theory is known to have limitations owing to its neglect of many-body electron-electron interactions. This neglect leads to errors in the single-particle energies, leading to underestimated band gaps and band widths as well as errors in band alignment at interfaces. Many-body perturbation theory, in the form of the $GW$ self-energy correction, has been widely used to improve upon these short-comings. Though less well studied, the same $GW$ method is also able to predict the finite quasiparticle lifetime that is seen to cause anomalous broadening in the lowest-lying lines of valence emission spectra. Using near-edge x-ray absorption and emission, we probe the electronic structure of Li$_2$CO$_3$. Our measurements are compared to first-principles calculations, including $GW$ self-energy corrections to the single-particle energies and excitonic effects from the Bethe-Salpeter equation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

In the context of dental health, the two most crucial properties of HAp are mechanical stability, which ensures resistance to forces, and chemical stability, which preserves surface integrity in acidic environments. During early stages of human evolution, e.g. when teeth were used to crush uncooked food, mechanical stability was of paramount importance. However, with changes in diet and lifestyle, the principal origins of tooth damage and loss shifted towards bacterially mediated chemical attack, known as tooth decay, or caries. To enhance the chemical stability, ion doping has emerged as a particularly significant approach, and it lies at the focus of the present study. A Molecular Dynamics (MD) framework was developed to investigate the effects of ion doping on the chemical and mechanical stability of HAp and to identify optimal doping candidates. The framework combines conventional MD with Steered Molecular Dynamics (SMD), Thermodynamic Integration (TI) and uniaxial compression test simulations to provide comprehensive insights into the doping process. The findings revealed surface atoms as the most viable candidates for doping, as demonstrated by SMD and conventional MD simulations. Notably, TI calculations have identified magnesium ions as a better candidate among the ions considered here for enhancing the chemical stability of HAp. The results presented in this study offer valuable guidelines for synthesizing HAp-based substituent materials with properties tailored to meet the demands of modern dental applications such as implant coatings, enamel remineralization agents and restorative materials.

Abstract: The discovery of inorganic crystal structures with targeted properties is a significant challenge in materials science. However, current generative AI models still struggle to produce diverse, original, and reliable structures of experimentally achievable materials suitable for high-stakes applications.
  In this work, we propose a generative machine learning framework based on diffusion models with adaptive constraint guidance, which enables the incorporation of user-defined physical and chemical constraints during the generation process. This approach is designed to be practical and interpretable for human experts, allowing transparent decision-making and expert-driven exploration. Our approach has been tested and validated on several classical examples of inorganic families of compounds, as case studies. ### [87] [Spatial deformation of a ferromagnetic elastic rod](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13790)
*G. R. Krishna Chand Avatar,Vivekanand Dabade*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了不可伸展铁磁弹性杆在纵向磁场和终端载荷作用下的三维变形相图，揭示了软硬铁磁材料在哈密顿霍夫分岔行为上的差异，并分析了螺旋和局部屈曲模式的磁弹性耦合特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁磁弹性细长结构因其磁机械耦合特性，能在适度外部磁场下实现大驱动位移，具有重要应用潜力。本研究旨在深入理解不可伸展铁磁弹性杆在纵向磁场和终端张力、扭矩联合作用下的三维变形动力学行为。

Method: 通过结合Kirchhoff弹性应变能与适用于软硬铁磁材料的微磁能贡献（软磁材料考虑静磁能/demagnetization energy，硬磁材料考虑交换能和Zeeman能），构建总能量泛函。利用圆形截面对称性和控制方程的可积结构，识别守恒的Casimir不变量，将哈密顿量简化为欧拉极角下的单自由度系统。

Result: 相图分析表明：纯弹性杆和硬铁磁杆经历超临界哈密顿霍夫叉形分岔（supercritical Hamiltonian Hopf pitchfork bifurcation），而软铁磁杆仅在磁弹性参数范围$0<\tilde{K}_{dM}<1/8$内出现此分岔。数值构造了对应哈密顿相空间中同宿轨道（homoclinic orbits）的局部屈曲模式，软铁磁杆的局部构型表现出非共线延伸直线段，这是磁弹性耦合直接产生的几何特征。

Conclusion: 研究系统表征了铁磁弹性杆在各种加载场景下的载荷-变形关系，揭示了磁弹性耦合对分岔行为和屈曲模式的显著影响。软铁磁材料独特的几何特征为磁驱动结构设计提供了新的可能性，特别是局部屈曲模式中非共线直线段的出现，直接源于磁弹性相互作用。

Abstract: Ferromagnetic elastic slender structures offer the potential for large actuation displacements under modest external magnetic fields, due to the magneto-mechanical coupling. This paper investigates the phase portraits of the Hamiltonian governing the three-dimensional deformation of inextensible ferromagnetic elastic rods subjected to combined terminal tension and twisting moment in the presence of a longitudinal magnetic field. The total energy functional is formulated by combining the Kirchhoff elastic strain energy with micromagnetic energy contributions appropriate to soft and hard ferromagnetic materials: magnetostatic (demagnetization) energy for the former, and exchange and Zeeman energies for the latter. Exploiting the circular cross-sectional symmetry and the integrable structure of the governing equations, conserved Casimir invariants are identified and the Hamiltonian is reduced to a single-degree-of-freedom system in the Euler polar angle. Analysis of the resulting phase portraits reveals that purely elastic and hard ferromagnetic rods undergo a supercritical Hamiltonian Hopf pitchfork bifurcation, whereas soft ferromagnetic rods exhibit this bifurcation only within a restricted range of the magnetoelastic parameter, $0<\tilde{K}_{dM}<1/8$. Both helical and localized post-buckling configurations are analyzed, and the corresponding load-deformation relationships are systematically characterized across a range of loading scenarios. Localized buckling modes, corresponding to homoclinic orbits in the Hamiltonian phase space, are constructed numerically. In contrast to the purely elastic case, the localized configurations of soft ferromagnetic rods exhibit non-collinear extended straight segments, a geometrically distinctive feature arising directly from the magnetoelastic coupling.

</details>


### [88] [Probing local coordination and halide miscibility in single-, double-, and triple-halide perovskites using EXAFS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13442)
*Sonia S. Mulgund,Esther Y. -H. Hung,Leslie Bostwick,Ashley Galbraith,Owen M. Romberg,Justus Just,Rebecca A. Belisle*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三卤化物钙钛矿（triple-halide perovskites）相较于双卤化物体系展现出更好的稳定性和性能，但对其卤素混溶性和掺入机制的理解仍不充分。传统体相表征指标如晶格间距和光学带隙无法充分证明X位点上的均匀混合，因此需要更局部的探针来研究短程卤素配位和氯离子的作用。

Method: 采用低温X射线吸收光谱（cryogenic X-ray absorption spectroscopy, XAS）对一系列单卤、双卤和三卤化物钙钛矿成分进行表征。通过Pb L3-edge EXAFS的定量拟合和柯西小波变换（Cauchy wavelet transforms）分析卤素混合特征，并利用Br K-edge EXAFS的小波变换通过前向散射放大的第三壳层卤素-卤素相互作用来验证短程配位。

Result: 研究证实了溴含量介导的单一相三卤化物钙钛矿的形成。混合双卤和三卤化物钙钛矿的Pb L3-edge EXAFS分析显示出卤素混合的特征信号。Br K-edge EXAFS的小波变换结果表明，三种卤素在短程范围内完全配位，形成完全混合的钙钛矿相。

Conclusion: 该研究在理解三卤化物钙钛矿局部结构方面取得了重要进展，为全面描述和优化新型钙钛矿成分中的卤素掺入提供了关键的结构信息，有助于材料性能的进一步优化。

Abstract: Lead-halide perovskites are a promising material platform as semiconductors in next-generation solar cells because of their solution processability, defect tolerance, and tunable optoelectronic properties. While iodide-bromide perovskite compositions have shown promise as wide bandgap absorbers, they also suffer from significant instabilities under operating conditions. Triple-halide perovskites, where chloride is additionally incorporated, have demonstrated improved stability and performance over their double-halide counterparts; however, relatively little is understood about halide miscibility and incorporation in these novel materials. While bulk metrics such as lattice spacing and optical bandgap can be consistent with incorporation of chloride into a single phase, these results are not sufficient to fully describe the material as having homogeneous mixing on the X site. This uncertainty motivates the use of a more local probe to study short-range halide coordination and illuminate the role of chloride in triple-halide perovskites. We use cryogenic X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) to characterize lead-halide bonds in a range of single-, double-, and triple-halide perovskite compositions. We show formation of a single-phase triple-halide perovskite whose miscibility is mediated by bromide content. We identify signatures of halide mixing from the Pb L3-edge EXAFS of mixed double- and triple-halide perovskites using both quantitative fits and Cauchy wavelet transforms. Finally, using wavelet transforms of the Br K-edge EXAFS, we demonstrate via forward scattering amplified 3rd shell halide-halide interactions that all three halides coordinate at short range in a fully mixed perovskite phase. These results are a step forward in the understanding of local structure that is required to fully describe and optimize halide incorporation for novel perovskite compositions.

</details>


### [89] [Strain-Mediated Lattice Reconstruction Enhances Ferromagnetism in Cr2Ge2Te6/WTe2 van der Waals Heterobilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13640)

Abstract: Van der Waals (vdW) heterostructures enable tailored electronic and magnetic phases by stacking atomically thin layers with pristine interfaces. Here, we investigate fully 2D Cr2Ge2Te6/WTe2 heterostructures and identify a strong enhancement of ferromagnetism in Cr2Ge2Te6 (CGT). Interface microscopy confirms chemically abrupt vdW interfaces with no detectable interdiffusion, while control experiments rule out processing- or stray-field-induced artifacts. Our experiments and theoretical calculations demonstrate that interfacial charge transfer renders CGT conductive and that proximity-induced lattice distortions in CGT enhance exchange and magnetocrystalline anisotropy. These results establish strain-mediated lattice reconstruction as a strategy for engineering high-temperature magnetic order in 2D heterostructures and clarify that modifications within the magnetic layer itself can govern proximity effects in vdW stacks.

### [90] [A Generalized Method for Spatial Operations on Physical Properties of Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13752)
*Hongjin Xiong,Teng Ma*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物质物理性质通常由受晶体对称性（crystal symmetry）约束的系数矩阵描述，但系数矩阵类型的多样性使得通过简单矩阵乘法进行变换变得复杂。现有方法存在符号繁琐、计算成本高、缺乏直观解释等问题，且随着系数矩阵尺寸增大，传统方法愈发不足。

Method: 提出了一种通用的"输入-系数-输出（input-coefficient-output, ICO）"方法，用于构建适用于各种物理系统中系数矩阵的空间操作矩阵。该方法提供简洁的形式体系，使空间变换的推理更加直观，同时将密集计算委托给计算工具。

Result: ICO方法能够应用于包括高阶非线性光学（high-order nonlinear optics）、弹性力学（elastic mechanics）、电磁学（electricity and magnetism）在内的多种物理系统。该方法类似于费曼图（Feynman diagrams）在物理学中促进理解的作用。

Conclusion: 该方法为未来理论和实验研究提供了有价值的见解，解决了传统方法在处理系数矩阵空间变换时的局限性，特别是在矩阵尺寸增大的情况下。

Abstract: The physical properties of matter are typically described by coefficient matrices governed by crystal symmetry. Applying spatial operations, such as rotation, inversion, and mirror, to these matrices provides an effective approach for investigating material properties. However, the diversity of coefficient matrix types complicates their transformation via simple matrix multiplication, and existing methods suffer from cumbersome notation, high computational cost, and lack of intuitive interpretation. Moreover, as coefficient matrices grow in size, conventional approaches become increasingly inadequate. We present a generalized ``input-coefficient-output (ICO)" approach for constructing spatial operation matrices applicable to coefficient matrices across diverse physical systems, including but not limited to high-order nonlinear optics, elastic mechanics, electricity and magnetism. Our approach offers a concise formalism that enables intuitive reasoning about spatial transformations while delegating intensive computations to computational tools, which is analogous to the role of Feynman diagrams in facilitating understanding in physics. This method also offers valuable insights for future theoretical and experimental research.

Abstract: Chalcogenide perovskites have emerged as promising lead free materials for photovoltaic and thermoelectric applications. Among them, BaZrS3 has attracted particular attention due to its thermal and chemical stability, favorable optoelectronic properties, and low thermal conductivity. Here, we combine molecular dynamics and Monte Carlo simulations based on machine learned interatomic potentials with scanning transmission electron microscopy to investigate mixing thermodynamics and phase stability in the BaZr(S,Se)3 system. We identify an unusual ordered structure that persists at room temperature, most prominently at 33% S, where S and Se atoms form alternating layers within the crystal. Free energy calculations yield the temperature composition phase diagram, including a nonperovskite delta phase in the Se rich limit and a perovskite phase in the S rich limit, separated by a broad two phase region. Analysis of the dielectric function and the absorption coefficient demonstrates that composition, crystal structure, and anion ordering jointly control the optical band gap. ### [92] [Step Bunching and Meandering as Common Growth Modes: A Discrete Model and a Continuum Description](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13821)
*Vassil Ivanov,Vesselin Tonchev,Marta A. Chabowska,Hristina Popova,Magdalena A. Załuska-Kotur*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 台阶聚束与台阶蜿蜒在理解不稳定的台阶流生长（step-flow growth）中存在矛盾，两种不稳定性通常产生独立建模传统。一维框架在两者同时发生时面临根本困难——台阶聚束通常与反向埃利希-施沃贝尔效应（inverted Ehrlich-Schwoebel effect）相关，而台阶蜿蜒则与直接效应相关。关键实验主要关注两个基本极限情况，需要解释两种不稳定性如何在相同生长过程中共存。
