Result: 两种建模方法产生相似图案，并在参数层面建立了联系。连续框架能够探索长时间尺度演化，发现大量表面图案多样性。VicCA模型通过引入适当的势能景观形状，能够复现类似图案。

Conclusion: 研究通过对比两种不同建模方法，成功解释了台阶聚束与台阶蜿蜒在晶体生长过程中的共存机制，克服了传统一维框架的局限性，并在参数层面建立了模型间的联系。

Abstract: The coexistence of step bunching and step meandering remains contradictory in the understanding of the unstable step-flow growth. Considered separately, the two instabilities have generated rich but largely independent modeling traditions. Especially, the one-dimensional framework faces a fundamental difficulty once bunching and meandering occur simultaneously -- step bunching is usually associated with an inverted Ehrlich--Schwoebel effect, whereas step meandering is associated with a direct one. The key experiments also focus mainly on the two basic limiting cases. How, then, can both instabilities coexist within the same growth process once the simultaneous occurrence of bunching and meandering cannot be adequately captured as a simple superposition of the two? In this work, we confront results from two substantially different approaches: a (2+1)D Vicinal Cellular Automaton based model (VicCA) and a differential-difference PDE-based description combining a model of step bunching with a relaxation term in the perpendicular direction. The continuous framework enables to explore long-time scales evolution to find large variety of surface patterns. Introducing a proper shape of the potential energy landscape in the VicCA model produces similar patterns and links both models on the level of parameters.

The MLIP is demonstrated to be highly transferable to large regions of the phase diagram around the compositions included in the dataset. The MLIP is then exploited to simulate the crystallization with phase separation of three Ge-rich alloys on the Ge-Sb$_2$Te$_3$ and Ge- Ge$_2$Sb$_2$Te$_5$ tie-lines that correspond to the set process of the memory cell. ### [95] [Symmetry-protected coexistence of a nodal surface and multiple types of Weyl fermions in $P6_3$-$\text{B}_{30}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13948)
*Xiao-Jing Gao,Yanfeng Ge,Yan Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不同维度拓扑态在单一晶体系统中的共存现象，为探索不同类型费米子激发之间的相互作用提供了独特平台。需要寻找结构稳定且能清晰展现多维拓扑物理的理想材料候选体系。

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与对称性分析（symmetry analysis），研究P6₃-B₃₀的拓扑性质。通过分析时间反演（time-reversal）与二重螺旋对称性（twofold screw symmetry）的组合效应，以及C₆和C₃晶体旋转对称性（crystalline rotational symmetries）的保护机制。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了P6₃-B₃₀作为研究多维混合拓扑费米子物理及其相互作用的理想材料平台。表面态计算显示非平庸费米弧（Fermi arcs）连接相反手性的外尔节点，进一步验证了其拓扑特性。

Abstract: The coexistence of topological states with different dimensionalities in a single crystalline system offers a unique platform to study the interplay of distinct fermionic excitations. Here, integrating first-principles calculations with symmetry analysis, we propose the three-dimensional boron allotrope $P6_3$-$\text{B}_{30}$ as an ideal, structurally stable candidate for exploring multidimensional topological physics. Benefiting from the practically negligible spin-orbit coupling of the light-element framework, $P6_3$-$\text{B}_{30}$ operates as a pristine spinless topological semimetal. We show that the combined time-reversal and twofold screw symmetry ($\mathcal{T}S_{2z}$) enforces a robust two-dimensional nodal surface on the $k_z = π$ plane via a Kramers-like degeneracy. Concurrently, the system hosts a diverse set of zero-dimensional Weyl fermions -- including an unconventional double-Weyl point ($\mathcal{C} = -2$), conventional Type-I WPs ($\mathcal{C} = -1$), and completely tilted Type-II WPs ($\mathcal{C} = +1$) -- emerging at the high-symmetry points $Γ$ and K, as well as along the H-K path, protected by $C_6$ and $C_3$ crystalline rotational symmetries. Crucially, the substantial momentum-space separation between the nodal surface and Weyl points allows for their unambiguous independent resolution. Calculations of the (100) surface states reveal distinct, nontrivial Fermi arcs connecting Weyl nodes of opposite chirality. This work establishes $P6_3$-$\text{B}_{30}$ as a compelling material platform for investigating the physics of multidimensional hybrid topological fermions and their interplay.

</details>


### [96] [Twist-engineering of a robust Quantum Spin Hall phase in $β$-/flat bismuthene bilayer from first principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13960)
*Umberto Pelliccia,Alberto M. Ruiz,Diego López-Alcalá,Gonzalo Abellán,Rafael Gonzalez-Hernandez,José J. Baldoví*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过30°转角堆叠β-铋烯与平面铋烯形成异质结构，利用第一性原理计算发现该结构诱导独特的层间轨道杂化，结合强自旋轨道耦合和自然破缺的反演对称性，产生了显著的Rashba自旋劈裂和增强的量子自旋霍尔相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料的转角工程（twist-engineering）为超越传统应变或化学调控的电子结构调控提供了新途径。第15族（pnictogens）单层材料如铋烯因其强本征自旋轨道耦合（SOC）和稳健的拓扑特性，成为理想的研究平台。

Method: 研究采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），分析30°转角堆叠的β-铋烯单层与平面铋烯层在SiC(0001)衬底上形成的异质结构。通过计算Z2拓扑不变量和自旋霍尔电导（SHC）确认系统的拓扑性质，并探索了锑（Sb）替代的化学可调性。

Result: 特定转角排列诱导了独特的层间轨道杂化，结合强SOC和自然破缺的反演对称性，产生了孤立单层中不存在的显著Rashba自旋劈裂。系统展现出稳健的量子自旋霍尔（QSH）相，其拓扑响应相比单层材料有所增强。通过锑替代逐步降低SOC，能系统性地缩小带隙同时保持非平凡拓扑。

Conclusion: 大转角第15族异质结构为工程化自旋轨道驱动现象和推进拓扑自旋电子学（topological spintronics）提供了一个多功能平台，展示了转角工程在调控拓扑相方面的强大能力。

Abstract: Twist-engineering of topological phases in two-dimensional materials offers a powerful route to modulate electronic structure beyond conventional strain or chemical control. In particular, group 15 (pnictogens) monolayers such as bismuthene provide an ideal platform due to their strong intrinsic spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and robust topological character. Here, we investigate a previously unexplored heterostructure consisting of a $β$-bismuthene monolayer rotated by 30$^\circ$ on a planar bismuthene layer stabilized on a SiC(0001) substrate. Using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that this specific rotational alignment induces a unique interlayer orbital hybridization which, combined with the strong SOC and the naturally broken inversion symmetry, gives rise to a pronounced Rashba spin-splitting, absent in the isolated monolayers. The topological nature of the system is confirmed through the calculation of the Z2 topological invariant and Spin Hall Conductivity (SHC), revealing a robust Quantum Spin Hall (QSH) phase with an enhanced topological response compared to the individual layers. Furthermore, we explore the chemical tunability of this system via Sb substitution, showing that the gradual reduction of SOC systematically narrows the band gap while preserving the non-trivial topology. Our results establish large-angle twisted group 15 heterostructures as a versatile platform for engineering spin-orbit-driven phenomena and advancing topological spintronics.

To address this challenge, we evaluate the role of natural language embeddings capturing the synthesis and testing conditions in enhancing the predictability of glass dissolution. Evaluating the approach on hand-curated ~700 datapoints extracted from the literature, we reveal that the machine learning (ML) model including natural language embeddings (NLP-ML) outperforms classical ML model in predicting glass dissolution rate. Furthermore, we developed a generalizable ML model by transforming the compositional features to structural descriptors of glass alongside NLP-derived features, enabling extrapolation capability to glass compositions with completely new elements absent in the training data. Evaluating this model on a completely new dataset of glass compositions 34 chemical components in contrast to the training dataset that had only 28 components, we demonstrate that the model indeed exhibits generalizability to glass compositions that are out-of-distribution. Altogether, this integrated approach offers a pathway towards high-fidelity glass dissolution prediction and accelerate the discovery of novel glass compositions with tailored durability for sustainable nuclear waste management.

### [99] [Realistic Detector Geometry Modeling and Its Impact on Event Reconstruction in JUNO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13747)
*Zhaoxiang Wu,Miao He,Wuming Luo,Ziyan Deng,Wei He,Yuekun Heng,Xiaoping Jing,Bo Li,Xiaoyan Ma,Xiaohui Qian,Zhonghua Qin,Yifang Wang,Peidong Yu*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: JUNO探测器通过分析PMT实际位置与设计值的偏差，提出几何预测方法，证明探测器变形对能量重建影响可忽略，但几何不准确会导致顶点偏差，通过真实几何模型可消除此偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JUNO探测器旨在实现3%的能量分辨率以确定中微子质量顺序（neutrino mass ordering），但实际安装过程中不锈钢结构变形导致光电倍增管（PMT）位置偏离设计值，需要评估这种几何偏差对探测器性能的影响。

Method: 基于有限的PMT和不锈钢桁架（stainless-steel truss）测量数据，进行相关分析并提出预测所有PMT位置的方法，构建真实几何模型，并将其整合到基于校准的PMT响应模型中。

Result: 探测器变形对能量重建影响可忽略，但几何假设不准确会导致高达40毫米的顶点偏差（vertex biases），将真实几何纳入PMT响应模型可消除此偏差并保持重建算法的稳定性。

Conclusion: JUNO探测器的不锈钢结构安装变形不影响能量重建精度，但准确建模PMT真实几何位置对消除顶点重建偏差至关重要，基于测量的几何预测方法能有效提升重建算法性能。

Abstract: JUNO is designed to determine the neutrino mass ordering with an energy resolution of 3% at 1 MeV. In the real detector, however, deformations of the central stainless-steel structure during installation lead to deviations of the photomultiplier tube (PMT) positions from their design values. Based on the limited survey data of the PMTs and the stainless-steel truss, we perform a correlation analysis of the measured points and propose a method to predict the positions of all PMTs. Using the resulting realistic geometry, we demonstrate that the detector deformation has a negligible effect on the energy reconstruction. In contrast, inaccuracies in the assumed geometry can introduce vertex biases of up to 40 mm. Incorporating the realistic geometry into the calibration-based PMT response model removes this bias and preserves the stability of the reconstruction algorithms.

### [100] [Measuring quasiparticle dynamics for particle impact reconstruction in a superconducting qubit chip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13176)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过统计分析建模辐射诱导的量子比特能量弛豫的时间演化，区分复合（recombination）和俘获（trapping）衰减通道，并采用统计定位方法通过弹道声子传播（ballistic phonon propagation）提取衬底沉积能量。

Result: 精确测量了多个transmon量子比特中的准粒子复合过程，发现了量子比特弛豫动力学对沉积能量的意外依赖性，通过相关弛豫事件与蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）良好吻合地提取了衬底沉积能量。

Abstract: Quasiparticle poisoning following particle impacts poses a significant challenge to the development of fault-tolerant superconducting quantum computers, as a sudden excess of quasiparticles can simultaneously degrade the coherence of multiple qubits across large device arrays. In this work, we present a statistical analysis that models the time evolution of radiation-induced qubit energy relaxation through quasiparticle density dynamics. This study provides insight into quasiparticle loss processes by distinguishing between recombination and trapping decay channels and assessing their respective impact on qubit performance. We precisely measure quasiparticle recombination in multiple transmon qubits and uncover an unexpected dependence of qubit relaxation dynamics on deposited energy. By linking correlated relaxation events across qubits to ballistic phonon propagation, we introduce a statistical localization approach to extract the energy deposited in the substrate, which is in good agreement with Monte Carlo simulation. This work establishes the quantitative framework for using an arbitrary subset of superconducting transmon qubits in a QPU as energy-resolving witness particle detectors.

### [101] [Wandering range of robust quantum symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13894)
*Daniel Burgarth,Paolo Facchi,Marilena Ligabò,Vito Viesti,Kazuya Yuasa*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究哈密顿量鲁棒对称性在扰动下的行为，量化受扰时间演化 $\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{i}t(H+\varepsilon V)} S \mathrm{e}^{-\mathrm{i} t(H+\varepsilon V)}$ 相对于未受扰演化 $\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{i} tH} S\mathrm{e}^{-\mathrm{i} tH} = S$ 的偏离程度。

Method: 引入"游荡范围（wandering range）"作为量化工具，分析该量度与扰动强度$\varepsilon$的标度关系，识别线性标度恢复的条件，并推导显式的非微扰边界（nonperturbative bounds）。

Result: 游荡范围不一定与扰动强度$\varepsilon$呈线性标度关系，但在特定条件下可恢复线性行为，并获得了显式的非微扰边界。

Conclusion: 游荡范围为分析鲁棒对称性在扰动下的行为提供了量化框架，建立了线性标度行为的恢复条件和非微扰边界，深化了对对称性鲁棒性的理解。

Abstract: This paper introduces the concept of the wandering range of a robust symmetry $S$ of a Hamiltonian $H$. This quantity measures how the perturbed time evolution $\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{i}t(H+\varepsilon V)} S \mathrm{e}^{-\mathrm{i} t(H+\varepsilon V)}$ deviates from its unperturbed counterpart $\mathrm{e}^{\mathrm{i} tH} S\mathrm{e}^{-\mathrm{i} tH} = S$. Although the wandering range does not necessarily scale linearly with the perturbation strength $\varepsilon$, we identify conditions under which this linear behavior is recovered and we obtain explicit nonperturbative bounds.

Abstract: Response theory describes the reaction of observales to perturbations in external fields. We review this formalism for quantum fiels in isolation that have unitary time evolution. ### [103] [$κ$-entropic statistical paradigm for relativistic corrections to the Heisenberg principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13697)
*Giuseppe Gaetano Luciano,Jaume Gin\' e,Daniel Chemisana*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海森堡位置-动量不确定性关系是量子力学的基石，但其标准表述与狭义相对论不完全一致。虽然在超相对论区域已取得部分理解，但特别是在中间速度区域仍缺乏全面描述，该区域粒子速度远低于光速但相对论修正预期变得显著，是实验探测量子不确定性相对论修正的最有前景领域。

Method: 采用变分方法，在κ-变形Kaniadakis统计框架下推导了海森堡代数的相对论扩展。该方法基于将最大熵原理应用于Kaniadakis熵，这是由洛伦兹变换自然诱导的Boltzmann-Gibbs-Shannon熵的单参数推广。

Result: 推导了相对论不确定性关系，研究了其物理含义，并从精细结构常数的精密测量中推导出对Kaniadakis参数的约束。同时将本构造与近期文献中讨论的其他扩展进行了比较。

Conclusion: 本文在κ-变形Kaniadakis统计框架下建立了相对论扩展的海森堡代数，为中间速度区域的量子不确定性相对论修正提供了理论描述，并通过实验数据约束了理论参数。

Abstract: The Heisenberg position-momentum uncertainty relation is a cornerstone of quantum mechanics. However, its standard formulation is not fully consistent with special relativity. While partial understanding has been achieved in the ultra-relativistic regime, a comprehensive description is still lacking, particularly in the intermediate velocity domain, where particle speeds remain well below the speed of light yet relativistic corrections are expected to become appreciable. This regime constitutes the most promising arena for experimentally probing relativistic modifications of quantum uncertainty. By adopting a variational approach, in this work we derive a relativistic extension of the Heisenberg algebra within the framework of $κ$-deformed Kaniadakis statistics. The latter emerges from the application of the Maximum Entropy Principle to Kaniadakis entropy, a one-parameter generalization of the Boltzmann-Gibbs-Shannon entropy naturally induced by Lorentz transformations. We investigate the physical implications of the resulting uncertainty relation, deriving constraints on the Kaniadakis parameter from precision measurements of the fine-structure constant and confronting our construction with other extensions discussed in the recent literature.

Motivation: 研究旨在理解如何从量子真空场中有效提取纠缠，特别是探索多个探测器的空间排列如何影响纠缠提取效率，为优化纠缠收集提供理论指导。

Method: 采用微扰理论（perturbation theory）研究质量为零的标量场（massless scalar field）的量子真空，分析由有限数量Unruh-DeWitt探测器组成的子系统间的纠缠提取。

Result: 研究发现领头阶负性（leading-order negativity）完全由约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）的子矩阵决定，子矩阵维度仅随探测器数量线性增长。对于所有三探测器配置和若干对称四探测器配置，推导了负性的解析表达式并确定了最大化纠缠的配置。线性链配置下，提取的纠缠随探测器数量线性增长。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了如何排列多个探测器以优化纠缠提取，并表明增加探测器数量可以扩展能量间隙（energy gaps）和分离距离（separations）的范围，从而增强从场中提取纠缠的能力。

Abstract: We study bipartite entanglement harvesting from the quantum vacuum of a massless scalar field between two subsystems, each composed of a finite number of Unruh-DeWitt detectors. Using perturbation theory, we show that the leading-order negativity is fully determined by a submatrix of the reduced density matrix, with the submatrix dimension scaling only linearly with the number of detectors. Within this framework, we analyze how the detectors' spatial arrangement influences harvesting. For all three-detector configurations and several symmetric four-detector configurations, we derive analytic expressions for the negativity and identify the configurations that maximize it. For a linear chain, we find that the harvested entanglement scales linearly with the number of detectors. These results clarify how to arrange multiple detectors to optimize harvesting and show that increasing their number broadens the ranges of energy gaps and separations over which entanglement can be extracted from the field.

</details>


### [105] [Simulating the dynamics of an SU(2) matrix model on a trapped-ion quantum computer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14094)
*Gavin S. Hartnett,Haoran Liao,Enrico Rinaldi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在离子阱量子计算机上实现了玻色矩阵模型的数字量子模拟，使用Loschmidt回波作为动力学观测量，系统分析了三种误差来源，并展示了新的后选择方案，为更复杂矩阵模型的量子模拟奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵模型（matrix models）在弦论和理论物理中具有重要地位，但模拟其实时非平衡动力学仍是一个根本性挑战。现有方法如哈密顿蒙特卡洛模拟和规范/引力对偶主要研究热平衡态，而自举程序通过施加正定性约束有效确定算符期望值，但实时动力学模拟仍存在困难。

Method: 在Quantinuum System Model H2离子阱量子计算机上执行了首个玻色矩阵模型的数字量子模拟。研究聚焦于具有四次势的SU(2)规范理论，使用Loschmidt回波作为主要动力学观测量，系统分解了三种误差来源：希尔伯特空间截断、Trotter化和硬件噪声。

Result: 展示了一种新的后选择方案，能在Fock基中检测并丢弃规范对称性违反，并与零噪声外推结合在小尺度上提供适度的保真度改进。然而这些方法在当前实现中难以扩展到更大系统尺寸，突显了需要超越现有技术，专注于通过改进编译和幺正合成来减少电路深度，以及运行时错误处理。

Conclusion: 这项工作为将数字量子模拟扩展到更复杂矩阵模型奠定了基础，同时揭示了量子比特资源和电路深度方面的根本性挑战仍然是扩展到全息感兴趣区域的重要障碍。

Abstract: Matrix models are an important class of systems in string theory and theoretical physics, with applications to random matrix theory, quantum chaos, and black holes. Hamiltonian Monte Carlo simulations and gauge/gravity duality have been used to study these systems at thermal equilibrium, and the bootstrap program has been used to efficiently determine operator expectation values by imposing positivity constraints. However, simulating real-time, non-equilibrium dynamics remains a fundamental challenge. In this work, we present the first digital quantum simulation of a bosonic matrix model, executed on the Quantinuum System Model H2 trapped-ion quantum computer. We focus on an $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ gauge theory with a quartic potential as it is simple enough to validate against exact classical solutions and yet complex enough to reflect the non-local structure of larger theories. Using the Loschmidt echo as our primary dynamical observable, we systematically decompose simulation errors into three distinct sources: Hilbert space truncation, Trotterization, and hardware noise. We demonstrate a new post-selection scheme that detects and discards gauge-symmetry violations in the Fock basis and show that at small scales it, along with zero-noise extrapolation, can give modest improvements in fidelity. These approaches struggle to scale to larger system sizes in their current implementations, emphasizing the need to move beyond them and to focus on depth reduction through improved compilation and unitary synthesis, and run-time error handling such as additional error suppression, error detection, as well as error correction approaches. This work establishes a foundation for extending digital quantum simulation to more complex matrix models -- revealing that fundamental challenges in qubit resources and circuit depth remain formidable obstacles for scaling to holographically interesting regimes.

### [107] [Simple slow operators and quantum thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13172)
*Tian-Hua Yang,Sarang Gopalakrishnan,Dmitry A. Abanin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了典型初始态热化（thermalization）与局域算子（local operators）动力学之间的严格关系，通过引入简单慢算子（simple slow operators, SSOs）概念，证明了典型初始态不热化意味着存在近似守恒的SSOs，反之亦然。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立量子多体系统中典型初始态热化现象与算子动力学之间的严格理论联系，为理解热化机制提供新的分析框架。

Method: 方法包括引入简单慢算子（SSOs）概念——与哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）对易子小且具有显著小尺寸分量的算子，以及定义算子相对于态系综的系综方差范数（ensemble variance norm）。对于低纠缠系综，该范数与算子尺寸相关。

Result: 主要结果表明：如果从低复杂度态系综（low-complexity state ensemble）抽取的典型初始态在时间尺度t上不热化，则必然存在在时间尺度t上近似守恒的SSOs。等价地，SSOs的缺失意味着典型初始态会热化。

Conclusion: 结论是通过建立算子增长（operator growth）与热化之间的直接联系，为理解量子多体系统热化行为提供了基于算子动力学的严格理论框架，揭示了典型初始态热化与局域算子动力学之间的本质关系。

Abstract: We establish a rigorous relation between the thermalization of typical initial states and the dynamics of local operators. We introduce a concept of simple slow operators (SSOs), defined as operators that have a small commutator with the Hamiltonian and have significant small-sized components. We show that if typical initial states (drawn from a low-complexity state ensemble) do not thermalize on timescale $t$, then SSOs must exist that are approximately conserved up to timescale $t$. Equivalently, the absence of SSOs implies that typical initial states thermalize. We establish these results by introducing the concept of an ensemble variance norm of an operator, defined as the typical magnitude of the expectation value of that operator with respect to states in the ensemble. For low-entanglement ensembles, the norm is related to operator sizes, allowing us to establish a direct link between operator growth and thermalization.

</details>

*Yangshuo Zhou,Jiao Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于量子踢转子多体相互作用系统的理论分析，通过解析方法研究波包和二分纠缠熵（bipartite entanglement entropy）的动力学行为，并考虑相关势能的对称性（symmetries）影响。

Result: 研究结果揭示了三种不同的动力学区域：二次扩散（quadratic spreading）、周期-2振荡（period-2 oscillation）及其混合态，这些行为由相关势能的对称性所支配。同时阐明了波包动力学与纠缠动力学之间的联系。

Conclusion: 结论表明，基于对称性分析可以理解量子共振态下多体踢转子系统的复杂动力学行为。研究还讨论了高阶共振效应、预测动力学行为的鲁棒性、向多体踢陀螺（many-body kicked tops）的扩展以及与实验研究的相关性。

Abstract: We investigate a many-body interacting system of quantum kicked rotors, where each rotor resides in its respective quantum resonance. Rich many-body dynamics are found to emerge from the interplay between the principal and secondary resonances. In particular, for both the wavepacket and bipartite entanglement entropy, we analytically demonstrate three distinct dynamical regimes -- quadratic spreading (growth), period-2 oscillation, and their hybrid -- governed by the respective symmetries of the relevant potentials. Based on these symmetries, the connection between the wavepacket and the entanglement dynamics is illustrated. Other related issues are also discussed, including higher-order resonance effects, the robustness of the predicted dynamical behaviors, extension to many-body kicked tops, and relevance to experimental studies.

Method: 论文采用综述分析方法，首先介绍不同类型的自旋量子比特实现，包括单电子自旋量子比特（single electron-spin qubits）、空穴自旋量子比特（hole-spin qubits）、施主量子比特（donor qubits）和多自旋编码（multispin encodings）。重点回顾了长程耦合机制的理论基础和实验演示。

Conclusion: 论文最后回顾了利用拓扑自旋纹理（topological spin textures）连接自旋量子比特的最新提案，为自旋量子比特平台的未来发展提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Spin qubits have emerged as a leading platform for quantum information processing due to their long coherence times, small footprint, and compatibility with the existing semiconductor industry. We discuss how the confinement and strain present in semiconductor heterostructures produce addressable levels whose spin degree of freedom can be used to encode a qubit. A large emphasis is placed on reviewing the theoretical foundations and recent experimental demonstrations of proposed mechanisms for long-range coupling, including hybrid approaches based on circuit QED and Andreev qubits, as well as spin shuttling. Finally, we review a recent proposal for linking spin qubits using topological spin textures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We develop a Melnikov framework for the Kuramoto Sivashinsky (KS) equation under weak deterministic and stochastic forcing. By treating KS as an infinite dimensional dynamical system, we derive a Melnikov functional that measures splitting of stable and unstable manifolds of a homoclinic orbit. Periodic forcing leads to phase dependent transverse intersections, while stochastic forcing produces random manifold splitting characterized by a variance determined by the adjoint solution. This provides a geometric mechanism linking invariant manifold theory to spatiotemporal chaos in dissipative partial differential equations.

### [113] [Lagrangian correspondences for moduli spaces of Higgs bundles and holomorphic connections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14127)
*Panagiotis Dimakis,Duong Dinh,Shengjing Xu*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文在亏格≥2的紧连通黎曼曲面C上，构造了秩n希格斯丛（Higgs bundles）模空间与T*C点希尔伯特概形（Hilbert schemes）之间的拉格朗日对应（Lagrangian correspondences），以及全纯联络（holomorphic connections）模空间与C的扭余切丛（twisted cotangent bundles）之间的对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立几何朗兰兹对应（geometric Langlands correspondence）的具体实现。作者旨在通过构造拉格朗日对应来理解Dolbeault几何朗兰兹对应，并期望通过量子化实现de Rham几何朗兰兹对应。

Method: 方法的核心是构造与线子丛（line subbundles）横截（transversal）的希格斯丛和全纯联络。这些构造自然地诱导出C上的除子（divisors）以及辅助参数：对于希格斯丛是谱曲线（spectral curves）上除子的提升，对于全纯联络是表观奇点（apparent singularities）的留数参数。

Result: 主要结果是成功构造了上述拉格朗日对应。这些对应为理解几何朗兰兹对应提供了具体框架，并建立了与Kapustin-Witten方程约化（reductions）、共形极限（conformal limit）、变量分离（separation of variables）以及共形场论（conformal field theories）中退化场（degenerate fields）等主题的联系。

Conclusion: 结论表明Dolbeault几何朗兰兹对应可由这些拉格朗日对应一般性地实现，而de Rham几何朗兰兹对应有望通过Drinfeld的Hecke特征层（Hecke eigensheaves）构造的量子化来实现。该工作为几何朗兰兹纲领提供了新的几何实现途径。

Abstract: On a compact connected Riemann surface $C$ of genus at least $2$, we construct Lagrangian correspondences between moduli spaces of rank-$n$ Higgs bundles (respectively, holomorphic connections) and the Hilbert schemes of points on $T^\ast C$ (respectively, the twisted cotangent bundles of $C$). Central to these constructions are Higgs bundles (respectively, holomorphic connections) which are transversal to line subbundles of the underlying bundles: these naturally induce divisors on $C$ together with auxiliary parameters, namely lifts to divisors on spectral curves for Higgs bundles and residue parameters of apparent singularities for holomorphic connections. We discuss the evidence showing that the Dolbeault geometric Langlands correspondence is generically realized by these Lagrangian correspondences; we expect that the de Rham geometric Langlands correspondence can be realized by their quantization, following Drinfeld's construction of Hecke eigensheaves. We also discuss the relations of our constructions to various topics, including reductions of Kapustin-Witten equations, the conformal limit, separation of variables, and degenerate fields in conformal field theories.

</details>


### [114] [Deformations of fibered Calabi--Yau varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14024)
*Benjamin Bakker,Kristin DeVleming,Stefano Filipazzi,Radu Laza,Jennifer Li,Roberto Svaldi,Chengxi Wang,Junyan Zhao*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文将Kollár关于椭圆纤维化光滑K-挠性簇小形变的结果推广到任意纤维化光滑K-挠性簇，并进一步证明在无上同调假设下，光滑K-挠性簇上半丰富线丛的小形变在同调等价意义下保持半丰富性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kollár先前证明了在$H^2(X,\mathcal{O}_X)=0$条件下，椭圆纤维化光滑K-挠性（K-torsion）簇的小形变保持椭圆纤维化结构。本文旨在将此结果推广到更一般的纤维化情形，并探索无上同调假设下的形变性质。

Method: 采用Hodge理论（Hodge theoretic）技术和Kawamata-Ran的$T^1$-提升准则（$T^1$-lifting criterion），处理光滑K-挠性簇的形变问题。该方法允许在更一般的纤维化框架下分析形变行为。

Result: 证明了对于任意满足$H^2(X,\mathcal{O}_X)=0$条件的纤维化光滑K-挠性簇，其小形变（small deformations）仍保持纤维化结构。更一般地，即使无上同调假设，光滑K-挠性簇上半丰富线丛（semiample line bundle）的小形变在同调等价（homological equivalence）意义下仍保持半丰富性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功扩展了Kollár关于椭圆纤维化形变的结果，建立了更一般的纤维化光滑K-挠性簇形变理论。通过Hodge理论和$T^1$-提升准则，证明了半丰富线丛的形变稳定性，为代数几何中的形变理论提供了新的工具和视角。

Abstract: Kollár showed that small deformations of elliptically fibered smooth $K$-torsion varieties with $H^2(X,\mathcal{O}_X)=0$ remain elliptically fibered. We extend this result to any fibered smooth $K$-torsion variety $X$ with $H^2(X,\mathcal{O}_X)=0$, using Hodge theoretic techniques and the $T^1$-lifting criterion of Kawamata--Ran. More generally, our strategy implies that even without the cohomological assumption, small deformations of a semiample line bundle on a smooth $K$-torsion variety remain semiample up to homological equivalence.

### [115] [Black holes in general relativity coupled with NEDs surrounded by PFDM: thermodynamics, epicyclic oscillations, QPOs, and shadow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13140)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Sardor Murodov,Bekzod Rahmatov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了浸没在完美流体暗物质（PFDM）环境中的正则黑洞的热力学性质与中性测试粒子动力学，通过准周期振荡（QPO）观测数据约束黑洞参数，并探讨了黑洞阴影的光学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索浸没在完美流体暗物质（perfect fluid dark matter, PFDM）环境中的正则黑洞（regular black hole）的热力学性质与粒子动力学行为，以理解此类黑洞系统的稳定性、物理行为及其潜在观测特征。

Method: 首先分析视界结构和关键热力学量（如霍金温度（Hawking temperature）和比热容（specific heat capacity））。随后采用哈密顿形式主义（Hamiltonian formalism）研究中性测试粒子动力学，推导有效势（effective potential），并基于此分析准周期振荡（quasiperiodic oscillations, QPOs）的星周频率（epicyclic frequencies）。最后，利用XTE J1550-564等源的QPO观测数据进行马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）分析以约束参数，并研究黑洞阴影（black hole shadow）。

Result: 研究获得了约束后的黑洞质量、磁荷参数（magnetic charge parameter）、PFDM参数以及特征轨道半径（characteristic orbital radius）。分析揭示了黑洞阴影的光学外观如何受各种几何参数影响，凸显了此类黑洞及其暗物质环境的潜在观测特征。

Conclusion: 该工作系统地研究了PFDM环境中正则黑洞的热力学、粒子动力学及观测特征。通过结合理论分析与观测数据约束，揭示了暗物质环境对黑洞性质及其可观测现象（如QPOs和阴影）的影响，为通过天文观测探测此类黑洞及其暗物质晕提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the thermodynamics and motion of neutral test particles around a regular black hole immersed in a perfect fluid dark matter environment. We begin by examining the horizon structure and key thermodynamic properties, with particular emphasis on quantities such as the Hawking temperature and the specific heat capacity. These aspects provide important insight into the stability and physical behavior of the black hole system. We then proceed to analyze the dynamics of neutral test particles using the Hamiltonian formalism, through which we derive the effective potential governing particle motion. Using the effective potential, we further study quasiperiodic oscillations by determining the associated epicyclic frequencies and comparing them with available observational data. Using the observed QPO data of XTE J1550-564, GRO J1655-40, GRS 1915+105, and M82 X-1, we perform a Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis to constrain the black hole mass, the magnetic charge parameter, the PFDM parameter, and the characteristic orbital radius. Finally, we investigate the black hole shadow and demonstrate how various geometric parameters influence its optical appearance. This analysis highlights the potential observational signatures of such black holes and their surrounding dark matter environment.

### [116] [Classical Spinors on Curved Spacetime: applications to Cosmology and Astrophysics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13143)
*Andrea La Delfa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Magueijo等人提出的旋量模型在宇宙学背景下的行为，发现该模型在不同条件下可分别描述暗物质和暗能量的背景行为。研究还探讨了旋量流体的宇宙学扰动和球对称晕问题，揭示了处理扰动时的困难以及模型在描述球对称天体时的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是深入分析Magueijo等人提出的旋量模型在宇宙学背景下的行为，探讨该模型能否描述暗物质（DM）和暗能量（DE）的宇宙学演化，并研究其扰动行为和球对称结构的适用性。

Method: 研究采用多种数学方法：首先将旋量流体的能量-动量张量（SET）重新表述为完美流体形式；然后采用SVT分解和(1+3)-分解方法处理宇宙学标量扰动；最后利用Fabbri等人的结果和旋量的极坐标形式，分析球对称时空中的旋量流体行为。

Result: 研究发现旋量模型在不同条件下可分别描述暗物质和暗能量的背景行为。在宇宙学扰动方面，研究获得了压力扰动的绝热声速表达式，但发现直接处理扰动非常困难。对于球对称晕，研究证明旋量流体的能量-动量张量各分量通常都不为零，这引发了模型描述球对称天体的适用性问题。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了旋量模型在宇宙学背景下的多方面行为，揭示了模型在描述暗物质和暗能量背景演化方面的潜力，但也指出了在处理宇宙学扰动和球对称结构时面临的数学困难和适用性挑战。

Abstract: We focus our attention on the spinor model proposed in an article by J. Magueijo et al. and we analyze it from the point of view of the cosmological background. We show that this model, under some conditions, can well-describe the background behavior of DM and, under other conditions, the behavior of DE. Furthermore, we show that the SET of the spinorial fluid, in the context of the cosmological background, can be recast in the form of that of a Perfect Fluid whose four-velocity is given by the normalized vector current density. Successively, we concentrate on the analysis of the scalar cosmological perturbations of this model, following the usual SVT Decomposition approach. We show that the treatment of cosmological perturbations is very difficult and cannot be done directly. Due to this fact, we tackle the problem with another method: the (1+3)-decomposition. We prove that we can further decompose the SET of a spinorial fluid, thanks to the presence of the axial current density. Employing the results found in an article by L. Fabbri et al. and the polar form of spinors, we show how the thermodynamical quantities that characterize the spinorial fluid can be written in terms of the four-velocity, the normalized axial current density, the chiral angle, and the projector on the hyperplane orthogonal to the first two. Moreover, in the context of scalar perturbations, we obtain an expression for the adiabatic speed of sound of the pressure perturbation in terms of the parameters that characterize the spinorial field written in polar form. In the end, we tackle the problem of spherically symmetric halos surrounding galaxies by analyzing the behavior of the SET of the spinorial fluid in a spherically symmetric space-time. We prove that, in general, none of its components vanish, giving rise to the problem of the suitability of the model for the description of spherically symmetric objects.

</details>


### [117] [Bilinear products and the orthogonality of quasinormal modes on hyperboloidal foliations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13182)
*Marica Minucci,Rodrigo Panosso Macedo,Christiana Pantelidou,Laura Sberna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了双曲叶层上黑洞准正则模（QNMs）的双线性积性质，发现虽然QNM解在双曲叶上是光滑有限的，但正交性双线性形式的被积函数仍然发散。作者提出了几种正则化方法以获得有限的双线性形式，并讨论了包含通量贡献的替代定义。最后在双曲框架下定义了QNM激发因子和系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞准正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）在双曲叶层（hyperboloidal foliations）上的双线性积（bilinear products）性质。尽管QNM解在双曲叶上是光滑有限的，但正交性双线性形式的被积函数仍然发散，需要解决这一理论问题。

Method: 在施瓦西时空（Schwarzschild family of spacetimes）的标量扰动背景下，采用双曲叶层框架研究QNMs。提出了几种正则化（regularisation）程序来处理双线性积的发散问题，并探讨了包含通量贡献（flux contributions）的替代定义方法。

Result: 发现双线性形式的被积函数发散源于定义中所需的反射（reflection）或CPT变换，该变换改变了被积函数在边界的行为。提出的正则化方法能够获得有限且定义良好的双线性形式。对于特定模数和常数初始数据，明确计算了QNM激发因子（excitation factors）和系数。

Conclusion: 在双曲叶层框架下，通过适当的正则化程序可以建立有限的双线性积，为黑洞准正则模的正交性和激发因子计算提供了理论基础。包含通量贡献的替代定义虽然有其优势，但也存在局限性。

Abstract: We explore the properties of bilinear products for black-hole quasinormal modes (QNMs) formulated on hyperboloidal foliations. We find that, although QNM solutions are smooth and finite on future-directed hyperboloids, the integrand of the bilinear form with respect to which the modes are orthogonal is still divergent. This is a result of the reflection (equivalently, CPT) transformation required in the definition of the products, which modifies the behaviour of the integrand at the boundaries. We present several regularisation procedures that yield a finite and well-defined bilinear form. In addition, we examine an alternative definition of the bilinear products that incorporates flux contributions, discussing its advantages and limitations. Finally, we define the QNM excitation factors and coefficients within the hyperboloidal framework in terms of the bilinear products, and compute them explicitly for a choice of mode numbers and constant initial data. For concreteness, we work with the QNMs associated to scalar perturbations of the Schwarzschild family of spacetimes.

</details>


### [118] [Uniqueness of stationary axisymmetric type D black holes with non-aligned electromagnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13202)
*Hryhorii Ovcharenko,Jiri Podolsky*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了Ovcharenko-Podolsky时空的唯一性：首先证明共形到Carter度规是满足特定几何条件的唯一可能形式，然后在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中证明该度规的唯一非平凡解就是2025年发现的Ovcharenko-Podolsky类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在证明作者近期发现的Ovcharenko-Podolsky时空的唯一性，通过两个层面的论证：首先从纯几何角度证明度规形式的唯一性，然后在具体物理理论中证明解的唯一性。

Method: 采用两个步骤的证明方法：首先在无场方程的一般几何框架下，证明共形到Carter度规（conformal-to-Carter metric）是满足特定几何条件的唯一可能形式；然后在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论（Einstein-Maxwell theory）中，分析该度规下的电磁真空解。

Result: 主要结果包括：1) 共形到Carter度规是满足Weyl类型D、测地主零方向（PNDs）无剪切且正交于极方向、特定1-form闭合等条件的唯一可能形式；2) 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中，完全非对齐且非零电磁场的唯一非平凡解是Ovcharenko-Podolsky类，而对齐电磁场的唯一解是1976年的Plebański-Demiański类。

Conclusion: 本文严格证明了Ovcharenko-Podolsky时空的唯一性，这一结果具有普适性，不依赖于特定场方程，因此可能在各种替代引力理论中找到有趣应用。

Abstract: We demonstrate the uniqueness of the spacetimes recently found by us in [H. Ovcharenko and J. Podolsky, Phys. Rev. D 112 (2025) 064076]. First, we prove that the conformal-to-Carter metric ansatz we used therein is the only possible for stationary axisymmetric geometries that are of Weyl type D, with geodesic and shear-free principal null directions (PNDs) which are orthogonal to polar directions, and whose specific 1-form $θ$ is closed. Because this result is general, without employing any field equations, such conformal-to-Carter metric may find interesting applications also in various alternative theories of gravity. Then, we show that in the Einstein-Maxwell theory the only non-trivial electrovacuum solution for the conformal-to-Carter metric with the fully non-aligned and non-null electromagnetic field is the Ovcharenko-Podolsky class found in 2025. Complementarily, the only solution with the double-aligned and non-null electromagnetic field is the Plebański-Demiański class found in 1976.

</details>


### [119] [Axial Oscillations of Viscous Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13208)
*Sofía Bussières,Jaime Redondo-Yuste,José Javier Ortega Gómez,Vitor Cardoso*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究利用相对论流体力学的新理论框架，首次系统地研究了致密星体振荡模式中粘性（viscosity）的作用，发现了无完美流体对应物的新粘性驱动模式族，并揭示了模式避免（mode avoidance）现象和长寿命模式谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恒星振荡模式在观测和恒星稳定性理解中具有重要作用，但迄今为止对致密星体振荡模式中粘性（viscosity）的作用理解非常有限，缺乏一个完善的理论框架。

Method: 利用最近在因果稳定相对论流体力学（relativistic hydrodynamics）理论构建方面的突破，研究中子星（neutron stars）的振荡模式，特别关注轴向谱（axial spectrum）的特征分析。

Result: 发现了新的、无完美流体对应物的粘性驱动模式族（viscosity-driven families of modes），揭示了某些模式族中的模式避免（mode avoidance）现象，并识别出长寿命模式谱（spectrum of long-lived modes）。

Conclusion: 这些新发现的粘性驱动模式及其特征（特别是长寿命模式）在天体物理动力学过程中的作用尚待进一步理解，为致密星体振荡研究提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The oscillation modes of stars play an important role in observations, and on the understanding of stellar stability properties. The role of viscosity in the oscillation modes of compact stars has been so far understood very loosely only, in absence of a well posed framework. We use recent breakthroughs in the formulation of a causal and stable theory of relativistic hydrodynamics, to study oscillation modes of neutron stars. We characterize the axial spectrum of compact stars and uncover new, viscosity-driven families of modes, without a perfect fluid counterpart. Our results show mode avoidance in some of these families, and a spectrum of long-lived modes, whose role in astrophysical, dynamical processes is yet to be understood.

### [120] [Observational constraints on nonlocal black holes via gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13223)
*Rocco D'Agostino,Vittorio De Falco*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了修正Deser-Woodard非局部引力理论中DD黑洞的引力透镜效应，通过弱偏转和强偏转极限下的偏转角分析、透镜可观测量约束以及费舍尔信息矩阵联合统计检验，发现DD黑洞参数与广义相对论在1.13σ水平一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过引力透镜效应分析DD黑洞（Deser-Woodard非局部引力理论中的扰动解）的特性，以探测爱因斯坦引力理论的偏离。该工作首次评估DD参数空间，并为未来更大数据集下的引力理论检验提供新见解。

Method: 首先推导了弱偏转（weak-deflection）和强偏转（strong-deflection）极限下偏转角的一般解析表达式，明确关联了非局部修正与施瓦西时空（Schwarzschild geometry）的关系。随后分析透镜可观测量（lensing observables），包括后牛顿效应（post-Newtonian effects）和黑洞阴影（black hole shadow），利用当前观测界限约束DD黑洞参数空间。最后基于费舍尔信息矩阵（Fisher information matrix）进行联合统计分析，结合先前从准正规模（quasinormal modes）获得的约束。

Result: 研究结果表明DD黑洞参数与广义相对论（general relativity）在1.13σ水平一致。通过引力透镜效应分析成功约束了DD参数空间，并为未来更大数据集下的引力理论偏离探测提供了定量基准。

Conclusion: 该工作首次系统评估了修正Deser-Woodard非局部引力理论中DD黑洞的参数空间，通过多观测手段联合分析证实了与广义相对论的高度一致性。研究为利用未来更大数据集探测爱因斯坦引力理论的偏离提供了新的分析框架和见解。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the gravitational lensing around the static and spherically symmetric DD black holes, which we recently derived as perturbations of the Schwarzschild geometry within the revised Deser-Woodard theory of nonlocal gravity. We first present general analytical expressions for the deflection angle in both weak- and strong-deflection limits, explicitly relating them to the nonlocal corrections to Schwarzschild spacetime. Subsequently, we analyze lensing observables, such as the post-Newtonian effects and the black hole shadow, to constrain the DD black hole parameter space using current observational bounds. Finally, we perform a joint statistical analysis based on the Fisher information matrix, combining these findings with our previously obtained constraints from quasinormal modes. Our results indicate consistency with general relativity at the $1.13σ$ level. This work provides a first assessment of the DD parameter space and offers new insights to probe deviations from Einstein's gravity in view of future larger datasets.

</details>


### [121] [On the Ghost-Free Conditions of Extended Hybrid Metric-Palatini Gravity with Ricci-Squared Invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13360)
*Jonathan Ramírez,Gustavo Melgarejo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了混合度规-帕拉蒂尼理论（hybrid metric-Palatini theory），该理论包含度规和帕拉蒂尼标量曲率及其二次里奇不变量。通过线性化分析，识别了理论中的额外自旋-2和自旋-0模式，并确定了消除鬼态（ghost）的代数条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立系统框架来评估扩展混合度规-帕拉蒂尼引力理论的理论一致性。研究混合度规-仿射结构（mixed metric-affine structure）产生的额外模式及其稳定性条件。

Method: 推导了任意函数$f(R,\mathcal{R},\mathcal{R}_{μν}R^{μν},R_{μν}R^{μν},\mathcal{R}_{(μν)}\mathcal{R}^{(μν)})$对应的场方程，并在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）周围进行线性化分析。通过计算引力子传播子（graviton propagator）识别理论中的动力学内容。

Result: 研究表明，里奇平方项（Ricci-squared terms）通常会产生有质量的自旋-2鬼态（massive spin-2 ghost）。确定了消除该鬼态所需的背景导数代数条件，仅保留健康的标量激发（healthy scalar excitations）。多个相关子类（包括混合$f(R,\mathcal{R})$、$f(\mathcal{R},\mathcal{R}_{(μν)}\mathcal{R}^{(μν)})$等）的无鬼态和无快子（tachyon-free）条件以统一方式获得。

Conclusion: 本文为评估扩展混合度规-帕拉蒂尼引力理论的理论一致性建立了系统框架。该框架能够统一处理多种极限情况，包括纯度规$f(R)$和帕拉蒂尼$f(\mathcal{R})$情形。

Abstract: We consider a hybrid metric-Palatini theory whose action depends on the metric and Palatini scalar curvatures, together with the corresponding quadratic Ricci invariants, through an arbitrary function $f(R,\mathcal{R},\mathcal{R}_{μν}R^{μν},R_{μν}R^{μν},\mathcal{R}_{(μν)}\mathcal{R}^{(μν)})$. We derive the associated field equations and linearize them around Minkowski spacetime in order to analyze the dynamical content of the theory. This formulation allows us to compute the graviton propagator and to identify the additional spin-2 and spin-0 modes generated by the mixed metric-affine structure. We show that, in general, the Ricci-squared terms give rise to a massive spin-2 ghost, and we determine the algebraic conditions on the background derivatives of $f$ required to eliminate it, leaving only healthy scalar excitations. Several relevant subclasses -- including hybrid $f(R,\mathcal{R})$, $f(\mathcal{R},\mathcal{R}_{(μν)}\mathcal{R}^{(μν)})$, $f(R,\mathcal{R}_{(μν)}\mathcal{R}^{(μν)})$, and the purely metric $f(R)$ and Palatini $f(\mathcal{R})$ cases -- are recovered as limiting regimes, and their ghost- and tachyon-free conditions are obtained in a unified way. Altogether, this establishes a systematic framework for assessing the theoretical consistency of extended hybrid metric-Palatini gravity theories.

</details>


### [122] [Exact rotating dilatonic branch in ModMax electrodynamics without Maxwell analogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13490)
*Leonel Bixano,Tonatiuh Matos*

Abstract: We present a novel class of rotating dilatonic solutions within the framework of Einstein-ModMax-type gravity. The configuration belongs to the nonlinear sector characterized by $\mathcal F/\mathcal G=\mathrm{const}$ and carries nontrivial electric and magnetic potentials, with both $A_t$ and $A_\varphi$ turned on, together with a nontrivial gravitomagnetic structure. We show that this solution does not admit continuation to the Maxwell framework of our parametrization, so it is intrinsically tied to the nonlinear ModMax regime. Moreover, in the prolate sector we identify a genuine black-hole regime in which the exterior region satisfies the null energy condition while the curvature singularity remains hidden behind the event horizon. These results provide an exact rotating dilatonic ModMax configuration with no Maxwell analog and a physically well-behaved exterior black-hole sector.

### [123] [Probing Kalb-Ramond gravity with charged rotating black holes: constraints from EHT observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13494)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 利用EHT测量的角阴影直径，并结合恒星动力学质量先验（stellar dynamics mass prior），从Sgr A*数据中得到了洛伦兹破缺参数ℓ的上限约束：ℓ ≲ 0.19。这为检验KR引力等修改引力理论提供了重要的观测限制。

Abstract: The Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) has guided strong-field gravitational physics by providing the first direct images of the supermassive black holes M87* and Sagittarius A*. The EHT observations offer unprecedented opportunities to test modified gravity theories against general relativity (GR). Motivated by this, we investigate charged rotating black holes in KR gravity, a framework motivated by string theory that incorporates spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking. The spacetime geometry is characterized by a Lorentz--violating parameter $\ell$ and electric charge $Q$, which modify the Kerr--Newman metric through a radial-dependent mass function. We compute black hole shadows and derive constraints on $\ell$ and $Q$ using EHT observations of M87* and Sgr A*. For angular shadow diameter $θ_{\rm sh}$ of Sgr A* at inclination $θ_o=50^\circ$ and fixed $Q=0.2$, the corresponding EHT-allowed range $θ_{\rm sh}\in(41.7,\,55.7)\,μ\mathrm{as}$ permits approximately $-0.075\lesssim\ell\lesssim0.110$ and $-0.124\lesssim\ell\lesssim0.076$ across the admissible spin interval. Our analysis reveals that the Lorentz-violating parameter suppresses the shadow radius by a factor $\sqrt{1-\ell}$, while charge introduces additional distortions. Using the angular shadow diameter measured by EHT, we obtain an upper bound $\ell \lesssim 0.19$ from Sgr A* data with the stellar dynamics mass prior.

### [124] [Quasinormal Modes of pp-Wave Spacetimes and Zero Temperature Dissipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13516)
*Huayu Dai,Guangtao Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文计算了Kaigorodov pp-wave时空上标量扰动的准正规模（quasinormal mode）谱，这是零温零流体（zero temperature null fluids）的无视界引力对偶。研究发现pp-wave变形将Poincaré视界转变为不规则奇点，作为几何吸收体产生无熵、无视界的零温耗散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括解析计算标量扰动在Kaigorodov pp-wave时空上的准正规模谱。通过分析径向方程，发现pp-wave变形将r=0处的Poincaré视界提升为秩为(d+2)/2的不规则奇点（irregular singular point），该奇点作为几何吸收体。对于d=2（极端BTZ黑洞）情况，径向方程简化为Whittaker方程；对于d≥3情况，进行数值谱计算。

Result: 主要结果包括：对于d=2（极端BTZ）获得精确的非耗散谱Im(ω)=0；对于d≥3，所有模式满足Im(ω_n)<0，证实了无视界、无熵的零温耗散。零阶近似下径向方程变为阶数μ=d/(d+2)的Bessel方程，证明所有标量准正规模都存在能隙（gapped）。d=3,4,5的数值谱显示离散耗散塔并确认线性稳定性。

Conclusion: 结论表明，Kaigorodov pp-wave时空中的不规则奇点可以作为几何吸收体，实现无需视界或熵的零温耗散。这扩展了我们对引力系统中耗散机制的理解，揭示了无视界几何中也可能存在耗散现象。

Abstract: We compute the quasinormal mode spectrum of scalar perturbations on Kaigorodov pp-wave spacetimes, the horizonless gravity duals of zero temperature null fluids. The pp-wave deformation promotes the Poincaré horizon at $r=0$ to an irregular singular point of rank $(d+2)/2$, which acts as a geometric absorber for ingoing waves: rank~$0$ corresponds to thermal dissipation, rank~$1$ to quantum-critical (extremal black hole), and rank~$\geq 2$ to gapped, horizonless dissipation. For $d=2$ (extremal BTZ) the radial equation reduces to the Whittaker equation with exact non-dissipative spectrum $\mathrm{Im}(ω)=0$; for $d \geq 3$ all modes satisfy $\mathrm{Im}(ω_n) < 0$, establishing zero temperature dissipation without horizon or entropy. At zeroth order the radial equation becomes Bessel's equation of order $μ=d/(d+2)$, proving all scalar QNMs are gapped. Numerical spectra for $d=3,4,5$ yield a discrete dissipative tower and confirm linear stability.

### [125] [Topologically equivalent yet radiatively distinct orbits in EMRI system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13564)
*Chao-Hui Wang,Shao-Wen Wei,Tao Zhu,Yu-Xiao Liu*

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在广义相对论之外的某些奇异致密天体（如双荷黑洞）中，存在多个势阱允许不同束缚轨道族共存的现象。这些轨道虽然具有相同的拓扑指数，但会产生辐射特性不同的引力波信号，为探测超越广义相对论的强场引力动力学提供了直接观测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法以双荷黑洞（dyonic black hole）为代表案例，分析其多势阱几何结构如何支持多个共存束缚轨道分支。通过比较具有相同有理旋转数（rational rotation number）和拓扑指数的周期轨道，研究它们在极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals）过程中的引力波辐射特性差异。

Result: 研究结果表明，虽然这些周期轨道具有相同的拓扑指数，但它们在代表性极端质量比旋近过程中会产生辐射特性不同（radiatively distinct）的引力波。不同轨道分支跨越时空曲率的不同区域，导致其振幅调制和谐波含量存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 这些"拓扑等价但波形可区分"（topologically equivalent yet waveform-distinguishable）的特征为探测超越广义相对论的强场引力动力学提供了直接观测探针。这种差异可能被未来的天基引力波探测器（space-based gravitational wave detectors）观测到，从而验证奇异致密天体的存在。

Abstract: Multiple potential wells for massive test particles, allowing distinct families of bound orbits to coexist, are a characteristic feature of certain exotic compact objects beyond general relativity. Taking the dyonic black hole as a representative example, we demonstrate that such multi-well geometries generically support multiple coexisting branches of bound orbits, in contrast to the single-branch behavior observed in the Schwarzschild spacetime. Crucially, the periodic orbits sharing identical rational rotation number, and hence identical topological indices can nevertheless produce \emph{radiatively distinct} gravitational waves in a representative extreme-mass-ratio inspirals: their amplitude modulation and harmonic content differ because each branch spans different regions of spacetime curvature. These ``topologically equivalent yet waveform-distinguishable'' signatures provide a direct observational probe of strong field gravitational dynamics beyond general relativity, potentially accessible to future space-based gravitational wave detectors.

Conclusion: KAGRA的加入显著增强了全球引力波探测器网络的性能，即使是一个中等灵敏度的探测器也能通过几何互补性提供重要贡献。这些结果强调了地理分布式网络对于多信使引力波天文学的重要性，KAGRA在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA网络中发挥着关键作用。

Abstract: The addition of KAGRA to the global gravitational-wave detector network introduces new baselines and complementary antenna response patterns that can enhance sky localization for compact binary coalescences. We investigate KAGRA's role in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network using a systematic injection study of binary neutron star signals. Sky maps are constructed with a radiometric, coherence-based framework, allowing isolation of geometric and timing contributions from individual detectors. Localization performance is quantified using the fraction of events localized within $100~\mathrm{deg}^2$, cumulative area distributions, and the median $90%$ credible region.
  We also assess KAGRA's impact on detection rates by varying its sensitivity over a wide range. Even at its current sensitivity of $\sim10~\mathrm{Mpc}$, KAGRA provides measurable improvements by breaking degeneracies through additional baselines and directional constraints. As sensitivity increases, improvements in signal-to-noise ratio and timing precision lead to substantial reductions in localization area. We identify a binary neutron star range of $\sim30~\mathrm{Mpc}$ as a practical benchmark for reliable localization suitable for electromagnetic follow-up, noting this as a conservative estimate.
  In addition, KAGRA increases the number of detectable events by enabling lower signal-to-noise detections. These results demonstrate that even a modest-sensitivity detector can significantly enhance network performance through geometric complementarity, highlighting the importance of a geographically distributed network for multimessenger gravitational-wave astronomy.

Abstract: We develop an analytic eikonal description of perturbations for four-dimensional regular black holes in quasi-topological gravity. Using first-order Schutz--Will WKB together with a small-coupling expansion and a large-$\ell$ expansion, we obtain closed quasinormal-mode formulas with explicit dependence on the black-hole parameters $(M,μ,ν,α)$. We then map the same geodesic invariants $(Ω_{\text{ph}},λ_{\text{ph}})$ to shadow and strong-lensing observables, deriving an explicit QNM--shadow--lensing correspondence. In this way, ringdown frequencies, shadow scale, and strong-deflection observables are unified in one analytic scheme for this quasi-topological family.

### [128] [Scalarizations of magnetized Reissner-Nordström black holes induced by parity-violating and parity-preserving interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13614)
*Hao-Jie Lin,Tao Zhu,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在磁化Reissner-Nordström时空中，由宇称破坏和宇称守恒相互作用引发的标量场自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization）。通过分析外部磁场对不同相互作用通道中标量化阈值的影响，揭示了磁场对宇称破坏和宇称守恒相互作用诱导的标量化具有本质不同的影响方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究外部磁场如何影响由宇称破坏（parity-violating）和宇称守恒（parity-preserving）相互作用诱导的标量场自发标量化。特别关注电磁Chern-Simons、引力Chern-Simons和高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet）不变量三种耦合机制在磁化背景下的行为差异。

Method: 在解耦极限（decoupling limit）下工作时，采用时域演化方法研究标量扰动，确定引发快子不稳定性（tachyonic instability）的临界耦合。通过比较相同磁化背景中不同相互作用通道的行为，分析外部磁场对标量化阈值的影响。

Result: 研究发现磁场降低了电磁和引力Chern-Simons通道中的标量化阈值。在高斯-博内通道中，效应分为两支：在负α分支（标准GB⁺分支）中，临界耦合的幅值随磁场增加；在正α分支（GB⁻分支）中，临界耦合随磁场减小但在磁场消失极限下发散。磁场还修改了晚期动力学并产生类Melvin模式，非线性耦合将线性理论的无限增长替换为有界振荡演化。

Conclusion: 外部磁场以本质上不同的方式影响宇称破坏和宇称守恒相互作用诱导的标量化，揭示了高斯-博内两支之间的显著不对称性。这些结果表明磁场在标量化现象中扮演着复杂而重要的角色，其影响机制依赖于相互作用的宇称特性。

Abstract: We study spontaneous scalarization of a scalar field in the magnetized Reissner--Nordström spacetime induced by parity-violating and parity-preserving interactions, represented by couplings to the electromagnetic Chern--Simons, gravitational Chern--Simons, and Gauss--Bonnet invariants, respectively. Working in the decoupling limit, we evolve scalar perturbations in the time domain and determine the critical coupling for the onset of tachyonic instability. This allows us to compare, within the same magnetized background, how the external magnetic field affects scalarization induced by parity-violating and parity-preserving interactions. We find that the magnetic field lowers the scalarization threshold in the electromagnetic and gravitational Chern--Simons channels. In the Gauss--Bonnet channel, by contrast, the effect divided into two branches: on the negative-$α$ branch in our convention, corresponding to the standard GB$^{+}$ branch, the magnitude of the critical coupling increases with the magnetic field, whereas on the positive-$α$ branch, corresponding to GB$^{-}$, the critical coupling decreases with the magnetic field but diverges in the limit of vanishing field. The magnetic field also modifies the late-time dynamics and gives rise to Melvin-like modes. When nonlinear couplings are included, the unbounded growth of the linearized theory is replaced by bounded oscillatory evolution. These results show that external magnetic fields affect scalarization induced by parity-violating and parity-preserving interactions in qualitatively different ways, and reveal a pronounced asymmetry between the two Gauss--Bonnet branches.

</details>


### [129] [Precision tests of analytical tail-term approximations for radiation reaction in Schwarzschild spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13684)
*Bakhtinur Juraev,Arman Tursunov,Zdeněk Stuchlík,Martin Kološ,Dmitri V. Gal'tsov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了史瓦西时空中带电粒子所受电磁自力的近似解析表达式的自洽性与精度，提出基于正交性条件的协变诊断工具，并应用于Smith-Will保守项和Gal'tsov耗散项两种常用近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于验证弯曲时空中辐射反作用计算所用近似尾项模型的内在自洽性。相对论粒子动力学要求四速度归一化保持恒定，这要求总自力必须与粒子四速度正交。

Method: 方法基于正交性条件（$u_μF^μ_{\text{tail}}=0$）引入协变诊断工具，定量评估近似尾项模型的自洽性。将该诊断应用于两种广泛使用的电磁尾力解析近似：Smith-Will保守分量和Gal'tsov耗散分量。

Result: 分析发现，单独的保守Smith-Will项会导致正交性条件的微小但可测量的偏离，而包含耗散Gal'tsov贡献后，这些偏离被抑制多个数量级。对于实际的辐射反作用参数，违反变得极其微小。

Conclusion: 提出的正交性诊断为验证弯曲时空中近似自力模型提供了简单且协变的工具，可能对今后研究致密天体附近的辐射反作用动力学有用。

Abstract: We investigate the consistency and precision of approximate analytical expressions for the electromagnetic self-force acting on a charged particle in Schwarzschild spacetime endowed with weak electromagnetic fields. A fundamental requirement of relativistic particle dynamics is the preservation of the four-velocity normalization ($u^μu_μ=-1$), which implies that the total self-force must remain orthogonal to the particle's four-velocity. We introduce a covariant diagnostic based on the orthogonality condition ($u_μF^μ_{\text{tail}}=0$), which provides a quantitative measure of the internal consistency of approximate tail-term models used in radiation-reaction calculations. We apply this diagnostic to two widely used analytical approximations for the electromagnetic tail force: the conservative component derived by Smith and Will and the dissipative component derived by Gal'tsov. The analysis is performed for several physical configurations, including pure Schwarzschild spacetime, a weakly electrically charged Schwarzschild black hole, and a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in a weak external magnetic field. We find that the conservative Smith--Will term alone leads to small but measurable deviations from the orthogonality condition, while inclusion of the dissipative Gal'tsov contribution suppresses these deviations by many orders of magnitude. For realistic radiation-reaction parameters, the violation becomes extremely small. The proposed orthogonality diagnostic offers a simple and covariant tool for validating approximate self-force models in curved spacetime and may be useful for future studies of radiation-reaction dynamics near compact objects.

### [130] [VIGILant: an automatic classification pipeline for glitches in the Virgo detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13687)
*Tiago Fernandes,Francesco Di Renzo,Antonio Onofre,Alejandro Torres-Forné,José A. Font*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器数据常受毛刺（glitch）污染，干扰天体物理信号的观测与分析。现有方法需要改进毛刺自动分类与监测能力，以提升数据处理效率。

Method: 研究评估两种机器学习方法：基于结构化Omicron参数的树模型（决策树、随机森林和XGBoost），以及基于频谱图（spectrogram）图像的卷积神经网络（ResNet）。使用Virgo O3b观测运行中的精选毛刺数据集进行训练与测试。

Result: ResNet34模型表现最优，在测试集上达到0.9772的F1分数和0.9833的准确率，每个毛刺推理时间为数十毫秒。树模型虽具更高可解释性和快速训练优势，但性能不及ResNet。该流水线已在Virgo O4c观测运行中部署，提供交互式仪表板监测毛刺群体和探测器行为。

Conclusion: VIGILant流水线成功实现了Virgo探测器毛刺的自动分类与可视化，ResNet34模型展现出卓越性能。部署后为合作组提供实时监测能力，并能识别低置信度预测以标记需进一步关注的毛刺。

Abstract: Glitches frequently contaminate data in gravitational-wave detectors, complicating the observation and analysis of astrophysical signals. This work introduces VIGILant, an automatic pipeline for classification and visualization of glitches in the Virgo detector. Using a curated dataset of Virgo O3b glitches, two machine learning approaches are evaluated: tree-based models (Decision Tree, Random Forest and XGBoost) using structured Omicron parameters, and Convolutional Neural Networks (ResNet) trained on spectrogram images. While tree-based models offer higher interpretability and fast training, the ResNet34 model achieved superior performance, reaching a F1 score of 0.9772 and accuracy of 0.9833 in the testing set, with inference times of tens of milliseconds per glitch. The pipeline has been deployed for daily operation at the Virgo site since observing run O4c, providing the Virgo collaboration with an interactive dashboard to monitor glitch populations and detector behavior. This allows to identify low-confidence predictions, highlighting glitches requiring further attention.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 结果表明，对于非对称反弹模型，类似于对称反弹模型，非均匀尘埃分布下壳交叉奇点（SCS）是不可避免的。然而，对于无反弹且具有无界聚合化函数的模型，在非均匀递减尘埃分布下不会形成SCS，这一情况类似于经典理论中通过适当选择初始数据可以避免SCS的情形。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了模型特性对壳交叉奇点形成的关键影响：具有有界聚合化函数的反弹模型中SCS不可避免，而具有无界聚合化函数的无反弹模型中SCS可避免。这一发现区分了不同量子引力启发的有效模型在奇点形成行为上的差异。

Abstract: We extend the investigation into the formation of shell-crossing singularites (SCS) in effective polymerized LTB models to the LQG-inspired asymmetric bounce model, as well as to effective LTB models based on the solutions of Bardeen and Hayward, in which no bounce occurs. While the asymmetric bouncing model belongs to the class of bounded polymerization functions, the latter models feature unbounded polymerization functions.
  Our results show that, similar to the symmetric bouncing model, for the asymmetric bouncing model SCS are unavoidable for inhomogeneous dust profiles. In contrast, for models without a bounce and with unbounded polymerization functions, no SCS form for inhomogeneous, decreasing dust profiles -- a situation that resembles classical theory, in which SCS can also be avoided by a suitable choice of initial data.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过求解测地线方程，识别了各种闭合轨道构型，并模拟了相应的引力波信号和电磁光变曲线。研究聚焦于轨道形态与暗物质晕参数的关系。

Result: 闭合轨道形态主要由方位角周期与径向周期的比值决定。暗物质晕参数（如核心尺度和密度参数）对轨道尺度产生显著放大效应，并进一步在引力波信号中诱导可辨别的相位滞后。某些轨道结构（包括叶片数量）虽难以仅通过引力波信号区分，但在光变曲线的特征峰中表现出可识别特征。

Abstract: Timelike orbits in curved spacetimes encode intrinsic information about the background geometry and serve as critical probes for investigating gravitational theories and source distributions. In this study, we investigate strictly closed timelike orbits within a Schwarzschild spacetime embedded in a Dehnen-type dark matter halo. By solving the geodesic equations, we identify various configurations of these closed orbits and simulate their corresponding gravitational waves and electromagnetic light curves. Our findings reveal that the morphology of closed orbits is primarily governed by the ratio of the azimuthal period to the radial period. Notably, dark matter halo parameters such as the core scale and density parameters exert a significant amplification effect on the orbital scale, which further induces a discernible phase lag in the gravitational wave signals. Furthermore, although certain orbital structures including the number of leaves remain challenging to distinguish via gravitational wave signals alone, they exhibit identifiable signatures in the characteristic peaks of light curves. These findings reveal the multi-messenger potential of closed orbits in bridging black hole environments and dark matter properties, providing theoretical guidance for future dark matter searches.

Abstract: We present Basilic, a dedicated pipeline for Bayesian model selection and parameter estimation of short-duration gravitational-wave burst signals observable with ground-based detectors. Built on top of the bilby framework, Basilic combines modularity, pre-implemented burst models, and HTCondor integration to enable rapid, user-friendly analyses with minimal technical overhead. This work outlines the design philosophy, operational flow, and a set of example use cases demonstrating its scientific potential. As a case study, we also undertake an in-depth exploration of the comparison between a binary black hole merger and a cosmic string signal, through a parameter space exploration injection campaign. In addition to the well-known high-mass binary black-hole signal morphology degeneracy with cosmic string-like signals, we find that high anti-aligned component spins, even at moderate mass, can result in a similar degeneracy. Motivated by the likely low-SNR expected regime of possible future detections, we propose a data-driven study of model degeneracy, to be employed in the event of an inconclusive Bayes factor.

### [134] [Robust parameter inference for Taiji via time-frequency contrastive learning and normalizing flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13867)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法结合了条件归一化流（conditional normalizing flows）、时频多模态融合编码器（time-frequency multimodal fusion encoder）和对比学习（contrastive learning）。为实现在受污染数据上的大规模训练，还引入了神经伪影生成器（neural glitch generator）以较低计算成本生成高保真合成瞬态信号。

Abstract: Transient noise artifacts, commonly referred to as glitches, pose a major challenge to parameter inference for space-based gravitational-wave (GW) observations. We develop a glitch-robust amortized inference framework for massive black hole binaries in the Taiji detector configuration by combining conditional normalizing flows, a time-frequency multimodal fusion encoder, and contrastive learning. To enable large-scale training on contaminated data, we further introduce a neural glitch generator that produces high-fidelity synthetic transients at substantially reduced computational cost. Systematic experiments show that, under glitch contamination, the proposed method yields more accurate and better-calibrated posteriors than a conventional Markov Chain Monte Carlo baseline. In ablation studies, the full time-frequency model with contrastive learning performs best overall and remains robust to variations in glitch duration and merger-relative timing. We further show that standard coverage diagnostics alone are insufficient to fully assess posterior fidelity. We therefore complement them with the continuous ranked probability score, which provides a stricter assessment of global distributional agreement in non-ideal GW data. Taken together, these results establish deep-learning-based amortized inference as a promising framework for fast and robust Bayesian parameter estimation in future space-based GW observations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation in the presence of a cosmological constant for general thermodynamically consistent equations of state, without imposing regularity at the center. Formulating the problem as an initial value system integrated from an outer boundary inwards, we obtain a general classification of solutions and show that singular configurations dominate the solution space. We demonstrate that all singular solutions share a universal geometric structure and give rise to spacetimes that are bounded-acceleration complete, indicating that the associated singularities are comparatively mild. Our results extend the classification previously obtained for Λ=0 and reveal qualitatively new features for $Λ\neq  0$. For $Λ> 0$, we find four distinct classes of solutions with cosmological horizons, distinguished by the behavior of their temperature gradients.

Method: 通过推导Killing张量和Killing-Yano张量来建立时空结构，计算回磁比（gyromagnetic ratio），并分析Hamilton-Jacobi方程的可分离性在f(R)引力中的表现。

Result: 研究发现回磁比保持g=2的普适值，与所有四维黑洞一致；揭示了隐藏对称性与Hamilton-Jacobi方程在f(R)引力中可分离性之间的内在联系。

Conclusion: 该工作推进了修正引力理论中黑洞的研究，为理论框架和观测宇宙学（如引力波分析）提供了重要启示，表明即使在f(R)修正引力下，黑洞的基本对称性特征仍然保持。

Abstract: We explore hidden symmetries in electrically charged, four-dimensional rotating Kerr-Newman black hole within $f(R)$ gravity. By deriving the Killing and Killing-Yano tensors, we establish their role in the spacetime structure. The gyromagnetic ratio is calculated and shown to retain its universal value of $g = 2$, consistent with all four-dimensional black holes. These findings show that the gyromagnetic ratio remains consistent in this modified gravity setting. Moreover, they highlight the connection between hidden symmetries and the ability to separate the Hamilton-Jacobi equation in $f(R)$ gravity. This work advances the study of black holes in modified gravity, offering implications for both theoretical frameworks and observational cosmology, such as gravitational wave analyses.

</details>


### [138] [Finding and characterising physical states of Euclidean Abelianized loop quantum gravity using neural quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14067)
*Hanno Sahlmann,Waleed Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究使用神经网络量子态和变分蒙特卡洛方法，在完全图K5上研究4维欧几里得圈量子引力的物理态，分析了不同哈密顿约束算符的变分解及其物理特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索4维欧几里得圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）在Smolin弱耦合极限下的物理态，特别是在完全图K5上分析哈密顿约束（Hamilton constraint）的不同排序形式及其解的性质。

Method: 采用变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）结合神经网络量子态（neural network quantum states）方法，研究Thiemann提出的哈密顿约束算符排序，包括$\hat{H}$、$\hat{H}^\dagger$及其和$\hat{H}+\hat{H}^\dagger$。

Result: 研究发现$\hat{H}$和$\hat{H}^\dagger$的变分优化选择了不同的解族：$\hat{H}$的解族在所有最小环上平坦且具有非零体积期望值，其边荷边际随截断增加而离域；$\hat{H}^\dagger$的解族可归一化，显示非平凡荷关联，位于体积核中且不平坦；$\hat{H}+\hat{H}^\dagger$更难求解，产生结合两者特征的准解。

Conclusion: 通过色度1点和2点函数、最小环和乐（holonomies）、几何面积和体积可观测量表征解，发现两个解族可分别解释为接近Ashtekar-Lewandowski真空和Dittrich-Geiller真空的态族，并建立了截断理论与连续理论解之间的联系。

Abstract: We study physical (near-kernel of constraints) states of 4-d Euclidean loop quantum gravity in Smolin's weak coupling limit on the complete graph $K_5$ using variational Monte Carlo with neural network quantum states. We investigate the Hamilton constraint $\hat{H}$ in the ordering proposed by Thiemann, as well as $\hat{H}^\dagger$ and $\hat{H}+\hat{H}^\dagger$. We find that the variational optimisation selects distinct solution families for $\hat{H}$ and $\hat{H}^\dagger$ across several considered cutoffs on the kinematical degrees of freedom. The solution family of $\hat{H}$ is flat on all minimal loops and has non-vanishing volume expectation values. Its edge-charge marginals delocalise with increasing cutoff, which indicates they are approximations to solutions that are non-normalisable in the kinematical inner product. The solution family for $\hat{H}^\dagger$ is normalisable, shows non-trivial charge correlations, lies in the kernel of volume and is not flat. $\hat{H}+\hat{H}^\dagger$ turns out to be much harder to solve and yields quasi-solutions combining features of both previous families. We characterise all solutions using chromaticity 1- and 2-point functions, minimal loop holonomies, geometric area and volume observables and show that the two families can be interpreted as, on the one hand, a family of states close to the Ashtekar-Lewandowski vacuum and the Dittrich-Geiller vacuum with some numerical noise on the other hand. We also present some results that link solutions of the truncated theory to solutions of the continuum theory.

</details>


### [139] [Time delay as a probe of multiple photon spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14132)
*Kajol Paithankar,Sanved Kolekar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究证明，瞬态源高阶图像的时间延迟观测能够有效打破不同球对称时空几何中黑洞阴影图像的简并性，特别适用于存在多个光子球（photon spheres）的时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞阴影图像主要由光子球性质决定，在不同球对称时空几何中可能出现简并（degeneracies）。研究旨在寻找能够打破这种简并性的观测探针，以更精确地探测致密天体结构和强场引力区域。

Method: 采用与模型无关的参数化静态球对称框架，捕捉双峰有效势（double-peaked effective potentials）的通用特征。研究光子测地线（photon geodesics），并用角偏转（angular deflection）、传播时间和图像阶数（order of the image）进行量化分析。

Result: 发现探测不稳定光子球之间区域的轨迹具有独特特征：非平凡的时间行为，包括最小传播时间、最小角偏转，以及具有特定到达序列的高阶图像特征三重态结构（characteristic triplet structure）。两个光子球之间势阱深度对观测时间延迟的影响，为探测时空不可及区域提供了直接手段。

Conclusion: 时域透镜观测（time-domain lensing observables）编码的信息超越了静态阴影图像，为探测致密天体结构和引力的强场区域（strong-field regime）提供了有前景的新途径。

Abstract: Black hole shadow images are primarily determined by the properties of photon spheres and can exhibit degeneracies across different spherically symmetric spacetime geometries. We show that time delay observables associated with higher-order images of transient sources provide a robust probe to break such degeneracies in spacetimes admitting multiple photon spheres. Adopting a model-independent, parametrized, static, spherically symmetric framework that captures the generic features of double-peaked effective potentials, we investigate photon geodesics and quantify them in terms of angular deflection, travel time, and the order of the image. We identify distinctive signatures of trajectories probing the region between the unstable photon spheres. In particular, we find that these trajectories are characterized by the nontrivial temporal behavior, including a minimum travel time, a minimum angular deflection, and a characteristic triplet structure of higher-order images with a specific arrival sequence. We further show that the influence of the depth of the potential well, between the two photon spheres, on the observed time delays provides a direct handle on otherwise inaccessible regions of the spacetime. Our results highlight that time-domain lensing observables encode information beyond static shadow images and offer a promising avenue for probing the structure of compact objects and the strong-field regime of gravity.

### [140] [Non-Hermitian Exceptional Dynamics in First-Order Heat Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13639)
*Pengfei Zhu*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个统一的非厄米（non-Hermitian）动力学框架，将热传导的弹道传播和扩散弛豫等不同机制统一描述，揭示了异常点（exceptional point）作为热动力学跨尺度组织的基本原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，热传导从弹道传播到扩散弛豫的不同机制由不同的理论框架描述，缺乏统一的理论体系。本文旨在建立一个统一的动力学框架来整合这些看似不同的热传输机制。

Method: 引入统一的一阶算符表述（unified first-order operator formulation），将温度和热通量作为耦合状态向量处理，实现了热传导的最小动力学闭合。该框架生成了本质非厄米的生成元（generator），其谱结构由异常点（exceptional point）主导。

Result: 异常点将过阻尼扩散与欠阻尼波状传播分离，并诱导非解析谱跃迁、非模态瞬态动力学以及传统模态分解的失效。傅里叶定律（Fourier law）作为双曲耗散系统的奇异极限出现，而Cattaneo方程则作为动理学理论的最小流体动力学闭合自然产生。

Conclusion: 该理论建立了热传导的统一非厄米动力学框架，揭示了异常点物理（exceptional-point physics）作为跨尺度热动力学的基本组织原理，并可推广到各向异性介质中实现热流的本征调控。

Abstract: Heat transport exhibits distinct regimes ranging from ballistic propagation to diffusive relaxation, traditionally described by disparate theoretical frameworks. Here, we introduce a unified first-order operator formulation in which temperature and heat flux are treated as a coupled state vector, yielding a minimal dynamical closure of heat transport. The resulting generator is intrinsically non-Hermitian and gives rise to a spectral structure governed by an exceptional point that separates overdamped diffusion from underdamped wave-like propagation. In this framework, Fourier law emerges as a singular limit of a hyperbolic dissipative system, while the Cattaneo equation arises naturally as the minimal hydrodynamic closure of kinetic theory. We show that the exceptional point induces nonanalytic spectral transitions, nonmodal transient dynamics, and a breakdown of conventional modal decomposition. The theory further generalizes to anisotropic media, where direction-dependent exceptional surfaces enable intrinsic steering of heat flow. Our results establish a unified non-Hermitian dynamical framework for heat transport and reveal exceptional-point physics as a fundamental organizing principle underlying thermal dynamics across scales.

### [141] [Mirror Surface Evaluation for the Einstein Telescope Using Virtual Mirror Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14008)
*A. Bianchi,A. C. Green,J. Degallaix,F. A. Feldmann,A. Soflau,A. Freise*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合泽尼克多项式分解（Zernike polynomial decomposition）和空间频率（功率谱密度，PSD）分析，并与数值光学模拟相结合，量化表面畸变对反射光场的影响。方法使用Advanced Virgo引力波探测器中安装的镜面计量数据进行验证。

Result: 开发了一个生成真实虚拟镜面图的框架，能够复现测量表面的低阶像差和高空间频率内容。这些虚拟图用于光学模拟中，系统性地探索和比较未来探测器（特别是爱因斯坦望远镜，Einstein Telescope）的候选表面质量规格。

Conclusion: 基于计量学的虚拟镜面提供了一个实用的设计工具，用于评估不同表面规格对光学性能的影响，并将未来要求与现有干涉仪的性能联系起来，为未来引力波探测器的镜面质量规格设计提供了有效方法。

Abstract: The performance of mirrors in optical interferometers is critically influenced by their surface quality. Accurate metrology enables mirror surfaces to be characterized through phase maps describing their three-dimensional structure after coating. In this work, we combine Zernike polynomial decomposition and spatial frequency (PSD) analysis with numerical optical simulations to quantify the impact of surface distortions on the reflected optical field. The method is validated using metrology data from mirrors currently installed in the Advanced Virgo gravitational-wave detector. Building on this validation, we introduce a framework for generating realistic virtual mirror maps that reproduce both low order aberrations and high spatial frequency content of measured surfaces. These virtual maps are used in optical simulations to systematically explore and compare candidate surface quality specifications for future detectors, with particular focus on the Einstein Telescope. Our results show that metrology-informed virtual mirrors provide a practical design tool to assess the impact of different surface specifications on optical performance, and to relate future requirements to the performance of existing interferometers.

Result: 通过调整参数，能够将能量流完全导向左侧、完全导向右侧，或进行分裂传输。该方案展示了能量流向的精确可控性。

### [143] [Tuning light-matter interaction of near-infrared nanoplasmonic scintillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13775)

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个量子光学框架，用于分析近红外闪烁体纳米晶体与纳米等离子体天线从弱耦合到强光-物质耦合的演化过程，发现基于石墨烯的导电纳米天线是实现可观测相干交换的最低阈值平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了量子光学框架，比较了宽谱和窄谱天线平台，包括单根和周期性金纳米棒，并以基于氧化铟锡和石墨烯的导电等离子体天线作为基准。代表性发射体包括宽谱PbS纳米晶体和窄谱立方Lu2O3:Er3+闪烁体。

Abstract: Nanoplasmonic modification of scintillation has so far been explored mainly in the weak-coupling regime, where changes in the local density of optical states enhance radiative recombination via Purcell-type rate engineering. By contrast, strong light-matter coupling generates hybrid states that modify emission dynamics beyond simple decay-rate acceleration, but its implications for scintillator nanocrystals (NCs) under ionizing radiation remain poorly understood. All of these effects are beneficial for near-infrared scintillators, which are typically slow and have low brightness. Here, we present a quantum-optical framework to investigate how near-infrared scintillator NCs coupled to nanoplasmonic antennas evolve from weak coupling toward strong light-matter coupling. We compare broad- and narrow-antenna platforms with single and periodic Au nanorods and benchmark them against conductive plasmonic antennas based on indium tin oxide and graphene. As representative emitters, we consider wide-band PbS NCs and narrow-band cubic Lu2O3:Er3+ scintillators. The calculations show that the onset of strong-coupling signatures is jointly governed by emitter dephasing and the antenna linewidth, with narrow-band emitters coupled to spectrally narrow antennas providing the most favorable conditions. Among the platforms considered, graphene gives the lowest threshold (g = 4 meV) for observable coherent exchange owing to its ultranarrow antenna linewidth (\k{appa} = 3.5 meV). These results identify near-infrared conductive nanoantennas, particularly graphene-based ones, as promising platforms for accessing hybrid scintillation regimes relevant to radiation detection.

### [144] [Non-Hermitian reshaping of high-order Landau modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13808)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 朗道能级（Landau levels）由一系列简并的朗道模式（Landau modes）组成，是进行大容量信息处理的有前景平台。然而，迄今为止，利用高阶朗道模式并控制其空间分布仍然难以实现。

Method: 提出在非厄米系统中同时构造磁场、电场和虚动量来重塑高阶朗道模式。通过构建非厄米电路平台，实验上实现了：通过非均匀耦合产生赝磁场（pseudomagnetic fields），通过梯度在位势产生赝电场（pseudoelectric fields），同时通过非互易耦合引入虚动量。

Abstract: When charged particles are subjected to strong magnetic fields, they form discrete energy levels known as Landau levels. The Landau levels consist of a series of degenerate states of Landau modes, making them a promising platform for large-capacity information processing. However, to date, exploiting the high-order Landau modes and control their spatial distributions has remained elusive. Here, we propose to construct magnetic fields, electric fields, and imaginary momentum simultaneously to reshape high-order Landau modes in non-Hermitian systems. By building a non-Hermitian electric circuit platform, we experimentally realize pseudomagnetic fields via inhomogeneous coupling and pseudoelectric fields via a gradient on-site potential, while simultaneously introducing an imaginary momentum via non-reciprocal coupling. We directly observe multi-frequency single-peak localization of high-order Landau modes. Our work provides a universal method for manipulating high-order Landau modes and exploring applications in nonHermitian systems, such as frequency multiplexing and wave packet reshaping.
