### [145] [Breakdown of spallation in multi-pulse ultrafast laser ablation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13858)
*David Redka,Julian Vollmann,Nicolas Thomae,Maximilian Spellauge,Heinz P. Huber*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究通过时间分辨泵浦-探测干涉测量技术，揭示了超短脉冲激光烧蚀金属时均匀剥离（homogeneous spallation）现象仅主导首次脉冲，而在多脉冲条件下会迅速转变为相爆炸（phase-explosion）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超短脉冲激光烧蚀金属的传统理解基于单脉冲理想平坦表面的均匀剥离机制，但实际应用中的多脉冲加工会持续改变表面状态。均匀剥离在多脉冲条件下是否持续存在一直是个未解问题。

Method: 采用时间分辨泵浦-探测干涉测量（time-resolved pump-probe interferometry）技术，对奥氏体不锈钢进行逐脉冲分析，结合傅里叶域相干性分析（Fourier-domain coherence analysis）排除粗糙度引起的去相干光学伪影。

Result: 首次脉冲主导均匀剥离，第二次脉冲贡献显著降低，第三次脉冲牛顿环消失且表面隆起坍塌，第四次脉冲光学瞬态完全饱和为相爆炸特征。四个独立观测结果一致显示三到四次脉冲后发生机制转变。

Conclusion: 剥离层形成（spallation-layer formation）是单脉冲现象而非多脉冲烧蚀机制，这对超短脉冲激光金属加工的理论理解和实际应用具有重要修正意义。

Abstract: Ultrashort-pulse laser ablation of metals near damage threshold is governed by homogeneous spallation, in which tensile unloading releases a nanometre-thin liquid film whose optical signatures are temporally evolving concentric Newton rings in pump--probe experiments. This well-established picture rests almost exclusively on single-pulse results obtained on ideally flat surfaces, yet application-oriented processing invariably operates in a multi-pulse regime in which each pulse irradiates a surface progressively modified by preceding pulses. Whether homogeneous spallation persists under these conditions has remained an open question. Here we resolve this question using time-resolved pump-probe interferometry applied pulse by pulse to austenitic stainless steel. We show that homogeneous spallation dominates the first pulse, while its contribution is strongly reduced for the second pulse. By the third pulse, Newton rings vanish and sustained surface bulging collapses, with the optical transients fully saturating into a phase-explosion-like signature by the fourth pulse. Fourier-domain coherence analysis rules out roughness-induced decoherence as an optical artefact. Four independent observables, spanning time-resolved and final-state measurements, converge on the same transition after three to four pulses. Spallation-layer formation, widely invoked to explain ultrashort-pulse ablation of metals, is thus a single-pulse phenomenon rather than a multi-pulse ablation mechanism.

</details>


### [146] [Time-resolved SNOM via phase-domain sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13892)
*Philipp Schwendke,Julia Stähler,Samuel Palato*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于相位域采样（phase-domain sampling）的新型时间分辨扫描近场光学显微镜（tr-SNOM）实验方法，成功在WS₂单层和多层区域测量并分离了近场信号，实现了样品动态介电函数（dynamic dielectric function）的提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间分辨扫描近场光学显微镜（tr-SNOM）在测量功能表面动态光学响应时面临实验挑战，包括脉冲光源的使用以及需要干涉信号调制来分离近场贡献。现有方法受到奈奎斯特极限（Nyquist limit）的限制。

Method: 研究采用200 kHz激光系统和伪外差调制（pseudo-heterodyne modulation），通过采样每个激光脉冲的调制相位、泵浦强度和SNOM信号来规避奈奎斯特极限。提出了一种独立于检测方案或近场增强物理假设的通用时间分辨SNOM信号模型。

Result: 在WS₂单层和多层区域成功测量并分离了tr-SNOM信号，通过信号-距离曲线、材料边界处的空间限制以及识别单个调制谐波（modulation harmonics）的信号贡献来确认信号定位。实现了动态贡献的分离和样品动态介电函数的提取。

Conclusion: 相位域采样方法展示了整合更多样化和专用光源的潜力，为光学超快近场测量开辟了新途径，扩展了时间分辨近场光学显微镜的应用范围。

Abstract: Time-resolved scanning near-field optical microscopy (tr-SNOM) enables the measurement of the dynamic optical response of functional surfaces beyond the diffraction limit. Experimental challenges are imposed both by the use of a pulsed light source, and by the need for interferometric signal modulation to isolate the near-field contribution. We present a novel experimental approach to retrieve the tr-SNOM signal using a 200 kHz laser system and pseudo-heterodyne modulation. We circumvent the Nyquist limit for spectral demodulation by sampling modulation phases, pump intensity and SNOM signal for every laser shot. A general time-resolved SNOM signal is derived, independent of detection scheme or physical assumptions about the near-field enhancement, and is successfully measured and isolated on WS$_2$ monolayer and multilayer regions. We confirm localization by signal-distance curves, spatial confinement at material boundaries, and by identifying signal contributions at individual modulation harmonics. Disentangling the dynamic contributions enables us to extract the dynamic dielectric function of the sample. Showing the capability of phase-domain sampling paves the way to integration of more diverse and specialized light sources, growing the potential of optical ultrafast near-field measurements.

</details>


### [147] [Twistoptics in Planar Heterostructures with an Arbitrary Number of Rotated 3D Thin Layers and 2D Conductive Sheets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13907)
*Christian Lanza,José Álvarez-Cuervo,Kirill V. Voronin,Gonzalo Álvarez-Pérez,Aitana Tarazaga Martín-Luengo,Javier Martín-Sánchez,Alexey Y. Nikitin,Pablo Alonso-González*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个分析模型，用于描述任意数量各向异性层和超薄导电层构成的平面堆叠结构中极化激元（polariton）的传播，为扭转光学（twistoptics）提供了通用理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转光学作为纳米光学的新分支，研究各向异性薄层相对旋转堆叠中的光传播，尤其在范德华（van der Waals）材料中，极化激元对层间扭转角高度敏感。然而，目前缺乏描述扭曲平面异质结构中极化激元传播的通用分析框架。

Method: 提出了一个分析模型，适用于包含任意数量有限厚度各向异性（双轴）层和无限薄各向异性导电层的平面堆叠结构。该形式体系包含高动量（high-momentum）和薄膜近似（thin-film approximations），并提供了开源数值脚本实现。

Result: 该模型能够预测关键的极化激元观测参数，包括波长、传播长度和电磁场分布。形式体系及其近似方法为扭转光学提供了通用理论基础。

Conclusion: 研究结果为扭转光学建立了通用理论框架，将促进跨电磁频谱的扭转工程极化激元现象的发现和实际应用。

Abstract: Twistoptics has recently emerged as a branch of nano-optics that explores light propagation in stacks of thin anisotropic layers rotated relative to one another. The concept is particularly relevant for polaritons -- hybrid light-matter quasiparticles -- in van der Waals (vdW) materials, where strong in-plane anisotropy and deep subwavelength confinement make the polaritonic dispersion highly sensitive to interlayer twist angles. This sensitivity enables exotic phenomena such as canalization, i.e., diffraction-free propagation, with potential applications ranging from thermal management to super-resolution imaging. Despite rapid progress, a general analytical framework to describe polariton propagation in twisted planar heterostructures has been missing. Here we present an analytical model for planar stacks comprising an arbitrary number of finite-thickness anisotropic (biaxial) layers and infinitesimally thin anisotropic conductive sheets. The formalism and its high-momentum and thin-film approximations predict key polaritonic observables, such as wavelength, propagation length, and electromagnetic field distributions. We also provide open-access numerical scripts implementing the model to support their practical use. Together, these results provide a general theoretical foundation for twistoptics and should facilitate the discovery and accelerate the implementation of twist-engineered polaritonic phenomena across the electromagnetic spectrum.

### [148] [Three-dimensional photon transport in spinodal photocatalytic aerogels: how bicontinuous morphology controls kinetic rate constants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13929)
*Renaud A. L. Vallée*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究量化了基于锐钛矿型二氧化钛（anatase TiO2）在二氧化硅气凝胶中的多孔整体光催化剂的光学模型误差，揭示了双连续旋节结构（bicontinuous spinodal architecture）中光子通道效应（photon channelling）导致固相接收光子比体积平均多50-70%，三维蒙特卡洛与扩散模型提取的动力学描述符差异达34%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔整体光催化剂在空气净化中具有应用前景，但其双连续旋节结构的光学特性复杂。当前方法将复杂的三维孔网络简化为均匀的一维平板模型，这种近似在旋节几何结构中的误差未知，需要准确的光学模型来提取本征动力学速率。

Method: 结合Cahn-Hilliard模拟生成的三维旋节掩模与GPU蒙特卡洛光子传输模拟，引入考虑催化位点分布的固相注量估算器，并与体积平均和扩散近似方法进行比较。

Result: 固相接收的光子比体积平均多50%（孔隙率0.70时）至70%（孔隙率0.90时），这种优先照明源于通过孔通道的准弹道路径（称为光子通道效应）。三维蒙特卡洛与扩散模型提取的动力学描述符差异达34%，其中约50%的差异源于双连续结构本身，无法通过有效介质理论修正。

Conclusion: 研究首次为这类光催化剂的动力学提取提供了定量校正，建立了连接合成粗化、孔径和光效率的设计规则，揭示了双连续结构对光传输的固有影响。

Abstract: Porous monolithic photocatalysts based on anatase TiO2 in silica aerogels are promising for air purification. Their bicontinuous spinodal architecture offers high surface area and strong light scattering. However, extracting intrinsic kinetic rates requires accurate optical models. Current methods replace the complex 3D pore network with a homogeneous 1D slab, an approximation whose error is unknown for spinodal geometries. We combine 3D spinodal masks from Cahn-Hilliard simulations with GPU Monte Carlo photon transport to quantify this. We introduce a solid-phase fluence estimator that accounts for catalytic site distribution, comparing it to volume averages and diffusion approximations. The solid phase receives 50% more photons than volume averages at porosity 0.70, rising to 70% at 0.90. This preferential illumination stems from quasi-ballistic paths through pore channels, termed photon channelling. The extracted kinetic descriptor differs by 34% between 3D Monte Carlo and diffusion models. Homogeneous controls show that roughly 50% of the total 73% discrepancy is intrinsic to the bicontinuous structure and cannot be fixed by effective medium theories. These results provide the first quantitative correction for kinetic extraction in such photocatalysts and establish design rules linking synthesis coarsening, pore size, and light efficiency.

### [149] [Controlling the Band Filling and the Band Width in Nickelate Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13875)

Abstract: The new family of superconducting nickelates centered around La$_{3}$Ni$_{2}$O$_{7}$ possesses attractive features, such as the high transition temperature and the presence of an antiferromagnetic ground state at ambient pressure, suggesting an unconventional pairing mechanism. In the nonsuperconducting state, the possibility of different density-wave orders with opposite pressure dependencies is discussed, whose relationships and microscopic origins are largely unknown. However, sample-quality issues, such as impurity-phase formation or oxygen vacancies, impede the progress in the field. Here, we employ high-pressure synthesis and hydrostatic high-pressure transport techniques to investigate bilayer nickelates with controlled band width and filling, and perform a systematic study on their impact on the superconductivity and other characteristic properties. While increasing the tilting of the NiO$_6$ octahedra shifts the superconducting phase to higher pressure, simultaneous hole doping reverts this trend. We also observe up to three distinct anomalies in the nonsuperconducting state which are possibly related to density-wave formation.

### [150] [Crystal structure effects on vortex dynamics in superconducting MgB$_2$ thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14022)
*Clemens Schmid,Anton Pokusinskyi,Markus Gruber,Corentin Pfaff,Theo Courtois,Alexander Kasatkin,Karine Dumesnil,Stephane Mangin,Thomas Hauet,Oleksandr Dobrovolskiy*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和模拟分析了两种MgB₂薄膜中微结构缺陷对涡旋动力学的影响，发现电阻转变由正常畴的形成和生长介导，而非磁通流不稳定性，揭示了薄膜微结构和薄膜-缓冲层界面对超导器件性能的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电流驱动的电阻转变（current-driven resistive transition）是超导单光子探测器、跃迁边缘传感器和磁通器件等超导器件的核心物理过程。研究旨在探究两种微结构缺陷（织构薄膜中的柱状生长和单晶薄膜中的缓冲层粗糙度）对MgB₂薄膜中涡旋动力学（vortex dynamics）的影响。

Method: 研究采用实验测量和理论模拟相结合的方法：在T≈0.25Tc温度下测量两种薄膜的电流-电压（I-V）曲线，并使用时变金兹堡-朗道（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau）模拟来复现实验I-V曲线的主要特征。

Result: 两种薄膜的I-V曲线均呈现多步特征，模拟表明电阻转变由正常畴（normal domains）的形成和生长介导，而非磁通流不稳定性（flux-flow instabilities）。具有缓冲层粗糙度的单晶薄膜在更高电流下发生超导性击穿，其钉扎激活能约为织构薄膜的两倍，且I-V曲线的多步特征更明显。

Conclusion: 薄膜微结构和薄膜-缓冲层界面（film-buffer interface）对电阻转变至关重要。缓冲层粗糙度引起的超导序参数横向变化导致更强的钉扎作用，结合较低的热边界电阻（thermal boundary resistance），共同解释了单晶薄膜的优异性能。这些发现为需要在高传输电流下控制耗散的超导器件提供了重要见解。

Abstract: The current-driven resistive transition is central to superconducting single-photon detectors, transition-edge sensors, and fluxonic devices. Depending on sample uniformity, dimensions, and heat removal, it can be driven by phase-slip events, flux-flow instabilities (FFI), or normal-domain formation. Here, we investigate the influence of two types of microstructural defects on vortex dynamics in MgB$_2$ films: columnar growth in textured films and buffer-layer roughness in single-crystal films. The current-voltage ($I$-$V$) curves measured at $T \approx 0.25 T_\mathrm{c}$ for both films exhibit multiple steps. Time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau simulations reproduce the major features of the experimental $I$-$V$ curves and suggest that the resistive transitions for both films are mediated by the formation and growth of normal domains rather than FFI. The single-crystal film with buffer-layer roughness exhibits superconductivity breakdown at higher currents and pinning activation energies approximately twice those of the textured film, along with more pronounced multi-step features in the $I$-$V$ curves. These features are attributed to the combination of stronger pinning induced by lateral variations of the superconducting order parameter along the MgO buffer layer and its lower thermal boundary resistance. Our results show that both the film microstructure and the film-buffer interface are critical for the resistive transition, offering insights for superconducting devices requiring controlled dissipation at high transport currents.

### [151] [Strong Correlation Drives Zero-Field Josephson Diode Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14045)
*Yiheng Sun,Zhenyu Zhang,James Jun He*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了强电子关联（strong electron correlation）作为实现零磁场约瑟夫森二极管效应（Josephson diode effect）的新机制，通过自发破缺时间反演和镜像对称性形成φ结（φ-junction），无需磁序即可产生非互易超导输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超流二极管效应（supercurrent diode effect）在有无磁场条件下均被观测到，但无需显式对称性破缺即可实现零磁场SDE的机制尚未充分探索。本研究旨在探究强电子关联如何作为实现零磁场非互易超导输运的独特机制。

Method: 研究采用具有强电子-电子相互作用的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）模型，包含哈伯德U项（Hubbard U term）和奇数个电子。通过分析强关联诱导的自发对称性破缺，探讨了φ结的形成机制及其对非互易输运的影响。

Result: 强关联诱导了时间反演和镜像对称性的自发破缺，形成具有±φ简并能量极小值的φ结，从而产生零磁场约瑟夫森二极管效应且无需磁序。自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）破坏SU(2)对称性但不决定二极管极性。微小塞曼场（Zeeman field）可增强强磁关联，实现可控JDE并在能级交叉转变（level-crossing transition）时达到峰值强度。

Conclusion: 强电子关联是产生非互易超导输运的独特机制，为理解超流二极管效应的起源提供了新视角，区别于磁手性机制（magneto-chiral mechanisms）。该发现拓宽了对SDE物理起源的认识，并展示了通过微小外场实现高效可控非互易输运的可能性。

Abstract: The supercurrent diode effect (SDE), characterized by unequal critical currents in opposite directions, has been observed with or without magnetic fields, yet mechanisms enabling zero-field SDE without explicit symmetry breaking remain underexplored. Here we investigate a Josephson junction with strong electron-electron interaction modeled by a Hubbard $U$ term and an odd number of electrons. We find that strong correlations induce spontaneous breaking of time-reversal and mirror symmetries, forming a $\varphi$-junction with degenerate energy minima at $\pm\varphi$, resulting in zero-field Josephson diode effect (JDE) without magnetic order. Spin-orbit coupling breaks SU(2) symmetry but does not determine diode polarity, contrasting with magneto-chiral mechanisms. We further show that applying a tiny Zeeman field enables controllable JDE with sizable efficiency due to the enhancement by the strong magnetic correlation, and the JDE strength peaks when the field induces a level-crossing transition. These findings establish strong electron correlation as a distinct mechanism for nonreciprocal superconducting transport, broadening the understanding of SDE origins.

### [152] [Beyond the dipole approximation: A compact operator form to describe magnetizable many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13647)
*Dirk Romeis*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于完整二体解（full 2-body solution）的解析近似方案，用于描述软磁粒子系统的多体全场相互作用。该方法通过改进的算子实现了类似偶极子（dipole-like）的简洁形式，既能准确描述粒子间相互作用，又保持了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前描述软磁粒子系统相互作用的方法存在局限性：数值全场方法（numerical full-field methods）计算量大，而简单偶极子模型（dipole models）在粒子靠近时会严重低估实际作用力。需要一种既能准确描述相互作用又计算高效的方法。

Method: 基于完整二体解（full 2-body solution），开发了一种多体全场相互作用的解析近似方案。该方法将概念表述为改进的算子，该算子与经典偶极子形式等价，但能更准确地描述粒子靠近时的相互作用。

Result: 完整的相互作用算子（full interaction operator）能够非常紧凑且高效地描述外加磁场中粒子的簇形成（cluster formation）和分散（dispersion）。该方法具有简单的"类似偶极子"形式，在软磁物体应用的许多领域中易于实现。

Conclusion: 提出的解析近似方案有效解决了软磁粒子系统相互作用建模中的准确性与计算效率矛盾，为相关领域提供了一种实用且易于实现的相互作用描述方法。

Abstract: To describe the interactions in magnetically soft particle systems either numerical full-field methods or dipole models are used. Whereas the former are computationally challenging, simple dipole interactions are largely underestimating the actual forces when particles get closer. Based on the full 2-body solution, an analytic approximation scheme for many-body full-field interactions is developed. The concept is formulated in terms of an improved operator that is equivalent to the classical dipole form. The full interaction operator allows to describe cluster formation and dispersion among particles in applied magnetic fields very compactly and highly efficient. In view of its simple 'dipole-like' form, the implementation is straightforward in many areas where magnetically soft objects are used.

</details>

In this study, we perform a comprehensive analysis to explore correlations between KM3-230213A and all viable GRBs. We explicitly account for the angular uncertainties intrinsic to both the neutrino event and the respective GRBs. Our analysis identifies a larger set of correlated GRBs. ### [154] [Deferred Cyclotomic Representation for Stable and Exact Evaluation of q-Hypergeometric Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13196)
*Seth K. Asante*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种用于有限q-超几何级数（finite q-hypergeometric series）和q形变振幅（q-deformed amplitudes）的循环多项式表示（cyclotomic representation），通过将求和项表示为不可约循环多项式（irreducible cyclotomic polynomials）上的稀疏指数基（sparse exponent basis），将量子阶乘的乘积和比值简化为整数向量运算，从而在求值前精确处理分子分母间的消去。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理q-超几何级数和q形变振幅时面临代数结构与求值过程混杂的问题，导致计算过程中出现中间表达式膨胀（intermediate expression swell）和消去引起的误差放大（cancellation-induced error amplification）。需要一种能够分离代数结构与求值过程，并在求值前精确处理消去的表示方法。

Method: 提出循环多项式表示方法，将每个求和项表示为不可约循环多项式上的稀疏指数基，使所有量子阶乘（quantum factorials）的乘积和比值简化为整数向量运算。该方法产生延迟循环多项式表示（deferred cyclotomic representation, DCR），这是一个与参数无关的组合对象，通过环同态（ring homomorphism）在任何目标域中实现求值。

Result: 对于量子重耦合系数（quantum recoupling coefficients），该框架在编译阶段实现线性内存缩放（linear memory scaling），消除精确算术中的中间表达式膨胀，并通过减少消去引起的误差放大显著扩展可靠双精度计算的范围。DCR为q形变振幅提供了统一视角，结构特性如单位根处的可容许性（admissibility at roots of unity）和经典极限都作为单一基础组合对象的内在属性出现。

Conclusion: 延迟循环多项式表示不仅提供了计算优势，还为q形变振幅提供了统一的理论视角。它将代数结构与求值过程分离，使结构特性成为基础组合对象的内在属性，从而在计算效率和理论理解上都取得了重要进展。

Abstract: We introduce a cyclotomic representation for finite $q$-hypergeometric series and $q$-deformed amplitudes that separates algebraic structure from evaluation. By expressing each summand in a sparse exponent basis over irreducible cyclotomic polynomials, all products and ratios of quantum factorials reduce to integer vector arithmetic. This ensures that cancellations between numerator and denominator are resolved exactly prior to any evaluation. This formulation yields the deferred cyclotomic representation (DCR), a parameter-independent combinatorial object of the series, from which evaluation in any target field is realized as a ring homomorphism.
  For quantum recoupling coefficients, we demonstrate that this framework achieves linear memory scaling in the compilation phase, eliminates intermediate expression swell in exact arithmetic, and substantially extends the range of reliable double-precision computation by reducing cancellation-induced error amplification. Beyond its computational advantages, the DCR provides a unified perspective on $q$-deformed amplitudes. Structural properties like admissibility at roots of unity, and the classical limit all emerge as intrinsic properties of a single underlying combinatorial object.

</details>


### [155] [Continuation of Hamiltonian dynamics from the plane to constant-curvature surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13250)
*Cristina Stoica*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了从欧几里得平面到二维常曲率曲面的余切丛（cotangent bundle）对称性形变，以及哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian system）中局部动力学特征的延续性。通过李代数（Lie algebra）的Inönü-Wigner收缩和黎曼指数坐标（Riemannian exponential coordinates），证明了从平直空间到弯曲空间中非退化相对平衡（relative equilibria）和相对周期轨道（relative periodic orbits）的持久性，并将框架应用于牛顿n体问题（Newtonian n-body problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索对称性从欧几里得平面到二维常曲率曲面的形变过程，以及哈密顿系统中局部动力学特征在空间几何变化下的延续性。这涉及到理解物理系统在不同几何背景下的行为一致性。

Method: 方法包括：1) 使用Inönü-Wigner收缩处理李代数从𝔰𝔬(3)或𝔰𝔬(2,1)到𝔰𝔢(2)的对称性；2) 采用以北极为中心的黎曼指数坐标，并结合关联动量映射（momentum map）和辛形式（symplectic form）的回拉；3) 在几何框架内使用局部切片构造（local slice construction）。

Result: 研究证明了从平直空间到弯曲空间中，一般余切丛哈密顿系统的非退化相对平衡和相对周期轨道的持久性。这一结果通过严格的几何构造得以验证，并建立了从欧几里得几何到球面和双曲几何的连续性框架。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了从平直空间到常曲率曲面的对称性形变理论框架，证明了局部动力学特征的延续性。所发展的几何方法可应用于牛顿n体问题，为研究不同几何背景下的物理系统提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate the deformation of symmetry on cotangent bundles from the Euclidean plane to two-dimensional constant-curvature surfaces and the continuation of local dynamics aspects in Hamiltonian systems. For a fixed curvature sign $σ\in\{+1,-1\}$, the curved problem is set up either on the sphere $(σ=+1)$ or on the hyperbolic plane $(σ=-1)$, both with radius $R=1/\varepsilon$, recovering flat space in the limit $\varepsilon\to 0$. The symmetry of these spaces is taken into account by using the Inönü--Wigner contraction of Lie algebras from $\mathfrak{so}(3)$ or $\mathfrak{so}(2,1)$ to $\mathfrak{se}(2)$. We use Riemannian exponential coordinates centred at the North pole together with the pull-back the associated momentum map and the symplectic form. Within this geometric setting we use a local slice construction and prove the persistence from flat to curved spaces of non-degenerate relative equilibria and relative periodic orbits of general cotangent bundle Hamiltonian systems. We apply the resulting framework to the Newtonian $n$-body problem.

### [160] [Measurement of jet quenching in O+O collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}=200$ GeV by the STAR experiment at RHIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13935)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究氧-氧（O+O）碰撞系统中夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）的形成，特别是在小碰撞系统中验证喷注淬火（jet quenching）现象的存在。

Method: 在相对论重离子对撞机（Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider, RHIC）的STAR实验中，测量高横动量（7 < p_T < 30 GeV/c）带电强子触发器与反冲带电强子（3 < p_T < 7 GeV/c）或带电粒子喷注（p_T,jet > 8 GeV/c）的关联，在事件活动性选择的O+O碰撞中进行分析。

Result: 高事件活动性碰撞中关联强子和喷注产额（归一化于触发器强子数）被抑制约20%，大半径带电粒子喷注（R=0.5）的p_T偏移为0.70±0.15(stat.)±0.10(syst.) GeV/c，表明未态相互作用导致的能量再分布。

Abstract: The STAR experiment at the Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider presents measurements of correlations between charged hadron triggers of high transverse momenta ($7 < p_{\rm T} < 30$ GeV/$c$) with recoiling charged hadrons ($3 < p_{\rm T} < 7$ GeV/$c$) or charged--particle jets ($p_{\rm T, jet} > 8$ GeV/$c$) in event--activity selected O+O collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm {NN}}}=200$ GeV. Yields of associated hadrons and jets, normalized by the number of trigger hadrons, are suppressed by approximately 20\% in high event activity relative to low event activity collisions, with an absence of suppression excluded with high significance. This suppression corresponds to a shift in p_{\rm T} of $0.70\pm0.15~(\rm stat.)~\pm0.10~(\rm syst.)$ GeV/$c$ for large--radius charged--particle jets ($R=0.5$), quantifying their energy redistribution due to final--state interactions. These measurements provide strong evidence for jet quenching in O+O collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}=200$ GeV, offering new insight into quark--gluon plasma formation in small collision systems.

### [161] [Covariant phase space approach to noncommutativity in tensile and tensionless open strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13163)
*Pratik K. Das,Sarthak Duary,Sourav Maji*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究使用协变相空间形式体系（covariant phase space formalism）分析了开弦中的非对易性（noncommutativity）。对于有张力开弦（tensile open strings）在恒定Kalb-Ramond背景场中，恢复了Seiberg-Witten非对易参数；对于内禀无张力弦（intrinsically tensionless strings），在背景场存在时相空间纯边界支撑，端点坐标获得非对易泊松代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用协变相空间形式体系（covariant phase space formalism）分析开弦动力学。对于有张力开弦在恒定Kalb-Ramond背景场中，分析（预）辛流（(pre)-symplectic current）的分解；对于无张力弦，分别研究无背景场和有恒定Kalb-Ramond场的情况，并考虑边界规范场耦合（boundary gauge-field coupling）的影响。

Result: 对于有张力开弦，发现（预）辛流分解为体动能项加精确边界项，恢复了Seiberg-Witten非对易参数。对于无张力弦，无背景场时约化相空间简并且无内禀泊松结构；有恒定Kalb-Ramond场时，辛流完全局域在边界，物理相空间纯边界支撑，端点坐标获得非对易泊松代数。边界规范场耦合导致边界辛形式由D膜上的有效Born-Infeld组合支配。

Conclusion: 研究结果为有张力和无张力开弦中的非对易性提供了统一描述，表明协变相空间形式体系能有效揭示不同弦理论模型中非对易结构的起源和特性，特别是在边界效应和背景场相互作用方面。

Abstract: We study noncommutativity in open strings using the covariant phase space formalism. For tensile open strings in a constant Kalb-Ramond background, we show that the (pre)-symplectic current splits into a bulk kinetic term plus an exact boundary term, recovering the Seiberg-Witten noncommutativity parameter. We then extend the analysis to intrinsically tensionless strings. In the absence of background fields, the reduced phase space is degenerate and carries no intrinsic Poisson structure. In the presence of a constant Kalb-Ramond field, the symplectic current localises entirely on the boundary, so that the physical phase space becomes purely boundary-supported and the endpoint coordinates acquire a noncommutative Poisson algebra. Including a boundary gauge-field coupling similarly leads to a boundary symplectic form governed by the effective Born-Infeld combination on the D-brane. Our results provide a unified description of noncommutativity in both tensile and tensionless open strings.

### [163] [Structural Obstruction to Replica Symmetry Breaking for Multi-Entropy in Random Tensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13261)
*Sriram Akella,Norihiro Iizuka*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机张量网络（RTN）畴壁自旋模型中多熵（multi-entropy）的复本对称破缺（RSB）行为。主要发现是：在该框架下，多熵对任意Rényi指数n和任意多部分数q均不展现RSB，这与纠缠负性（entanglement negativity）形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索随机张量网络（random-tensor-network, RTN）畴壁自旋模型中多熵（multi-entropy）的复本对称破缺（replica symmetry breaking, RSB）行为。特别关注多熵与纠缠负性（entanglement negativity）在RSB特性上的差异，以理解其背后的结构原因。

Method: 研究方法基于随机张量网络（RTN）畴壁自旋模型框架，分析多熵的边界排列（boundary permutations）在复本超立方体（replica hypercube）中的几何结构。通过考察Cayley图（Cayley graph）中共同测地中间排列（common geodesic intermediate permutation）的存在性来判定RSB。作为鲁棒性检验，还考虑了具有最小体规范约束的Z₂规范扩展玩具模型。

Result: 主要结果是：在RTN自旋模型框架内，多熵对任意Rényi指数n和任意多部分数q均不展现复本对称破缺（RSB）。这种无RSB特性的根源是结构性的：与多熵相关的边界排列沿着复本超立方体中相互不兼容的坐标方向组织，因此在S_N的Cayley图中不允许非平凡的共同测地中间排列τ。这与纠缠负性形成鲜明对比，后者确实允许这样的τ介导鞍点并在同一框架中展现RSB。在Z₂规范扩展模型中，数值证据表明多熵在n=2和n=3时仍无RSB迹象，而负性继续展现RSB。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在RTN自旋模型描述中，多熵不是"RSB友好"的：其边界数据在结构上与非平凡共同测地中间排列不兼容，这与负性不同。这一结构差异解释了两种纠缠度量在复本对称破缺行为上的根本区别。

Abstract: We study replica symmetry breaking (RSB) for multi-entropy in the random-tensor-network (RTN) domain-wall spin model. Our main result is that, within this framework, multi-entropy does not exhibit RSB for any Rényi index~$n$ and any multipartite number~$\mathtt{q}$. The origin of this no-RSB property is structural: the boundary permutations relevant to multi-entropy are organized along mutually incompatible coordinate directions of the replica hypercube, and therefore do not admit a nontrivial common geodesic intermediate permutation~$τ$ in the Cayley graph of~$S_N$. This is in sharp contrast to entanglement negativity, which does admit such a $τ$-mediated saddle and exhibits RSB in the same framework. As a robustness check, we also consider a toy $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge extension of the spin model with a minimal bulk gauge constraint. Numerical evidence in this gauged model indicates that multi-entropy continues to show no sign of RSB at $n=2$ and $n=3$, while negativity continues to exhibit RSB. Our results show that, within the RTN spin-model description, multi-entropy is not ``RSB-friendly'': its boundary data are structurally incompatible with a nontrivial common geodesic intermediate permutation, unlike negativity.

</details>


### [164] [Atiyah--Singer Index Theorem for Non-Hermitian Dirac Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13358)
*João Pedro Breveglieri da Silva,Dmitri Vassilevich*

TL;DR: 该论文证明了非厄米（non-hermitian）可对角化算子在满足椭圆性条件时，其手征指数（chiral index）同样具有拓扑保护性（topological protection）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了对于满足条件的非厄米算子，手征指数 $\mathrm{Ind}(Γ_*,H)$ 在参数和背景场的平滑变化下保持恒定，即具有拓扑保护性。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，非厄米可对角化算子的手征指数在适当条件下同样受到拓扑保护，这扩展了Atiyah-Singer定理的应用范围。

Abstract: If an operator $H$ anticommutes with a chirality operator $Γ_*$ such that $Γ_*^2=1$, the null space of $H$ can be decomposed in a direct sum of two spaces having positive and negative chiralities, respectively. When both spaces are finite dimensional, one can define an index, $\mathrm{Ind}(Γ_*,H)$, as the difference of dimensions of these two spaces. The key issue is whether $\mathrm{Ind}(Γ_*,H)$ is topologically protected, i.e., whether it remains constant under smooth variations of the parameters and background fields entering $H$. For Hermitian Dirac operators, topological protection of the index is guaranteed by the Atiyah--Singer theorem. In this paper, by using the heat kernel methods, we show that $\mathrm{Ind}(Γ_*,H)$ is topologically protected also for non-hermitian operators $H$ as long as they are diagonalizable and satisfy some ellipticity conditions.

The resulting formulae provide explicit expressions that can be computed on finite 2-surfaces, given a choice of null hypersurface. They yield a geometric definition of celestial symmetries and multipoles in generic spacetimes in terms of higher-valence solutions to the twistor equations. This, in turn, gives rise to natural flux-balance laws along the null hypersurface. We also present a first-principles phase-space derivation of these charges, starting from a twistor space action for self-dual gravity that can be identified with the standard gravitational asymptotic phase space at null infinity, performing a large gauge transformation analysis and using the Penrose transform to connect with the corresponding spacetime expressions. Motivation: 麦伦子在杨-米尔斯理论（Yang-Mills theory）中作为瞬子（instantons）的基本构成单元和禁闭（confinement）的定性描述具有特殊地位，但需要探究其在更广泛规范理论中的存在性和普适性。

Result: 证明了麦伦子配置在广泛的非阿贝尔规范理论中具有普适性，其引力背景下的奇异行为在广义框架中得到正则化，并成功构建了由真正非阿贝尔规范场支撑的正则黑洞解和欧几里得虫洞（Euclidean wormholes）。

Conclusion: 麦伦子的普适性意味着其固有物理效应（如自旋来自同位旋效应）同样具有普适性，其中规范群下的玻色激发可有效表现为费米自由度，这为理解非阿贝尔规范理论中的拓扑结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: Within the wide variety of topological solitons supported by Yang--Mills theory, merons occupy a particularly distinguished role. Despite their simplicity, they represent genuinely non-Abelian configurations that can be regarded as the fundamental building blocks of instantons, and they provide a qualitatively accurate picture of confinement. In this work, we show that such configurations are, in fact, supported by a broad class of non-Abelian gauge theories beyond Yang--Mills, provided that suitable physical conditions are satisfied, thereby rendering them universal. Taking into account their gravitational backreaction, we further demonstrate that both black holes and Euclidean wormholes sourced by merons admit natural extensions within this generalized framework, which regularizes the singular behavior they exhibit in constant--curvature backgrounds. As a byproduct, we construct a regular black hole solution supported by genuinely non-Abelian gauge fields, based on a non-Abelian generalization of the Ayón--Beato--García nonlinear electrodynamics. As a consequence of this universality, physical effects intrinsic to merons are likewise expected to be universal. A notable example is the spin from isospin effect, whereby bosonic excitations charged under the gauge group can effectively behave as fermionic degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [174] [Chiral Fermion Localization in Two-Kink Scalar Backgrounds: Tunable Brane Positioning and Universal Divergence at the Single-Kink Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14103)
*H. P. Pinheiro,C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过变形方法构建双扭结（two-kink）标量场背景，在有效实现(1+1)维Jackiw-Rebbi模型的系统中，揭示了手征费米子零模（chiral fermionic zero modes）局域化的两个独立标度律，为膜世界（brane-world）场景提供了可调谐的实现平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征费米子零模在具有畴壁结构（domain wall structure）的标量场背景中的局域化是膜世界（brane-world）场景的核心机制。研究旨在通过双扭结标量背景深入探索这一机制，为额外维（extra dimension）中的局域化物理提供可调谐平台。

Method: 采用变形方法（deformation method）应用于φ⁴模型，生成双扭结（two-kink）标量背景。该系统有效实现了(1+1)维Jackiw-Rebbi模型，并引入两个物理参数：控制标量背景左右对称性的不对称参数a₂，以及控制组成畴壁间距离的扭结间分离参数b。

Result: 建立了两个独立的标度律（scaling laws）：手征零模的集体质心位置对a₂呈线性响应，为连续调谐额外维中有效膜位置提供了机制；两个手征模的微分空间分离在双扭结背景坍缩为简单扭结时发散，遵循(b-1)的幂律，指数统计上一致于-1。

Conclusion: 这两个结果在物理上相互独立，均可在膜世界（brane-world）场景语言中获得精确解释。该机制在非对称双扭结静电势下的双层石墨烯（bilayer graphene）中具体实现，为探测额外维局域化物理提供了可调谐平台。

Abstract: The localization of chiral fermionic zero modes in scalar field backgrounds with domain wall structure is a central mechanism in brane-world scenarios. We investigate this mechanism in a system that provides an effective realization of the $(1+1)$-dimensional Jackiw--Rebbi model, using a two-kink scalar background generated by the deformation method applied to the $\varphi^4$ model. The two-kink profile introduces two physically distinct parameters: an asymmetry parameter $a_2$ controlling the left-right symmetry of the scalar background, and an inter-kink separation parameter $b$ controlling the distance between the constituent domain walls. We establish two independent scaling laws. First, the collective center-of-mass position of the chiral zero modes responds linearly to $a_2$, providing a mechanism for continuously tuning the effective brane position in the extra dimension. Second, the differential spatial separation between the two chiral modes diverges as the two-kink background collapses into a simple kink, following a power law in $(b-1)$ with exponent statistically consistent with $-1$. These two results are physically independent and each admits a precise interpretation in the language of brane-world scenarios. The mechanism is realized concretely in bilayer graphene under an asymmetric two-kink electrostatic potential, providing a tunable platform for probing extra-dimensional localization physics.

### [175] [Gravitational Sommerfeld Effects: Formalism, Renormalization, and Perturbation to $O(G^{10})$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14112)
*Chih-Hao Chang,Chia-Hsien Shen,Zihan Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文为双星旋近（binary inspirals）的有效场论（EFT）描述开发了系统框架，计算引力Sommerfeld因子（Sommerfeld factor），解析求解至$O(G^{10})$阶，并建立了辐射多极矩（radiative multipole moments）的新重整化群方程（renormalization group equation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双星旋近的有效场论描述中，辐射引力波形受到弯曲背景的普遍修正，即"尾效应（tail effects）"，这些效应重整化为所谓的"Sommerfeld因子"。本文旨在系统计算存在潮汐效应（tidal effects）时标量扰动的引力Sommerfeld因子。

Method: 采用世界线有效场论（worldline EFT），将图论重整化（diagrammatic resummation）重新表述为具有局域源（localized source）的$d$维波动方程解，推导出用EFT连接矩阵（connection matrix）表示的Sommerfeld因子闭式表达式。结合EFT重整化技术与黑洞微扰理论（black hole perturbation theory）中的Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi方法，解析求解Sommerfeld因子。

Result: 证明了当无潮汐耗散（tidal dissipation）时，Sommerfeld因子的相位与弹性康普顿散射（elastic Compton scattering）相移完全相同。对于$\ell = 0, 1, 2$分波（partial waves），将Sommerfeld因子的幅度和相位解析求解至$O(G^{10})$阶。建立了辐射多极矩的新重整化群方程，其精确解产生了超越普遍尾对数（universal tail logarithms）的波形改进重整化。

Conclusion: 这些高精度数据和精确关系为未来波形重整化模型（resummation models）的发展铺平了道路，提供了超越传统尾对数近似的改进波形描述。

Abstract: In the effective field theory (EFT) description of binary inspirals, the radiated gravitational waveform receives universal corrections from the curved background, the ``tail effects'', that resum into the so-called ``Sommerfeld factor''. We develop a systematic framework for computing this gravitational Sommerfeld factor for scalar perturbations with the presence of tidal effects on the system. Using the worldline EFT, we recast the diagrammatic resummation as a solution to the $d$-dimensional wave equation with a localized source, and derive a closed-form expression for the Sommerfeld factor in terms of the EFT connection matrix. We prove that the phase of the Sommerfeld factor is exactly the same as elastic Compton scattering phase shift when there is no tidal dissipation. By combining the renormalization techniques in EFT with the Mano--Suzuki--Takasugi method in black hole perturbation theory, we analytically solve the Sommerfeld factor for both the magnitude and phase to $O(G^{10})$ for the $\ell = 0, 1, 2$ partial waves. We further establish a new renormalization group equation for the radiative multipole moments, whose exact solution yields an improved resummation of the waveform beyond the universal tail logarithms. These high-precision data and exact relations pave the way for future resummation models of the waveform.

</details>

*Yu-Qi Lei,Xian-Hui Ge,Yu Tian,Shao-Feng Wu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用周期性驱动的全息系统（periodically driven holographic system）进行研究。通过分析离散时间晶体到时间半晶体的相变过程，提取临界标度行为（critical scaling behavior），并识别不同周期骨架（periodic skeleton）之间的动力学转变。

Result: 发现了一种离散时间半晶体相，该相在无序中保持持久时间序，连接了离散时间晶体和完全无序区域。该相呈现周期性骨架结构，离散次谐波峰（discrete subharmonic peaks）在连续谱上持续存在。研究揭示了从离散时间晶体到时间半晶体转变的临界标度行为，并识别了不同周期骨架之间的动力学转变，显示出离散尺度不变性（discrete scale invariance）。

Conclusion: 全息研究中的这些发现显著丰富了研究非平衡物相的平台，为理解量子系统中时间序的退化机制提供了新的视角和工具。

Abstract: Understanding how temporal order degrades in quantum systems remains a central issue in nonequilibrium physics. Here we study the melting of discrete time crystals in a periodically driven holographic system, where a distinct (discrete) time semicrystal phase emerges with persistent temporal order in disorder, bridging discrete time crystals and fully disordered regimes. This phase exhibits a periodic skeleton, with discrete subharmonic peaks persisting atop a continuous spectrum. We extract a critical scaling behavior across the discrete time crystal to time semicrystal transition. Furthermore, even dynamical transitions between distinct periodic skeletons can be clearly identified with systematic log-periodic corrections to power-law scaling, revealing discrete scale invariance. These findings in holography significantly enrich the platforms for studying nonequilibrium phases of matter.

### [177] [All-order structure of static gravitational interactions and the seventh post-Newtonian potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14134)

Method: 方法基于关联函数框架（correlation function framework），利用静态扇区的$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性推导出闭式公式。该方法为因子化定理（factorization theorem）提供了新的理论解释，并应用于计算第七阶后牛顿阶的引力相互作用。

Result: 成功推导出计算任意奇数阶静态后牛顿修正的闭式公式，并应用该公式计算了第七阶后牛顿阶（$\mathcal{O}(G_N^8 v^0)$）的引力相互作用，该计算涉及七圈图贡献。结果与使用因子化定理的图解法所得结果完全一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的闭式公式为计算任意奇数阶静态后牛顿修正提供了有效工具，并通过第七阶后牛顿阶的计算验证了其正确性。该工作不仅提供了计算方法，还为因子化定理提供了新的理论视角，对引力双体动力学的高阶修正研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present a closed formula for the computation of static post-Newtonian corrections to the two-body gravitational dynamics at any odd order, assuming the lower-order results are known. The formula is derived within a correlation function framework and exploits the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry of the static sector, leading to a novel theoretical interpretation of the factorization theorem. As an application, we compute the gravitational interaction of two compact coalescing objects at the seventh post-Newtonian order in the static limit, which receives contributions from seven-loop graphs at order $\mathcal{O}(G_N^8 v^0)$, and find complete agreement with the results obtained using the diagrammatic approach of the factorization theorem.

### [178] [Charged kaon electric polarizability from four-point functions in lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13269)
*Shayan Nadeem,Walter Wilcox,Frank X. Lee*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文采用格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）的四点函数方法计算了带电K介子的电极化率，通过分离弹性（Born）项和非弹性（non-Born）项，在淬火近似下获得了物理π质量外推后的数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在将四点函数框架应用于奇异介子（strange mesons），扩展先前四点函数极化率研究，并为未来更高统计量、包含动力学费米子（dynamical fermions）及更好控制系统不确定性的计算奠定基础。

Method: 采用格点QCD的四点函数方法（four-point function approach），这是低能康普顿散射（low-energy Compton scattering）的欧几里得类比。对于带电K介子，极化率被分离为弹性（Born）项（由K介子电磁形状因子提取的电荷半径确定）和非弹性（non-Born）项（通过四点关联函数的时间积分差获得）。研究使用500个Wilson淬火$24^3\times 48$格点配置，并计算连通图（connected diagrams）作为原理验证。

Result: 外推到物理π质量后，获得带电K介子电极化率$α_E = (0.988 \pm 0.534) \times 10^{-4}\;\mathrm{fm}^3$，以及K介子电荷半径平方$\langle r_E^2\rangle =0.3303\pm 0.0028\;\mathrm{fm}^2$。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了四点函数框架对奇异介子的适用性，扩展了先前的四点函数极化率研究，并为未来改进计算提供了基础。

Abstract: We present a lattice QCD calculation of the electric polarizability of the charged kaon using a four-point function approach, which is the Euclidean analog of low-energy Compton scattering. In the case of the charged kaon, the polarizability is separated into an elastic (Born) term, determined from the charge radius extracted via the kaon electromagnetic form factor, and an inelastic (non-Born) term obtained from the time-integrated difference of four-point correlation functions. Our study employs 500 configurations of Wilson quenched $24^3\times 48$ lattices, and we compute connected diagrams as a proof of principle. From this analysis, we obtain values for the charged kaon electric polarizability of $α_E = (0.988 \pm 0.534) \times 10^{-4}\;\mathrm{fm}^3$ as well as $\langle r_E^2\rangle =0.3303\pm 0.0028\;\mathrm{fm}^2$ for the squared kaon charge radius, after extrapolation to the physical pion mass. The study demonstrates the applicability of the four-point function framework to strange mesons, extends previous four-point function polarizability studies, and provides a foundation for future calculations with increased statistics, dynamical fermions, and improved control of systematic uncertainties.

</details>


### [179] [Flavoured Lattice Schwinger Model with Chiral Anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13146)
*Dogukan Bakircioglu*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种"风味晶格Schwinger模型"，通过在晶格上引入$\mathbb{Z}_2$风味自由度而非手征性交错来解决费米子倍增问题，该构造在有限晶格间距下保持精确的轴矢$U(1)$对称性，并提供了手征反常和费米子倍增的体-边界图像解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统晶格规范理论面临费米子倍增问题，标准解决方案通过交错手征性破坏了轴矢对称性。本文旨在开发一种新方法，在解决倍增问题的同时保持精确的轴矢$U(1)$对称性。

Method: 引入"风味晶格Schwinger模型"，这是一种$(1+1)$维$U(1)$晶格规范理论，通过交错$\mathbb{Z}_2$风味自由度而非手征性来解决费米子倍增问题。推导了连续极限，并展示了该模型可还原为两个由$α∈\{0,1\}$标记的无质量Schwinger模型副本。

Result: 风味构造允许定义良好、正则化的规范不变晶格轴矢荷$Q_G^A$，其手征反常方程为$\langle dQ_G^A/dt\rangle = -(2g/π)\int dx\,\langle E(x)\rangle$。该方程在连续极限下成立，是有限晶格间距下最小规范耦合的直接动力学结果。限制在$α=0$扇区可恢复标准单风味结果。

Conclusion: 风味晶格Schwinger模型提供了解决费米子倍增问题的新方法，同时保持精确的轴矢对称性。进一步研究表明，风味扇区的空间分离可实现为带状$(2+1)$维Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang拓扑绝缘体边界上的螺旋边缘态，这为手征反常和费米子倍增提供了体-边界图像解。

Abstract: We introduce the \emph{flavoured lattice Schwinger model}, a $(1{+}1)$-dimensional $U(1)$ lattice gauge theory in which the fermion doubling problem is resolved by staggering a $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ flavour degree of freedom rather than staggering chirality. Unlike all standard approaches, the flavoured construction preserves an exact axial $U(1)$ symmetry at finite lattice spacing. We derive the continuum limit, showing the model reduces to two copies of the massless Schwinger model labelled by $α\in\{0,1\}$. The central result is that the flavoured construction admits a well-defined, regularized, gauge-invariant lattice axial charge $Q_{G}^{A}$ with chiral anomaly equation $\langle dQ_{G}^{A}/dt\rangle = -(2g/π)\int dx\,\langle E(x)\rangle$ in the continuum limit, derived as a direct dynamical consequence of minimal gauge coupling at finite lattice spacing. Restricting to the $α=0$ sector recovers the standard single-flavour result. We further show that spatial separation of the flavour sectors can be realised as a helical edge states living on the boundaries of a ribbon shaped $(2{+}1)$-dimensional Bernevig--Hughes--Zhang topological insulator. This provides a bulk-boundary picture solution to both the chiral anomaly and fermion doubling.

### [180] [Multiradial Schramm-Loewner evolution: Infinite-time large deviations and transience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13387)

Result: 成功建立了多径向SLE(κ)在κ→0时的无限时间大偏差原理，良好速率函数为多径向Loewner能量。当κ≤8/3时，多径向SLE曲线在其公共终点处具有瞬态性，推广了[FL15, HL21]的结果。作为大偏差原理的推论，获得了有限能量径向多弦的布朗环测度相互作用项的显式渐近。

Abstract: In previous work [AHP24], we proved a finite-time large deviation principle in the Hausdorff metric for multiradial Schramm-Loewner evolution, SLE$(κ)$, as $κ\to 0$, with good rate function being the multiradial Loewner energy. Here, we extend this result to infinite time in the topology of common-capacity-parameterized curves, and streamline the proof. A main step is to derive detailed escape probability estimates for multiradial SLE$(κ)$ curves in the common parameterization, which extend the single-curve estimates achieved in [AP26]. As a by-product, we also get that multiradial SLE$(κ)$ curves, with $κ\leq 8/3$, are transient at their common terminal point, generalizing [FL15, HL21]. As a corollary to the LDP result, we obtain explicit asymptotics of the Brownian loop measure interaction term for finite-energy radial multichords, which is linear in the capacity-time and coincides with a certain choice of a cocycle for the Virasoro algebra.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究已通过间接方法构造了共形环系综（conformal loop ensemble, CLE）垫片的规范共形协变测度，但缺乏直接的实现方案。本文旨在证明该测度可以通过多种自然逼近方案获得，从而提供更直观的数学理解。

Method: 采用多种逼近方案来构造CLE垫片测度，包括欧几里得闵可夫斯基内容（Euclidean Minkowski content）、二进方格（dyadic squares）计数方法，以及基于规范测地线和电阻度量的覆盖球（covering balls）最小数量。这些方案均经过适当的重整化处理。

Result: 证明了对于κ∈(4,8)的CLE垫片，其规范共形协变测度确实可以通过上述逼近方案实现。特别地，将CLE₆垫片测度与Garban-Pete-Schramm构造的临界渗流簇顶点数标度极限测度等同起来。此外，证明了CLE垫片测度在所有阶矩上都是有限的。

Conclusion: 该研究为CLE垫片的规范测度提供了多种自然的实现方式，建立了不同数学构造之间的联系，并扩展了对该测度矩性质的理解，为后续研究提供了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: We show for $κ\in (4,8)$ that the canonical conformally covariant measure on the conformal loop ensemble (CLE$_κ$) gasket, previously constructed indirectly by the first co-author and Schoug, can be realized as the limit of several natural approximation schemes. These include the Euclidean Minkowski content and its box-count variants, the properly renormalized number of dyadic squares that intersect the gasket, and the properly renormalized minimal number of balls of radius $δ$ necessary to cover the gasket with respect to both its canonical geodesic and resistance metrics. This in particular allows us to identify the CLE$_6$ gasket measure with the conformally covariant measure constructed by Garban-Pete-Schramm as a scaling limit of the number of vertices in a macroscopic critical percolation cluster on the triangular lattice. Along the way, we show that the CLE gasket measure of every fixed compact set has finite moments of all orders; previously this was only known for first moments.

</details>


### [182] [The scaling limit of random walk and the intrinsic metric on planar critical percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14122)
*Irina Đanković,Maarten Markering,Jason Miller,Yizheng Yuan*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明二维三角晶格上临界点渗流（p=1/2）的开放顶点簇上简单随机游走，在标度极限下收敛于CLE₆布朗运动，且内禀度量收敛于CLE₆测地度量，从而推导出化学距离指数、电阻指数和谱维度的存在性，并验证爱因斯坦关系成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维三角晶格上临界点渗流（critical site percolation）的几何与概率特性，特别是开放顶点簇（clusters of open vertices）上随机游走的极限行为及其度量结构，旨在理解临界渗流簇的标度极限（scaling limit）与共形圈系综（conformal loop ensemble）的关联。

Method: 采用数学分析方法，研究简单随机游走（simple random walk）在临界渗流簇上的标度极限行为，证明其收敛于CLE₆布朗运动（CLE₆ Brownian motion），同时证明内禀度量（intrinsic metric）或化学距离（chemical distance）收敛于CLE₆测地度量（geodesic CLE₆ metric）。

Result: 证明了随机游走收敛于CLE₆布朗运动，内禀度量收敛于CLE₆测地度量，由此推导出化学距离指数（chemical distance exponent）、电阻指数（resistance exponent）和谱维度（spectral dimension）的存在性，并验证这些指数满足爱因斯坦关系（Einstein relations）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了临界渗流簇的随机游走与度量结构在标度极限下与CLE₆的精确对应关系，为理解临界渗流的普适性（universality）提供了严格的数学框架，并确定了关键临界指数的存在性及其相互关系。

Abstract: We consider critical site percolation ($p=p_c=1/2$) on the triangular lattice $\mathbf{T}$ in two dimensions. We show that the simple random walk on the clusters of open vertices converges in the scaling limit to a continuous diffusion which lives in the gasket of a conformal loop ensemble with parameter $κ= 6$ $\big(\mathrm{CLE}_6\big)$, the so-called $\mathrm{CLE}_6$ Brownian motion. We also show that the intrinsic (i.e., chemical distance) metric converges in the scaling limit to the geodesic $\mathrm{CLE}_6$ metric. As a consequence, we deduce the existence of the chemical distance exponent, the resistance exponent, and the spectral dimension of the critical percolation clusters. Moreover, we show that the exponents satisfy the Einstein relations.

</details>

### [183] [Membrane Tension Governs Particle Wrapping-Unwrapping Transitions and Stalling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13415)
*Yasin Ranjbar,Yujun Teng,Haleh Alimohammadi,Huajian Gao,Mattia Bacca*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了膜张力（membrane tension）在纳米颗粒包裹（particle wrapping）过程中的关键作用，提出了一个包含非接触区膜变形能量的统一物理框架，用于描述颗粒摄取（uptake）、停滞（stalling）和自发解包裹（spontaneous unwrapping）的竞争机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论描述通常关注颗粒-膜接触区内的粘附能（adhesion energy）和弯曲能（bending energy），而忽略了接触区外膜的变形能（deformation energy）。这种近似仅在膜张力（membrane tension）趋近于零时有效，而在有限张力下，非接触膜的变形成为主要的能量贡献，需要新的理论框架来准确描述。

Method: 通过分析总膜能量随包裹程度（wrapping degree）的变化，研究揭示了颗粒粘附、膜张力和颗粒尺寸之间的竞争关系。为了高效捕捉非接触变形，研究者推导了一个紧凑的解析近似（compact analytical approximation），该近似能准确再现膜形状的完整数值解（full numerical solution）。

Result: 研究发现张力依赖的非接触能量（tension-dependent non-contact energy）主导了颗粒包裹的进程。该框架揭示了一个停滞边界（stalling boundary），该边界分隔了颗粒摄取和排出的不同区域。由此产生的能量图谱（energetic map）为颗粒包裹和解包裹提供了统一的物理描述。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一的物理框架，强调了膜张力在决定纳米颗粒包裹命运（包括内吞作用（endocytosis）、膜融合（membrane fusion）和纳米颗粒设计）中的核心作用，超越了仅考虑接触区能量的传统模型。

Abstract: Membrane wrapping underlies nanoparticle uptake during endocytosis, whereas the reverse process of membrane unwrapping accompanies particle expulsion and membrane fusion events. Existing theoretical descriptions typically focus on adhesion and bending energies within the particle-membrane contact region and often neglect the deformation energy of the membrane outside the contact zone. This approximation is valid only in the limit of vanishing membrane tension, where the non-contact membrane assumes a catenoid-like configuration with negligible bending energy. However, at finite tension the deformation of the non-contact membrane becomes a dominant energetic contribution. Here we show that this tension-dependent non-contact energy governs the progression of particle wrapping. By analyzing the variation of the total membrane energy with wrapping degree, we uncover a competition between particle adhesion, membrane tension and particle size that determines whether wrapping proceeds, stalls, or reverses into spontaneous unwrapping. This framework reveals a stalling boundary separating regimes of particle uptake and expulsion. To capture the non-contact deformation efficiently, we derive a compact analytical approximation that accurately reproduces the full numerical solution of the membrane shape. The resulting energetic map provides a unified physical description of particle wrapping and unwrapping, with implications for endocytosis, membrane fusion, and nanoparticle design.

</details>

### [184] [Nonlinear scalings emerge in a linear regime: an observation in electrokinetic flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13615)
*Jin'an Pang,Guangyin Jing,Xiaoqiang Feng,Kaige Wang,Wei Zhao*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过双频激励方案在电动力学（electrokinetic）流动中发现了一种非线性系统的例外情况：即使在小扰动下，内在非线性仍主导着扰动行为，导致功率律谱的出现，这与完全发展的电动力学湍流理论预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，非线性系统中的小扰动通常被归因于可忽略的非线性，从而为线性近似提供依据。本研究旨在探索这一范式在电动力学（electrokinetic）流动中的例外情况，揭示内在非线性在小扰动条件下的作用。

Method: 采用新颖的双频激励方案，使用两个高频交流电场（> 10⁵ Hz），通过差频（Δf）高效激发比激励频率低四个数量级的流动扰动。该方法利用电场体力的非线性实现纯粹的非局部能量传递机制。

Result: 研究发现，这些名义上线性化的速度和电导率小扰动表现出功率律谱（power law spectra）。随着电瑞利数（electric Rayleigh number）增加，标度指数与Quad级联过程理论对完全发展的电动力学湍流的预测定量一致。

Conclusion: 该观察不仅暗示即使在低激励下也存在多重流动状态转变，而且表明内在非线性即使在线性区域也调节着扰动行为。这需要对电动力学和其他非线性系统中的线性近似进行根本性的重新审视。

Abstract: In nonlinear systems, small perturbations are conventionally attributed to negligible nonlinearity, justifying linear approximations. Here, we uncover a notable exception to this paradigm in an electrokinetic (EK) flow. Using a novel dual frequency excitation scheme with two high frequency AC electric fields ($> 10^{5}$ Hz), we efficiently excite flow perturbations at a difference frequency ($Δf$) four orders of magnitude lower. This approach reveals a strong nonlocal energy transfer mechanism mediated purely by the nonlinearity of the electric body force, enabling precise, clean flow control free from electrode polarization artifacts. Unexpectedly, these small, nominally linear velocity and electric conductivity fluctuations exhibit power law spectra. With increasing electric Rayleigh number, the scaling exponents agree quantitatively with predictions for fully developed EK turbulence by the Quad cascade process theory. This observation not only implies multiple flow state transitions even at low excitations, but also indicates that intrinsic nonlinearity regulates perturbations even in the linear regime, necessitating a fundamental re examination of linear approximations in electrohydrodynamics and other nonlinear systems.

</details>

### [185] [On the discrete Painlevé equivalence problem, non-conjugate translations and nodal curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13782)
*Anton Dzhamay,Galina Filipuk,Alexander Stokes*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了源自半经典正交多项式的非自治差分方程系统，通过递推系数和阶梯算子，识别其为离散Painlevé方程，并在Sakai分类方案中确定其类型。研究发现不同权重可能对应相同曲面类型但不等价，强调离散Painlevé等价问题的精细化需要考虑动力学生成群元素和参数约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在研究源自半经典正交多项式的非自治差分方程系统，这些系统通过递推系数和阶梯算子与广义Laguerre和Meixner权重相关。研究动机在于识别这些系统为离散Painlevé方程，并在Sakai分类方案中确定其类型。

Method: 研究方法基于半经典正交多项式的递推系数和阶梯算子，分析源自广义Laguerre和Meixner权重的非自治差分方程系统。通过Sakai分类方案，将这些系统识别为离散Painlevé方程，并确定其关联的有理曲面类型。

Result: 研究发现这些系统属于离散Painlevé方程，在Sakai分类中具有特定曲面类型，包括$D_5^{(1)}$类型。研究发现不同权重可能对应相同曲面类型但不等价，这种不等价性体现在动力学由$\widehat{W}(A_3^{(1)})$的非共轭元素生成，以及某些曲面具有节点曲线。对称性分析显示这些系统的对称群为$(W(A_1^{(1)})\times W(A_1^{(1)}))\rtimes \mathbb{Z}/2\mathbb{Z}$。

Conclusion: 研究结论强调，不同权重与Sakai分类之间的对应关系应当采用精细化的离散Painlevé等价问题框架，该框架不仅考虑曲面类型，还需考虑动力学生成群元素以及参数约束（如节点曲线对应的约束）。这些发现进一步支持了精细化分类方法的必要性。

Abstract: We consider several examples of nonautonomous systems of difference equations coming from semi-classical orthogonal polynomials via recurrence coefficients and ladder operators, with respect to various generalisations of Laguerre and Meixner weights. We identify these as discrete Painlevé equations and establish their types in the Sakai classification scheme in terms of the associated rational surfaces. In particular, we find examples which come from different weights and share a common surface type $D_5^{(1)}$ but are inequivalent in two ways. First, their dynamics are generated by non-conjugate elements of $\widehat{W}(A_3^{(1)})$. Second, some of the examples have associated surfaces being non-generic in the sense of having nodal curves. The symmetries of these examples form subgroups of the generic symmetry group, which we compute. In particular, we find $(W(A_1^{(1)})\times W(A_1^{(1)}))\rtimes \mathbb{Z}/2\mathbb{Z}$. These examples give further weight to the argument that any correspondence between different weights and the Sakai classification should make use of the refined version of the discrete Painlevé equivalence problem, which takes into account not just surface type, but also the group elements generating the dynamics as well as parameter constraints, e.g. those corresponding to nodal curves.

</details>
